/ /pra ptA kSha ra bha dra gha Ta nA ma bi dza hA ra tri sma/ // /thob yig bum pa bzang po zhes bya ba bzhugs so/ /(ka)dznye ya sa rba bi dya sa rba ta dznyA dzye ShTha dA
nta he ru ka sya wa stuH di gi dzI na gaM dza ga ta nA thaH swA mi ba ndhya na na mo gu rA be/ /shes bya kun rig thams cad mkhyen/ /dga' chen he ru ka yi dngos/ / phyogs
las rnam rgyal 'gro ba'i mgon/ /rje btsun bla ma la phyag 'tshal/ /bA gI sho mu da sa rba ba ndhu gaM / pu Nyauo tstshe dhwa dza k-I rti nA ya ka à½¿ shrI mAM ka lpa dha rA
gra ma ntra dhaM/ sa rba dznyA tsa ra NaM ku ro na maHnga~Xg gi dba~Xng phyug 'gro kuna~X dga~X' ba'i gnyen/ /bso~Xd nama~Xs mngon mtho graga~Xs pa~X'i rgyala~X mtsha~Xn
'dzin/ /dpa~Xl ldan skal ba bza~Xng po~X'i 'dren pa mchog / kun mkhyen sngags 'chang bla ma'i zhaba~Xs la~X 'duda~X/ // /rgya gar 'phags yul na legs sbyar smra ba rnams
kyi skad du/ praptA kSha ra bha dra gha Ta nA ma/ bod thugs rje tshad med pa'i zhing na 'dod rgyal du smra ba'i skad du/ thob yig bum pa bzang po zhes bya ba/ oM na mo manydzu
shrI ye/ chos sku 'gyur med 'khor 'das kun la khyab/ /zung 'jug longs sku nges pa lnga ldan sku/ /mchog dman kun la

snang mdzad sprul pa'i sku/ /de gsum dbyer med ngo bo nyid skur 'dud/ /lus rtsa gnas gyur bla ma sprul pa'i sku/ /rtsa yig gnas gyur bla ma longs spyod rdzogs/ /thig le gnas
gyur bla ma chos kyi sku/ /rlung khams gnas gyur bla ma ngo bo nyid/ /kun gzhi gnas gyur shin tu rnam dag sku/ /rigs kun khyab bdag drug pa rdo rje 'chang / /bka' drin
mnyam med rtsa ba'i bla ma dang / /brgyud par bcas pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ / gzhan gyi don du byang chub thugs bskyed nas/ /tshogs gnyis yongs rdzogs sgrib gnyis kun
spangs pa'i/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams dang dam pa'i chos/ /sras bcas dgra bcom rnams la rtag phyag 'tshal/ /dus gsum rgyal ba sras bcas thams cad kyi/ /gsung gi dbang
phyug 'jig rten kun gyi mig /dri med bstan dang 'gro ba ma lus gnyen/ /mkhas grub lo paN rnams la snying nas 'dud/ /rnam thar gsum gyi ngang las ma g.yos kyang / /'jigs
pa'i skur ston mtshon cha sna tshogs 'dzin/ /bstan la sdang ba'i dgra bgegs bdud kyi tshogs/ /mthar byed chos skyong srung ma rgyal gyur cig/ gangs can 'gro rnams sdug
bsngal gyis gtsais pa/ /sel phyir snying rjes smon pa mthu chen 'grub/ /sems dpa' che rnams rgyal blon tshul bzung ba'i/ /bstan pa'i sbyin bdag rim par byon la 'dud/ /rang
bzhin brjod pa'i rgyan gyis mchod par brjod nas/ thos par gyur pa'i dam pa'i chos rnams bla ma dam pa rnams la 'di skad du bdag cag skal ba dang ldan pa rnams kyis dus
tshes bzang po thams cad du nges par thos pa'i dus/ rgyud dgongs pa lung ston las/ skad cig thang cig yud tsam dang / /zla phyed zla ba lo yi dus// bskal pa grangs med gsum
po ni/ /skad cig gcig tu mnyam par byin gyis rlob par mdzad pa'i tshe na/ ston pa phun sum tshogs pa drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa drug pa rdo rje

'chang chen po rnams/ rdo rje gur las/ rdo rje sems dpa' ji lta bu'i/ /de ltar slob dpon gzugs 'dzin te/ /sems can rjes su bzung dmigs nas/ /phal pa'i gzugs su gnas pa'o/ /zhes
gang la gang 'dul gyis/ gnas phun sum tshogs pa chos tshigs kyis phye ba'i yul dbus bod gangs can gyi ljongs/ snod kyi 'jig rten gzhal yas khang gru bzhi sgo bzhi mtshan
nyid phun sum tshogs pa byang phyogs so bdun gyi rang bzhin 'ja' tshon gyi rnam pa rgyan stug po bkod pa dang mtshungs par byin gyis brlabs pa'i chos grwa chen po byang
chub kyi snying po rnams na 'di lta ste/ gtsang zhing yid du 'ong ba'i sa phyogs su/ /yangs pa'i stan ni rab tu bshams bting ste/ /bzang po'i tshon gyis legs par kha
bsgyur ba/ /chos gos gtsang ma de ni rab bgos nas/ /zhes dang / sham thabs che tshad legs par rab bgos nas/ /bcos bu'i ras rnams sna tshogs rab bting ba/ /rkang rten bcas
pa'i khri la rab 'dug cing / /rkang pa legs par bkrus te rab 'dzegs nas/ /gdong dang bzhin gyi mdog ni rab snum zhing / / chos kyi stan de la ni rab 'dug nas/ /sems can
lhags pa rtse gcig gyur rnams la// gtam yang rnam pa sna tshogs nye bar ston/ /dge slong dag dang dge slong ma dag dang / / dge bsnyen rnams dang dge bsnyen ma dag dang /
/rgyal po dag dang rgyal bu rnams la yang / /mkhas te rtag tu phrag dog med par ni/ /sna tshogs don ldan snyan pa'i gtam yang ston/ /dam chos pad dkar las gsungs so/ /gsung
gcig yan lag rgya mtsho'i sgra skad kyis/ /rgyal ba kun dbyangs yan lag rnam dag pa/ /'gro ba kun gyi bsam pa ji bzhin dbyangs/ /sangs rgyas gsung la rtag tu 'jug par
mdzad/ /'khor phun sum tshogs pa dag pa rab 'byams nam mkha'i mthil thams cad yongs su gang ba la 'di

lta ste/ brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams dang / rgyud sde bzhi'i yi dam zhi khro'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs rnams dang / rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rab byung gi cha lugs can rnams
dang / sa chen po la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang / 'phags pa nyan rang dgra bcom pa rnams dang / chos skyong srung ma'i tshogs dang bcas pa rnams rdul phran
re re'i steng na/ rdul snyed kyi grangs dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad na 'tsho zhing gzhes la chos kyang ston par mdzad pa rnams dang / 'dzin
ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po 'di yang nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam par byin gyis brlabs pa'i gzhi la/ rigs can gsum gyi rigs nges par sad pa'i skal ba can gdul bya rgya mtsho
bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ brjod du med pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa las bsgres pa'i grangs kyis mchod par mi nus pa rnams dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so/ /de'i tshe
'khor 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i tshogs rnams kyis khrus phyag gos gtsang ma gyon/ lus longs spyod maNDal dang bcas pa phal chen nas gsungs pa'i kun tu bzang po'i mchod sprin
lta bu phul/ snyim pa me tog gis gang ba snying gar sbyar nas/ rab tu dma' ba'i stan la 'dug /dga' dang ldan pa'i mig gis blta/ /tshig gi bdud rtsi 'thung ba bzhin/ /gus
pa bskyed de chos nyan no/ /skyes rabs las 'byung ngo / /phal chen las/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen la ni sman pa'i 'du shes dang / gdams ngag la ni sman gyi 'du shes dang / nan
tan la ni nad sel ba'i 'du shes kyis/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba lan gsum btab nas/ lud pa bsal ba'i sgra tsam yang med par nyan cing / legs par rab tu nyon la
yid la zungs shig ces pa'i don/ snod kha sbub dang / dri ma can dang / zhabs rdol gyi dpe gsum gyis dben par 'chad nyan la brtson pa de dag

dang don mthun par gyur pa'i skabs su bdag nyid kyang kha drag gi snyems pas slar yang stobs 'byor gyi rlabs che ru e 'gro'i re ba dang chung du song dogs pa'i rnam g.yeng
rlung dmar gyis ma khyer/ kha zhan bya ba thams cad gzhan dbang du gyur pa'i sdug bsngal drag po'i khur gyis ma non/ dal 'byor gyi chos bco brgyad dang ldan/ rang dbang can
du gyur/ sngon bsags kyi mthus dad pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bag yod pa dang / bshad na go ba'i shes rab dang ldan pas/ 'phags pa shA ri'i bu'i smon lam 'grub pa dang
chos mtshungs pa'i phyir dus phun sum tshogs pa 'dir/ chos phun sum tshogs pa thub gsung dri ma med pa theg pa gsum gyi dam pa'i chos thog mtha' bar gsum du dge ba nyan
te/ chos thos pa la phan yon bsam gyis mi khyab pa stai/ thos pas chos rnams shes par 'gyur/ /thos pas sdig las ldog par 'gyur/ /thos pas don med spong bar 'gyur/ /thos
pas mya ngan 'das pa thob/ /ces bya ba la sogs pa'i don snying la brnag pas thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son par 'dod nas/ ji ltar thos pa rnams rang gi dran pa gso
ba dang / tshong pa tshong khe mthong nas tshong las la 'jug pa ltar/ phyis nas kyang rang nyid spro ba 'phel zhing bskul ma 'byung ba'i phyir du yi ger dgod par bya'o/ /ji
ltar bri ba'i tshul yang / rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis dpal bzang po'i gsan yig bsregs bcad brdar ba gser gyi 'bum chung las/ phyi nas brgyud la nang brgyud
'ded pa dang / /nges brgyud dor nas ma nges rgyun 'dren dang / /ma thob pa'ang thob khul gleng ba dang / /the tshom can la thag chod byed pa ste/ /skyon bzhi'i brdzun gyi
dug chu 'dir spangs nas/ /phal cher gong ma'i gsan yig lugs bzhin bri| |zhes pa grub mtha' gzhan nas byung ba'i chos rgyun gyi brgyud pa dor nas rang ltos

kyi bla ma 'dren pa ni spre'u yos rkun 'dra ste brgyud pa thams cad 'chol du mi 'jug pa gces so/ /chos mi thob pa'i rgyu bzhi ni/ chos la dad pa med pa dang / bla ma'am dge
rgan ngan pas bkag pa dang / rang chen por rlom nas bla ma la mi gus pa dang / 'khor ba nas thar 'dod med pa'o/ /chos ma thob kyang chos thob khul gyis 'chad pa'i rkyen
ni stais dbang zhig gis khri mthon por thon pas dge ba'i bshes gnyen du khas blangs te/ ltogs lhas ngo tsha bsgribs pa'i dpes 'chad cing bstan pa'i chom rkun byas pas/ gzhan
la mi phan bzhin du rang dmyal bar skye ba'i rgyu yin zhes phyag chen thig le sogs rgyud mang por gsungs so/ /yang de nyid las/ 'ga' zhig gsung rgyun dag dang bstun la
rag /khungs ma chod rnams slar yang dpyad gzhir bzhag /nges pa 'ga' la dgag sgrub dang bcas te/ /yon tan bzhi ldan skyon med bdud rtsi'i sman/ /'di la dgos pa chen po mthong
nas bris/ /shes ldan gzur gnas don gnyer rnams kyis dpyod/ /da dung tshor dang ma tshor ma rig pas/ /ma rtogs log rtog the tshom dag gi skyon/ /lhag chad nor 'khrul
mchis na bzod par gsol/ /nges pa brnyed nas slar yang gso bar 'tshal/ /zhes so/ /mkhas pa 'jug sgo las/ bshad sla ba dang bzung bde zhing / /bstan bcos la yang rtsod bral
phyir/ /mkhas pa la la bstan bcos lus// bsdus te thog mar dgod par mdzad/ /cais gsungs pa ltar/ le'u dang po gleng gzhi'i skor/ gnyis pa nyan thos so thar sdom pa'i skor/
gsum pa byang sdom sems bskyed kyi skor/ bzhi pa sngags sdom 'bras bu'i theg pa gsang sngags gsar ma'i skor/ lnga pa gsang sngags rnying ma'i dbang rjes gnang man ngag
lung gi skor/ drug pa spyi bka' zur bka'i rjes gnang gi skor/ bdun pa man ngag khrid kyi skor/ brgyad pa bka'

'gyur lung gi skor/ dgu pa bstan 'gyur lung gi skor/ bcu pa bod gzhung dpal sa skya pa'i bka' 'bum skor/ bcu gcig pa bod gzhung sna tshogs kyi skor/ bcu gnyis pa rig gnas sna
tshogs kyi skor/ bcu gsum pa bsngo smon bkra shis kyi skor ro/ /thob yig bum pa bzang po las/ gleng gzhi mdor bstan gyi le'u ste dang po'o// //! de la gsan yig phal cher
bsgrigs rim mi 'dra yang 'gal ba ci la yod/ 'dir rim 'jug pa'i dbang du byas te/ rang lo bcu par yar 'brog theg mchog rgyud sde tshal gtsang dgon du bsgyur ba'i dus dpal
gser gling pa don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na byams pa shAkya rdo rje'i zhabs drung du lus bsgyur ming spos/ gtsug phud phul/ tshigs bar pa dge tshul du bsgrubs pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ thu mi'i gdung sde pa yar rgyab pa'i dbon bla chen kun dga' bsod nams la sgrub pa gnang 'dug pas 'og bsnyen rdzogs mkhan brgyud dang 'dra'o/ /rang lo nyer
gnyis par paN chen kun dga' bkra shis pa'i zhal snga nas mkhan slob dge 'dun dang bcas pa'i drung du bsnyen par rdzogs khul byas na'ang / khong rnam pa las chog la shin
tu ma 'dris pas/ las chog gi dpe klog pa'i tshe dbyangs yig sgrog pa ltar tshig lhad mang zhing / sdom pa skyes thob kyi brda 'phrod pa mi gsal bas the tshom gyi ngang du
dar cig bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i dbang du byas/ slar de dus sdom pa thob par song na 'bul chog dgos par bzhed pa'i lugs ltar/ bla ma rab 'byams pa rin chen rgya mtshos bslabs
nas sdom pa 'bul chog 'don pa bsgyur nas khyim pa'i tshul du ras dkar po gyon/ de ma thag mkhan po don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na 'dul ba 'dzin pa rnams kyi mchog
nyi ma gling pa tshul khrims bkra shis dpal bzang po dang / las kyi slob dpon paN chen

dpal ldan tshul khrims/ gsang ston pa nye ba 'khor lta bu skyed tshal slob dpon ngag dbang bstan 'dzin/ dus go brjod pa bla ma rab 'byams smra ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ kha skong
paN chen shAkya mchog ldan dang / de nyin snga dro'i bsgrub bya drug dang bcas pa rnams kyi zhabs drung du tshul gsum rim gyis nos pa'i dge slong gi dngos por gyur to/
/ brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang shA ri'i bu dang sgra gcan 'dzin/ /bram ze sgra gcan 'dzin dang klu sgrub zhabs/ /gu Na ma ti rin chen bshes gnyen dang / /dharma pA la gu Na
pa ti dang / / chos kyi phreng ba 'byung gnas sbas pa dpal/ kha che paN chen 'jam dbyangs sa paN zhabs/ /'od zer rgyal mtshan grags rgyal gzungs kyi dpal/ /dge bzang A
nanta pa chos rin zhabs/ /brtson 'grus rgya mtsho chos rgyal dpal 'byor dang / /nam mkha' rgyal mtshan nam mkha' rgya mtsho dang / /byams pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
dang / /tshul khrims bkra shis zhabs kyis bdag la bstsal/ /so thar sdom pa'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// //! theg pa chen po thams cad kyi rtsa bar gyur pa dbu ma lugs kyi sems
bskyed sa skya paNDi ta'i sems bskyed chen mo dang / rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal gyis mdzad pa nas byang sdom thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba shAkya thub pa/ rje
btsun 'jam dbyangs/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ zla ba grags pa/ rig pa'i khu byug /slob pa'i rdo rje/ dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ pu
Nya shrI| ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa/ 'dir dus zhabs pa chad
dam brtag /'jam dbyangs 'khon ston/ rin chen mgon po/ rgyal sras thogs med/ lo chen

byang chub rtse mo/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ chos rje kun dga' bzang po/ dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rdo rings kun spangs chen po/ tshar
chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /bla ma bsod nams chos 'phel/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ sa gnas kyi sems dpa' chen po mgon po bsod nams
mchog ldan/ rgyal ba'i myu gu tshul khrims bkra shis/ de gnyis kyis rigs kyi bu phrin las rnam rgyal la dgyes pa chen pos stsal lo/ /yang 'phags pa rin po che nas/ sgron
mon can pa rin chen dpal bzang / rin chen mgon po man 'dra/ yang na/ sa paN/ bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rje/ khro phu bsod nams seng ge /kun mkhyen bu ston/ 'jig rten dbang
phyug rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal man 'dra'o/ / thob yig bum pa bzang po las/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa thob pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// //! 'bras bu'i theg pa
gsang sngags gsar ma la rdo rje gur gyi dgongs pas rgyud sde bzhir gsungs pa las/ rnal 'byor bla med skor la/ thabs shes gnyis su med pa'i rgyud/ shes rab gtso bor ston
pa ma rgyud/ thabs gtso bor ston pa thabs rgyud gsum gyi dang po la/ rgya che ba gtso bor ston pa dpal dus kyi 'khor lo/ zab pa gtso bor ston pa dpal kye rdo rje gnyis kyi
dang po ni/ dang po'i sangs rgyas dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud las dkyil 'khor brgya dang brgyad/ rjes gnang bzhi/ man ngag / rig gnas sogs mtha' yas pa gsungs pa'i thams cad
kyi sngon du 'gro ba dbang thob pa ni/ ston pas shing pho rta'i lo sa ga nya ba'i tshes zag pa med pa'i bdud rtsi mchog mngon par mdzad nas lo bzhi drug 'das pa lcags
'brug nag pa'i zla bar/ gsan yig re khar chu lug lo zhes pa gsal/ shr-I dha nya ka Ta ka'i

mchod rten gyi nang gi steng du dpal ldan rgyu skar gyi dkyil 'khor spros te sprul pa'i chos rgyal zla ba bzang po sogs skal ldan gyi gdul bya rnams smin par mdzad/ de'i phyi
lo chos rgyal zla ba bzang pos dus 'khor rtsa ba'i rgyud bsdus/ gsan yig phal cher la chos rgyal bdun zhes pa gsal yang / ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i gsan yig spar
mar chos rgyal drug ces gsal 'dug pas/ de bzhin 'dir bkod pa yin/ byang phyogs shaM bha lar chos rgyal drug dang rigs ldan bcu dgu 'das shing / rgyal khams pa tA ra na
thas mdzad pa'i dus 'khor chos 'byung gi rigs ldan gong rim ltar na stobs chen yin 'dra/ gzhan la gong rim mi 'dra ba sna tshogs yod tshod 'dug /rigs ldan stobs po che chos
kyi khrir 'khod pa'i lo sum cu so bdun du sleb pa/ dur ma ti zhes pa lcags mo bya yi lo snron gyi zla ba'i mar ngo'i nyer bdun la gza' phur bu skar ma bra nye/ 'phrod
'phel/ sbyor ba las bzang / rten 'brel skye ba/ nyi ma 'brug /byed pa bag rnams 'dzom pa'i dus su/ badzra dha ra swa mi A nanta bi dza ya/ shrI bha dra chen pos phyag btab
pa'i sa'i cha/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan zhes yongs su grags pa'i dge 'dun 'du ba'i chos grwa chen po de nyid kyi nang du/ ston pas chu lug lo nag pa'i nya la dpal ldan 'bras
spungs kyi mchod rten chen po'i nang du/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud stong phrag bcu gnyis pa gsungs nas/ lo nyis stong dang lnga brgya dang nyer drug pa/ chos rgyal
bdun dang rigs ldan nyi shu pa stobs po che seng khri la bzhugs te chos bstan nas lo so gsum pa/ gro zhun gyi nya ba'i tshes lnga/ gza' lhag pa skar ma mig bzhi/ sbyor
ba zhi ba/ byed pa byis pa 'dzom pa'i dus su/ thugs gsung sku'i dkyil 'khor la lha drug brgya dang zhe gnyis/ yab yum gcig tu bgrangs na lha lnga brgya dang don gcig /'byung
po bye ba phrag phyed dang bzhi sogs bzhugs pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi yig cha 'ba' zhig nas dbang gong ma'i
'chad thabs chos rje phrin las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i spyod ldan spyan gzigs bcas kyi steng nas thun mong byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun/ gong ma kun rdzob drang

ba'i don gyi dbang bzhi/ gong ma'i yang gong ma don dam bdag po chen po'i dbang dang bcas pa dge slong gi rten la rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ! dang po'i sangs rgyas
dus kyi 'khor lo/ rgyal po zla ba bzang po/ sras lha dbang / gzi brjid can/ zla bas sbyin/ lha'i dbang phyug /sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang chos rgyal bdun rigs ldan nyer
lnga las dang po ldan/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ padma dkar po/ de nas rwa lugs la 'jam dbyangs sprul pa/ tsi lu A tsArya/ paNDi ta A tsArya/ dus zhabs pa che ba/ dus zhabs
pa chung ba/ manydzu kIrti/ sa manta shrI/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge /rwa 'bum seng / rje btsun rgwa lo/ bla ma shes rab seng ge /bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /bla
ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis ka la mkhan chen bu ston rin po che/ bla ma dharma shrI/ snar thang pa rgyal ba saM gha shrI bha dra/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ brag thog pa
chen po bsod nams bzang po| thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ bla chen ye shes dbang po/ rdo rje 'chang tshul
khrims bkra shis/ byams pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ sgyi chu ba blo gros dbang phyug /rnam grong chos dbang rgya mtsho/ 'bras gling pa bskal
bzang phrin las/ byams pa bstan 'dzin rab rgyas/ bka' drin mtshungs med byams pa bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag byams pa ngag dbang tshul khrims rgyal mtshan la'o/
/! yang / bu ston rin po che nas/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ lo tsA ba skyabs mchog dpal/ bla ma nam mkha' 'od zer/ lo chen shes rab rin chen/ rje btsun
rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal nas gong bzhin no//yang / chos rje bla mas brag kha ba grags pa seng ge la'ang dus 'khor dbang gsan no/ / ! yang / 'bro lugs shes
grags pa ni/ padma dkar po yan 'dra ba la/ rigs ldan

bzang po/ rnam rgyal/ bshes gnyen bzang po/ phyag dmar ba/ khyab 'jug sbas pa/ nyi ma grags/ shin tu bzang / rgya mtsho rnam rgyal/ rgyal ka /nyi ma/ sna tshogs gzugs/ zla
ba'i 'od/ mtha' yas/ sa skyong / dpal skyong / dus zhabs pa che ba/ dus zhabs pa chung ba/ kha che zla ba mgon po/ dgon pa dkon mchog srungs/ sgro ston gnam rtsegs/ grub
thob yu mo mi bskyod rdo rje/ sras dharme shwa ra/ grub thob nam mkha' 'od zer/ grub thob se mo che pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ chos rje 'jam gsar shes rab 'od/ bla ma chos
sku 'od zer/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ de gsum ga la 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ yang / 'jam gsar
nas/ rje btsun rgwa lo man gong bzhin byas kyang chog /yang / 'jam gsar shes rab 'od zer yan 'bro lugs gong bzhin las de la kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ byang sems
rgyal ba ye shes/ kun mkhyen shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rin po che gnyag phug pa bsod nams bzang po/ byams gling chos rje bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo
rje gdan pa man gong bzhin no/ /yang / dus zhabs pa don grub kun dga'/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po man 'dra/ ! paNDi ta nags rin lugs ni/ mchog gi dang po'i
sangs rgyas/ zla ba bzang po/ lha'i dbang phyug /gzi brjid can/ zla bas byin/ lha dbang / sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang ldan/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa padma dkar po/ bzang
po/ rnam rgyal/ dus zhabs pa che ba/ dus zhabs pa chung ba/ shAkya seng ge rgyal mtshan/ nyi ma'i 'od/ go taM dpal/ rin chen bkra shis/ rgyal ba'i rgyan/ blo ldan rje/
shAkya bsrung ba/ rje chen po legs skyes/ dpal sangs rgyas dbyangs/ paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa man gong

bzhin no/ ! /yang / shong lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ se mo che pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan nas/ bo dong rin chen rtse mo/ stag sde ba seng ge rgyal mtshan/ shong lo tsA ba rdo rje
rgyal mtshan/ shong lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston man gong ltar
ro/ /yang na bo dong rin chen rtse mo nas/ 'dzims pa rin chen shes rab/ shar pa dus 'khor ba ye shes rin chen/ kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya
mtsho/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa man gong ltar ro/ /yang na bu ston rin po che nas/ bla ma dharma shrI/ snar thang lo tsA ba saM gha shrI/ bzad pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/
brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ bla chen ye shes dbang po/ mtshungs med nyi
ma gling pa/ des bdag go /yang na shAkya kun dga' nas/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ nyi gling pa/ des bdag go /yang na bu ston nas/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po/
zha lu khang rnying slob dpon bsod nams 'phel/ stag tshang lo tsA ba man 'dra/ yang na kun mkhyen jo 'di'i rtsa ba'i brgyud pa 'og na yod nang pa nas/ gnyag phug pa bsod
nams bzang po| paN chen byams pa gling pa/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa man 'dra'o/ ! /yang / rwa lugs kyi brgyud pa gcig la/ dang po'i sangs rgyas/ zla ba bzang po/ chos
rgyal sum cu rtsa gnyis/ 'jam dbyangs sprul pa/ tsi lu paNDi ta/ pi to pa/ dus zhabs pa che chung / manydzu kIrti/ sa manta shrI/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge /rwa
'bum seng / rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ bla ma shes rab seng ge /skyi ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ jo nang kun mkhyen man gong ltar ro/ /yang na rgwa lo nas/ lo tsA ba mchog
ldan/ skyi ston man 'dra/ yang na

rje btsun rgwa lo nas/ bla ma tshul khrims dar/ dus 'khor ba ye shes rin chen/ kun spangs zhang / byang sems chen po/ skyi ston pa man 'dra'o/ ! /yang / rwa 'bro 'dres pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ 'jam gsar ba nas/ rong pa rgwa lo/ bla ma sher seng / dpal ldan seng ge man sngar bzhin no/ /yang na kun spangs zhang nas/ kun spangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/
skyi ston pa man 'dra/ ! yang / sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor lo/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje snying po/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/ tsi lu paNDi ta/ dus
zhabs pa che ba/ chung ba/ a nu pa ma rakShi/ sA dhu pu tra/ chos kyi 'byung gnas/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ bi khya ta de wa/ mahA paNDi ta shAkya shrI/ chos rje sa paNDi
ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ sgyus pa gzhon nu seng ge /dol po ye shes mgon/ kun spangs kun tu bzang po/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston
man 'dra/ ! yang / thar lo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam gsar ba yan gong ltar nas/ nyeg po chos ldan/ gong lung pa gzhon nu dpal/ thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen
bu ston man gong ltar ro/ ! /yang / 'bro lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dang po'i sangs rgyas/ chos sku rdo rje 'chang / longs sku dus kyi 'khor lo/ sprul sku shAkya thub pa/ chos
rgyal zla ba bzang po/ lha'i dbang po/ gzi brjid can/ zla bas byin/ lha'i dbang phyug /sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang ldan te chos rgyal bdun/ rigs ldan 'jam dpal grags
pa/ padma dkar po/ bzang po/ rnam rgyal/ bshes gnyen bzang po/ phyag na rin chen nam phyag dmar ba/ khyab 'jug sbas pa/ nyi ma grags pa/ shintu bzang po/ rgya mtsho rnam
rgyal/ rgyal dka'/ nyi ma/ sna tshogs gzugs/ zla ba'i 'od/ mtha' yas/ sa skyong / dpal skyong / grub chen dus 'khor zhabs pa che chung / rgyal sras nA landa pa/

kha che zla ba mgon po/ 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags/ grab sgom dkon mchog srung / rnal 'byor bzang po sgro ston gnam la brtsegs/ grub chen yu mo dad pa rgyal po/ sras chos
kyi dbang phyug /grub thob nam mkha' 'od/ sprul sku jo 'bum/ se mo che pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam gsar shes rab 'od zer/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ kun spangs thugs
rje brtson 'grus/ byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho/ jo nang kun mkhyen dol po shes rab rgyal mtshan dpal bzang nas gong bzhin no/ ! /gnyis
pa ni/ rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa nas gsungs pa/ mchog sgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor drug las/ man ngag lugs phyi'i rgyu dbang snying po kye rdo rje zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug
pa lha dgu'i rdul tshon dang / yang / ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen por/ mngon rtogs bla ma dam pa'i yan lag drug pa/ dkyil chog slob dpon rtse mo'i dbang chu chen mo/ ngag
'don brag thog pas mdzad pa rnams nas dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs lan gsum thob/ skabs 'dir dbang don ngo 'phrod pas smin byed kyi dbang zhes bya ba'am/ phyi'i rgyu dbang
zhes bya ba'i dbang du byas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sku lnga ye shes lnga ldan rdo rje 'chang / /rgyal yum ye shes mkha' 'gro bdag med ma/ /de yis byin brlabs rje btsun birWa
pa/ /yid bzhin nor bu gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de sras thu bo grub chen nag po pa/ /grag stong skye med Da ma ru 'dzin pa/ /gzung 'dzin gnyis med a ba dhU tI pa/ /grub
pa'i dbang phyug gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /ga ya dha ra mahA paNDi ta/ /'jig rten mig mkhan shAkya ye shes zhabs/ /phyi nang shes bya'i dkyil 'khor kun rig pa/ /mngon shes
rdzu 'phrul mnga' brnyes chos 'bar ba/ /thar pa'i sa mkhan bzhi la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'phags pa 'jam dpal kun dga' snying po'i zhabs/ /ye

shes sku can bsod nams rtse mo'i mtshan/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal/ /bstan pa'i bdag po gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan
zhabs/ /'gro mgon 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ / bshad sgrub bstan pa'i khur 'dzin kun dga' dpal/ /mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nyams rtogs
mthar son bsod nams brtan pa dang / /grub pa snying por mdzad pa'i bsod nams dpal/ /thub bstan nyin byed bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhabs/ /bstan pa'i 'byung gnas gsum la
phyag 'tshal lo/ /skad gnyis smra ba ma ti paNDi ta/ /manydzu shrI kun dga' bkra shis zhabs/ /rgyal ba gnyis pa bsod nams bzang po dpal/ /mtshungs med bla ma gsum la phyag
'tshal lo/ /rdo rje 'chang dbang kun dga' rnam rgyal zhabs/ /de yis byin brlabs rigs pa'i glog phreng 'phro/ /snyan brgyud rgya mtsho byang chub dbang gi rgyal/ /rgyal
tshab dam pa gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ / bstan pa'i sgron ma shAkya kun dga'i mtshan/ /rigs brgya'i khyab bdag ye shes dbang po mchog /dkon mchog gsum dngos tshul khrims bkra
shis zhabs/ /gtan gyi skyabs gnas gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bstan pa'i sgron me rin chen rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ /bka' drin mtshungs med phrin las rnam rgyal dpal/ /rdo rje
'chang dngos blo gros dbang phyug mtshan/ /rgyal tshab dam pa gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgyal ba sku dngos chos dbang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ /rigs brgya'i khyab bdag kun
dga' chos 'phel dang / /mkhas btsun bzang po yon tan lhun grub rjai/ /'gran bral bla ma gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bka' drin gsum ldan kun dga' brtson 'grus zhabs/ /bslab
gsum rnam dag kun dga' dbang rgyal dang / /snyigs dus rdo rje gdan gyi bstan pa 'dir/ /dbang lung man ngag spel mdzad dharma'i mtshan/ /bdag la snga phyir dgyes pa chen pos
stsal/ /yang na theg chen pa kun dga' bkra shis/ bzad pa rin rgyal/ brag

thog pa bsod nams bzang po man gong ltar ro/ /yang / thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' rnam rgyal la 'bri khung mkhan chen/ mkhas grub rigs pa'i glog phreng / chos rje lcang lo
can pa gsum gyis gsan/ de gsum ga la 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal lo/ /yang / 'jam 'di sgyi chu ba dang chu bo nyis bsres 'og na'o dbyangs chos dpal 'byor/ 'jam dbyangs
byang chub dbang rgyal lo/ /yang / nyan chen pa/ chos rje spang khang pa/ mkhan chen lha dbang pa/ bla ma dpal ldan bsod nams/ bzad pa rin rgyal lo// yang / 'phags
pa/ paNDi ta/ rdo rje shes rab/ bla ma 'phags pa rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen dpal bzang po/ chos rje bla ma'o/ /yang / brag phug pa/ chos rje ye shes dpal/ chos rje blo
gros bzang po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa'o/ /yang nyan chen pa/ chos rje bla ma'o/ /yang / chos rje bla ma/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos
dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa'o/ /yang / 'phags pa/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/ bla ma 'od ldan pa/ bla ma mnyam med pa/ bla ma sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma bsod nams don grub/ rdo
rje 'dzin pa dpal ldan blo gros/ brag thog pa'o/ /yang / chos rje bla ma/ mkhan chen dkon mchog bkra shis/ brag thog pa'o/ /yang / 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon dpal/
brag phug pa'o/ /yang / nyan chen pa/ kun spangs chos grags dpal/ sa bzang paN chen no/ /yang / theg chen nas brag thog pa la'ang 'dren rigs te| brag thog gsan yig las/
theg chen pa'i skabs su/ khrid yongs su rdzogs pa/ kye rdor yab yum gyi bka' byin brlabs/ lam zab bla ma dang / rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi byin brlabs/ zhes sogs/ lam 'bras
lam skor sogs/ lung gsan tshul dang bcas gsungs pas/ phyi dkyil/ lus dkyil dbang sogs kyang gsan par nges shing /

phyag len snyan brgyud la'ang yod do/ /yang na/ byams pa chos dpal 'byor/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ paN chen bde ba'i rdo rje/ bla ma lha dbang phrin las/ nyi gling
rje'o/ /yang na 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ paN chen bde ba'i rdo rje/ de gnyis kar bla ma byang chub dpal bzang / nyi gling rje'o/ /yang / paN chen bde ba'i
rdo rje dang / bla ma u rgyan rgyal po gnyis ka la bla ma lha dbang phrin las/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ yang na dpal shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug
rgyal mtshan/ rtsa ba'i bla ma'o/ /yang na bla chen ye shes dbang po/ grub chen kun dga' dpal bzang / nyi gling rje'o/ /yang na bla chen ye shes dbang po/ rtsa ba'i bla
ma dam pa byams pa shAkya rdo rje/ des bdag go /yang na dpal shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rtsa ba'i bla ma paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des
bdag la'o/ ! /yang na dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang chen po gzungs kyi dpal/ mnyam med bzang po rgyal mtshan/ sems dpa' chen po rgyal mtshan
dkon mchog /byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ byams pa dkon mchog dpal/ paN chen lha dbang blo gros/ rje mang thos rab gsal/ paN chen bzang po bkra shis/ de gnyis la byams
pa yon tan lhun grub/ mkhan chen byams pa bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na mkhan chen byams pa bzang po/ dga' ldan grub chen kun dga'
dpal bzang / nyi gling rje/ des bdag go ! /kye rdor rgyud lugs su grags pa gsum gyi dang po/ Dombhi he ru ka'i lugs dgyes pa rdo rje phyag bcu drug pa lha dgu'i rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor du/ mngon rtogs slob dpon rtse mo/ dkyil chog theg chen chos rje'i nas/ dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo

rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ Dombhi pa/ a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa| bsod snyoms pa rgyal ba dpal ye shes/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi
lo tsA/ mnga' ris gsal snying / sgyi chu ba dgra bla 'bar/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ 'jam dbyangs sa paNDi ta/ 'gro mgon chos
rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos sgo ba/ rje btsun brag thog pa/ thams cad mkhyen
pa rdo rje gdan pa/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ kun spangs rin chen dbang sgrol yar rgyab pa'i zhal ngo btsun mo/ bla chen ye shes
dbang po| g.yu lo bkod pa rgyal mtshan rdo rje/ rtsa ba'i bla ma paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gnyis pa dgyais pa rdo rje nag po lugs zhal brgyad phyag
bcu drug pa lha dgu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du rgya gzhung la thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung mchan bzhin/ 'jam dbyangs byang dbang gi ngag 'don/ dkyil chog rgya gzhung
la thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung mchan bzhin/ ngag 'don nyi gling rje'i nas/ dbang bzhi thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ nag po dam tshig rdo rje/ bram
ze nag po pa/ 'gos lo tsA ba/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ dkar
shAkya grags/ ban sde lung pa kun bzang dpal/ bla ma dharma ye shes/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen sher rdor/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod
nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ bla ma ur rgyan rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'dzin

pa'i dbang po paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag go ! /gsum pa ni/ dpal kye rdo rje slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rje'i lugs zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug pa lha dgu'i rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor du mngon rtogs theg chen chos rje/ dkyil chog slob dpon rtse mo'i steng nas dbang gsum pa man man ngag lugs nas kha bskang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / bi la sye badzra/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rje/ indra bhU ti/ lcam lakShi ma/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ ga ya dha
ra/ bla chen 'brog mi/ se ston kun rig /zhang chos 'bar/ sa chen kun snying / rta rtags so ba rin chen don grub/ de'i dbon bla ma chos shes/ chu bo ri la kha'i bla ma rgyal
grags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ bla ma kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos sgo ba/ brag thog pa chen po/ thams cad mkhyen pa
rdo rje gdan pa/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma mkhyen rab rnam rgyal/ bla chen ye shes dbang po/ bla ma shAkya bsam 'grub/ yi
ge bzhi ldan paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag go /mchog dbang gsum rgya gzhung na med sngar snga mo nas dpyad gzhi yod gsung ngo / ! /de nas lam 'bras bu dang bcas
pa'i khrid kyi skabs/ rgyud gsum gyis bkri ba rdzogs pa dang / lam dbang zhes pa bla ma'i lus kyi dkyil 'khor du thog ma'i dbang thob pa la lus dkyil gyi rgyu dbang / slar
thob pa la lam dbang zhes/ rdo rje 'chang nyi gling rje'i dgongs pa ltar ro/ /bla ma dam pa'i bskur chog dang / theg chen chos rgyal gyi lam bsdus rgyun khyer ma gnyis
kyi steng nas dbang bzhi rgyas pa dang / de ma thag tu maNDal gsol gdab rtogs brjod so sor sbyar ba'i dbang 'bring po dang / de ma thag tu maNDal gsol gdab rtogs brjod

sbyar ba'i dbang bzhi chu rgyun gcig ma dang bcas pa thob cing / 'bring bsdus gnyis nges par thob dgos tshul bskur lugs bcas phra mo glegs bam du dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas
bshad pa ltar lan bdun thob pa'i brgyud 'bring bsdus gnyis kyi brgyud pa 'og tu gsal yod pa ni/ rgyal ba khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / dpal ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro bdag med
ma/ mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug mgon po shrI bi rU pa/ shar phyogs nag po pa/ Da ma ru pa/ a ba dhU tI pa/ paN chen ga ya dha ra/ sgra bsgyur 'brog mi lo tsA/ se ston kun
rig /zhang dgon pa ba/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan/ gnas lnga rig pa'i sa skya paN chen/ 'gro
mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ yang sa skya paN chen/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ nyan chen bsod nams 'phan yul nyan po dgon brtan
pa/ na bza' brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de la sa bzang ma ti paN chen dang / sa skya bu ston dbang phyug dar/ de gnyis
ka la theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ brag thog pa chen po bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa chen po kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po/ mkhas grub rigs pa'i glog phreng
/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ bla ma dam pa ye shes dbang po/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des phrin las rnam rgyal la'o/
/yang na/ theg chen pa/ mkhan chen dpal 'byor ba/ brag thog pa chen po'o/ ! /gzhan yang brgyud lugs rnam grangs kyis dbye na/ chos rje sa paNDi ta/ grub thob yon tan dpal/
la ru bsod nams seng ge /kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa/ mkhas grub 'phags pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal

po'o/ /yang / nyan chen las/ gangs pa'o/ /yang / brag phug pa las/ brag phug pa dkon rgyal/ sa skya bu ston/ theg chen pa'o/ /yang / gangs pa las/ ma ti paN chen/ theg chen
pa'o/ /yang / tshogs sgom pa/ chag rin po che sher 'bum/ mkhan chen rdo rje tshul khrims pa/ dkon rgyal lo/ /yang / la ru ba/ rdo rje tshul khrims/ yang / tshogs sgom/ gnyag
/bar pa/ rdor tshul lo/ /yang / grub thob pa/ rwa gnyis pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ zhang dkon mchog dpal lo/ /yang / nyan chen pa/ 'jam skya/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge
/bla ma dam pa'o/ /yang / zhang dkon dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ dpal ldan seng ge'o/ /yang / 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal gyis/ 'jam dbyangs chos dpal 'byor la'ang
/ dbang khrid byin brlabs gzhung bshad lung sogs kyang gsan pas/ brgyud pa'i rim pa 'og tu 'chad la/ ! gzhan yang / theg chen chos kyi rgyal po'i lugs 'di la lam 'bras
zhwa ma lugs kyi rgyun kyang 'dus gsung bas/ de'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma se ston/ zhwa ma rgyal mo lcam/ myang sgom pa/ de la mkhan po smon mkhar ba dang / kha reg gi myos
chos kyi gzi brjid gnyis/ de gnyis ka la ko brag pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de la kham chen byang chub dpal/ de la 'dzin pa rgyal mtshan dpal/ de la gangs khrod pa'o/ !

bla ma sa skya pa chen po nas gong bzhin no/ /gzhan yang rje btsun sku mched/ chos rje khu dbon sogs nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po nyid dang bcas pa

bzhin no/ /'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la gsan pa'i brgyud pa yang phyi'i rgyu dbang bzhin no/ /'jam dbyangs byang dbang la khrid dang lam dbang bla bir thun mong

dbang rgyal/ paN chen bde ba'i rdo rje/ bla ma lha

dbang phrin las/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go ! /dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi phyi'i rgyu dbang dang / phyi'i lam dbang zhus nas/ khrid dang byin
brlabs thob pa'i skor la/ khrid yig sbas don gsal ba'i steng nas phyag len bzhin 'dzin chos blo nas thon nges kyi khrid dang dus mnyam du rdo rje tshig rkang 'dzin chos
khrid dang rdzogs mnyam/ rdor sems bsgom bzlas gong du yig brgya'i bzlas lung khyon bsdoms lan bzhi thob/yan lag lnga sbyong ston pa'i nub mo tsam rdo rje tshig rkang dang
/ 'khor 'das dbyer med 'dzin chos stong / 'khor 'das dbyer med rdzogs pa dang 'phrul 'khor rtsa tshig stong / 'di sbas don bskyed rim sems 'dzin tsam la rdzogs dgos/ rdo
rje tshig rkang me dmar skya tsam la rdzogs pa dgos/ 'khor 'das dbyer med rtsa ba 'dzin chos lta khrid kyi gong du rdzogs pa/ bum dbang gi lam gyi sngon du lus dkyil gyi
dbang dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i bskur chog dang / theg chen pa'i lam bsdus gnyis kyi steng nas dbang bzhi rgyas pa de nas zhus khyon bsdoms lan bdun thob/ aShta'i bzlas
lung phag mo'i khongs sa paN yig cha khyon bsdoms lan bzhi thob/ 'phrul 'khor rtsa tshig 'dzin chos rlung sbyor gong du rdzogs ma thag phrin las so gnyis bshad pa dang
lag len mtshungs pa zhus/ shes rab ye shes kyi lam man la lung mdzad pas/ de ltar lan gsum tsam dang / khrid rdzogs 'phral ras 'bud dang / lam zab bla ma'i byin brlabs thun
mong tshar lnga thob/ bir bsrung byin brlabs thun mong can gnyis rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal gsung bzhin snyigs dus rdo rje gdan gyi bstan pa'i mdzes rgyan du byon
pa rdo rje 'chang phun tshogs chos 'phel des byams pa ngag dbang tshul khrims rgyal mtshan la'o tshar lnga thob/ go cha lnga srung / lam zab bla ma lus dkyil ma'i byin
brlabs tshar gsum thob/ bir bsrung sa paN lugs la mu srad pas dag pa sbyar ba'i byin brlabs lan gnyis thob/ dbang bzhi ngo sprod/ phyag rgya chen po yi ge med pa/ zur

du gsungs pa'i yi ge bzhi po rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gsum khug (zha)pa lan gnyis thob/ aShtA'i byad (zha)bzlog /go cha lnga bsrung / rten
'brel (zha)lnga srung / man ngag bshad mdzod kyi brda chig brgyud gsung ngag nas gnang zhing de'i lung slar mi gnang ba dgos pa can dang / sgrub pa'i lung sbyin te de dag
gi byin brlabs dang / rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi dgongs pa gang zag rab tha'i nyams len mngon rtogs skad cig mas bskyed pa 'dzin chos rnams nyams len snyan brgyud bzhi ldan
dmar khrid du thob pa dang / gzhung rdo rje tshig rkang gi bshad pa man ngag bshad mdzod kyi steng nas 'dzin chos su thob pa dang de'i sa gzhung sprod pa mkhyen rtse
tshe dbang kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa rnams so/ /de dag gi khrid tshul gyi rnam grangs nyi gling rje'i gsung ni/ ji lta gnad drug rab 'bring bcu gcig la/ /rim bzhin klu 8'byung

drug lag 152pa tshes/ /rab 'bring me 63ro bcu gcig bgrod pa 42chu/ /lam zab rig byed 4'bring po rgyal 24ba dang / /bsdus pa bse 1ru 'khor 'das gzugs 51dbang po/ /ngo sprod

brgya/ /rlung sbyor yi ge 'khor bzhi dbang phyug don/ /mngon rtogs don bsdus yi ge nyer gsum mo/ /zhes so/ /de dag kyang gsal na/ kun gzhi'i yig chung / gdan gyi yig chung
/ lus dkyil yi ge /'chi ltas brtag pa 'chi blu dang bcas pa/ snang ba bsgyur ba'i 'da' kha ma/ gsang dbang gi thig le'i rnal 'byor/ shes rab ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i

gsum bkri ba/ gnad drug gis bkri ba/ gnad bcu gcig gis bkri ba/ lam 'jug ldog /phyag rgya 'jug ldog /shes pas phan 'dogs pa'i man ngag bdun/ lam bsre ba 'gros bzhi dang

gnyis/ bha ga'i yi ge bcu bzhi'i dpe chung / bla ma'i rnal 'byor dbu dbyung ma/ lung mtha' dag dang mdor bsdus te sbyar ba/ lung 'di nyid dang mdor bsdus te sbyar ba/ bla
ma bod dang rgya gar ba'i lo rgyus gnyis rnams thob bo// de dag kyang gzur gnas don gnyer rnams kyi don du cung zad dpyad na/ rje bla mas bdag sogs la bka' lung gnang

rigs kyi dbye bas lam gyi khrid/ / brjed pa dran pa gso phyir bri bar bya/ /zhes bris pa gcig yod la/ de rnam dag yin no| |tshigs bcad de med pa'i bsdus pa shog cig ma

na'o/ /'dir legs par dpyad na lung sbyor rnams kyi kha yig dang mjug dbyung nor ba'i glegs bam mang du 'dug par rtog dpyod zhib par 'tshal lags/ de yang lung sbyor gang gi

ma/ nyams chen ma/ gsang bdun ma/ kye rdor lus dkyil dbang chog 'di la yab kyi byin brlabs zer ram brtag go rnams sa chen gyi'o/ /rtse mo'i lung sbyor glegs bam khrod

pa lung sbyin/ aShta'i gzhi bshad/ phyag chen dbye ba/ rten 'brel lam rdzogs/ khrid kyi lung sbyor/ rlung ltas brtag pa/ 'khor bzhi'i rgya/ sa paN zin bris/ bla ma'i rnal
'byor ling chu rtse khab ma/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor gu shri jo 'bum rnams thob/ gces bsdus dang / phra bsgrub slar

e gcig brtag go /'phags pa rin po che'i lam 'bras phyag mchod/ dbang gsum pa'i lam rgyas bsdus/ lus dkyil gsal 'debs/ lam dus kyi dbang rgyas pa/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin
sreg /tshogs sbyor mngon rtogs rnams so/ /'dir sa chen gyi gags sel gsum sogs 'ga' shas ma gtogs/ gzhan rnams sa skya bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag dang bstun nas gnang byung
bas/ slar yang bka' 'bum dang bstun dgos yod do/ ! /nyi gling rjes 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la gsan pa ni/ bsag sbyang gnyis/ yig brgya'i bzlas lung / aShta'i
bzlas lung / lam zab bla ma lus dkyil yod med gnyis ka /bir bsrung thun mong ba/ brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa'i lung sbyin rnams kyi byin brlabs/ lung gi skor la/ khrid kyi
dkar chag /sgrub pa lung sbyin/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ lam 'bras phyag mchod/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg / 'phags pa'i rdo rje tshig rkang / rnam 'grel rnams kyi lung
gi brgyud pa ni/ dpal shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /nyi gling rjes/ bla ma lha dbang phrin
las la gsan pa ni/ sbas don gsal ba'i steng nas khrid phyag len bzhin tshang ma/ rdo rje tshig rkang / 'khor 'das dbyer med/ phrin las so gnyis gzhung lag len sogs tshang
ma/ kye rdo rje zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang / rje btsun bdag med ma'i lus dkyil dbang / yig brgya'i bzlas lung / aShta'i bzlas lung / brda chig brgyud/ lam zab
bla ma'i byin brlabs/ bir bsrung byin brlabs/ yang / lam zab lus dkyil ma'i byin brlabs/ bir bsrung dag pa dang sbyar ba rgyas pa gcig gi byin brlabs/ de rnams kyi nyams
len dang bcas pa/ man ngag bshad mdzod steng nas gzhung bshad tshang ma dang bcas pa thob bo//

de nas lung gi rim pa thob pa la/ lam skor nang ma la/ rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang lung dang / de'i bsdus don shog logs tsam gcig kyang zhus/ lam 'bras glegs bam gud du gsungs
pa rnams dang bcas yongs rdzogs thob cing / de yang zhib tu bshad na/ sdom tshig gi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ dkar
chag rnam 'grel gsal byed nyer gsum dang / /'phros don bcu bdun 'bring dang bsdus pa dang / /gzhung shing bzhi dang rtogs pa bskyed pa lnga/ /dpe chung lnga dang bla ma'i
rnal 'byor dang / /lung sbyor gsum dang brgyud pa'i lo rgyus gnyis/ /yi ge phra mo lnga bcu rtsa gnyis te/ /bco lnga lhag pa'i brgya phrag gcig bltas nas/ /rnam par phye
bas man ngag shes par 'gyur/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa de don rgyas par bshad pa la/ yig cha lhag chad spang ba'i phyir dkar chag bstan pa dang / des bstan pa'i yig cha'i rnam
grangs bshad pa gnyis/ dang po ni glegs bam dkar chag ste/ rje pa'i'o/ /gnyis pa la| rtsa ba'i gzhung gi rnam 'grel ngos bzung ba dang / de'i don gsal bar byed pa'i yig
cha'i grangs bstan pa'o/ /dang po ni rnam 'grel gnyag ma ste sa chen gyi'o/ /gnyis pa la/ rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum bstan pa dang / zab 'bring tha gsum bstan pa dang / de
dag gi rgyab rten bstan pa/ yi ge zhal 'phangs bstan pa ste bzhi las/ dang po la rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum bstan pa dngos dang / de gsum ga'i thun mong gi chos bstan pa gnyis
las/ dang po la rgyas pa 'bring po bsdus pa bstan pa ste gsum/ dang po la/ gnyag ma nyid kyi steng du 'chad pa gtso che ba gsal byed nyer gsum bshad pa dang / gud du
gsungs pa dang bcas pa'i 'phros don bcu bdun bshad pa gnyis/ dang po la/ 'khor 'das thun mong gsal byed bcu bdun bshad/ 'khor lo 'cham pa gsal byed

gnyis bshad/ 'khor lo bskor ba gsal byed gsum bshad/ thun mong du gsal byed gcig bshad pa ste bzhi las/ dang po la/ rgyud gsum gsal byed/ tshad ma gsal byed/ gdams ngag gsal
byed/ rten 'brel gsal byed/ bar chad bsrung ba gsal byed de lnga/ dang po ni/ kun gzhi'i yig chung / gdan gyi yig chung / lus dkyil yi ge / 'chi ltas brtag pa 'chi blu
dang bcas pa/ snang ba bsgyur ba'i 'da' kha ma/ gsang dbang gi thig le'i rnal 'byor/ shes rab ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid/ dbang bzhi pa'i phyag rgya chen po nas
'pho ba/ zhar byung bar do'i yig chung / lam dbang rgyas pa ste bcu'o/ /gnyis pa ni/ tshad ma bzhi'i yi ge /gsum pa ni/ gdams ngag drug gi yi ge |bzhi pa ni/ rten 'brel
lnga'i yi ge /lnga pa la/ grib sel sbyin sreg /grib ma khrus dang tsha tshas sel ba/ 'dzag pa drug sel ba/ yig brgya 'don thabs te bzhi'o/ / gnyis pa 'khor lo 'cham pa la/
rlung sbyor bdun gyi yi ge dang / bha ga'i yi ge bcu bzhi gsal na gnyis so/ /gsum pa 'khor lo bskor ba la/ 'khor bzhi'i rgya/ dbang phyug gi don brgyad/ sa bcu gsum pa'i
phyed kyi mngon rtogs te gsum mo/ /bzhi pa thun mong gi gsal byed ni/ de thams cad kyi bsdus don rnam 'grel a seng ma'o/ /gnyis pa gud du gsungs pa dang bcas pa'i 'phros
don bcu bdun bshad pa la/ lta ba'i yi ge |dbang gi yi ge /bskyed rim gyi yi ge /dam tshig gi yi ge /gags sel gyi yi ge ste lnga| dang po ni/ 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi rtsa
'grel bsdoms pas gcig go /gnyis pa la/ dbang chu chen po/ byin brlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams pa/ mchog dbang gsum grol lam la brten nas bskur ba/ dbang gi cho ga mtha'
dag mdor bsdus pa man ngag gi gnad de bzhi'o/ /gsum pa la/ yab kyi mngon rtogs rgyas pa yan lag bzhi

pa| 'bring po yan lag drug pa/ bdag med ma'i mngon rtogs/ phyi bskyed pa'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa ste bzhi'o/ /bzhi pa la/ rtsa ltung 'khrul spong / bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub pa'i
cho ga /tshogs 'khor/ las bzhi'i sbyin sreg ste bzhi'o/ /lnga pa la/ byung rgyal du mi btang ba'i gnad rnam pa bzhi/ bsam gtan 'dor ba'i 'phrang bdun bsal ba/ 'byung ba

'das thun mong las 'phros la/ 'og gags sel rnams 'khor 'das thun mong dang / 'khor lo 'cham pa gnyis ka las 'phros pas so/ /gnyis pa ni/ lam 'bring po'i yi ge gcig go /gsum
pa ni/ lam bsdus te sgrub pa'i lung sbyin pa'i yi ge gcig go /gnyis pa de gsum ga'i thun mong gi chos bstan pa la/ nyams su blang ba'i chos/ rtogs pa bskyed pa/ rtogs
pa gsal byed de gsum/ dang po la/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba/ dbang po rab 'bring gsum bkri ba/ gnad drug gis bkri ba/ gnad bcu gcig gis bkri ba ste khrid yig bzhi'o/
/gnyis pa la/ lam 'jug ldog /phyag rgya 'jug ldog /shes pas phan 'dogs pa'i man ngag bdun/ lam sre ba 'gros bzhi dang bcas pa/ phyi nang gi mdzad pa bcu gnyis te lnga'o/
/gsum pa la/ phrin las so gnyis kyi dpe chung / 'chi ltas brtag pa'i 'khor lo gnyis/ rtsa 'khor lo bzhi'i dpe chung / gags sel gzhan gyi dpe chung gnyis/ bha ga'i yi ge
bcu bzhi'i dpe chung ste lnga'o/ / gnyis pa zab 'bring tha gsum bstan pa la/ zab 'bring tha gsum las/ dang po ni/ lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor dbu dbyung ma zhes yi ge
gcig yod la/ gnyis pa 'bring dam tshig dang sdom pa'i lam dang / gsum pa tha ma lus so sor brtag pa'i

/ shod dgon spyan snga ma gnyis/ lnga pa de las gzhan pa/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg /bir bsrung / bdud rtsi ril bu bsgrub pa/ tshogs sbyor mngon rtogs te bzhi rnams
so/ /de ltar yig cha lnga bcu rtsa gnyis kyi lung dang / gzhan yang rjes 'brang yi ge nyi shu rtsa gsum yang / shin tu gces pas 'bad de blta bar bya/ rjes 'brang gi

dpal/ /lhun grub phrin las bzang po'i rgyal mtshan bsgreng / /rgyal ba'i myu gu rgyal mtshan dkon mchog dpal/ /dbang rgyud man ngag bdag po rdor rgyan pa/ /gzhung lugs

gsal byed gcig ste/ bir bsrung gi gsal byed bsrung ba gsum dang sbyar ba/ 'di ni nges pa mi 'dug kyang 'phags pa'i der sbyar bde bas sbyar ba yin no/ /bzhi pa gnyag ma cha

lam 'bring po'i zin bris che ba dang chung ba gnyis so/ /bzhi pa gzhung shing gsal byed kyi yi ge gnyis te/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i gzhung shing gsal byed gnyag
snying po rgyal mtshan gyi dang / nyan chen pa'i khrid yig gnyis so/ kha cig phyi ma 'di nyan chen pa'i gsung ma yin par smra'o/ / rang byin brlabs kyi dmigs pa nyer dgu
dang / dmar gyis mdzad pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor rin 'byung ma dang / gags sel gyi yi ge bzhi'i zhal gdams bla ma dam pa'i phyag dpe las dge slong dpal ldan gyis bris zhes
pa dang / sbas bshad 'phrul 'khor so gnyis dang / birWa pa dang sa chen mjal ba'i lo rgyus rje btsun gyis rga theng la bskur ba yin zer ba sogs 'bri ba dang / sa paN gyi
khrid kyi dkar chag dang / zangs tsha'i zin bris sogs med mi rung gi yi ge du ma 'dor ba ni shin tu mi rigs te/ dang po dmigs pa nyer dgu ni/ saM pu Ta'i rgyud 'chad pa'i
dus su gsung ba'i zhal shes yin gyi| lam 'bras kyi yan lag ma yin pa'i phyir dang / bla ma rin 'byung ni/ don dang

lag len tshang ba bla ma'i rnal 'byor thun mong ma yin pa las 'byung bas 'dir med kyang man ngag ma tshang ba'i skyon med la/ ci nas kyang bri bar byed na'ang dmar gyi yi ge
dag gi gseb tu bgrang bar bya ba yin pa'i phyir dang / gags sel gyi yi ge bzhi'i zhal gdams ni/ rnal 'byor gyi phrin las so gnyis ngos 'dzin pa na/ lus kyi phrin las nyi
shu/ rlung gi bdun/ thun mong gi phrin las lnga zhes sogs 'dir ma grags shing / zhwa ma'i lugs la grags pa mang du snang bas rang gzhan gyi lugs ma phyed par snang ba'i
phyir dang / bla ma dam pa la zhwa ma'i lugs kyi phyag dpe yod pas des/ thun mong min par mi 'grub pa'i phyir dang / sbas bshad 'phrul 'khor so gnyis ni/ mang khar bya tsha
lung pa'i bla ma rgyal mtshan 'bum la bla ma dam pas gsan te phyis byung ba yin pas med mi rung ba'i rtsa ba'i man ngag ma yin pa'i phyir dang / birWa pa dang sa chen
mjal ba'i lo rgyus rje btsun gyis rga theng la bskur ba yin zer ba ni/ deng sang gi dbang rgyud gdams ngag /bsam gyis mi khyab pa ji snyed pa/ sa chen gyis rje btsun sku
mched la brgyud de brgyud pa 'ded pa dang / yi ge der birWa pa dang mjal lugs tsam yang gtan ma thos par rjes su gzhan la dri dgos pa byung zhing / de'ang byis pa 'di tsho
khyed la 'dri ba'i dus gcig 'ong gi de tsa na zlos gsung zer ba shin tu 'gal te/ rnam 'joms bir lugs sogs rnal 'byor dbang phyug kho na la dngos su gsan pa'i gdams ngag
bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams brgyud pa gang las brgyud tsam yang rtsad gcod dka'o// sa paN gyi khrid kyi dkar chag ni ngan rtog gis spangs par snang mod/ bka' sgrub kyi
skabs su tshad mar bsgrubs zin pa'i phyir dang / zangs tsha'i yi ge sogs med mi rung gi yi ge du ma ni gzhan dag gi spyod yul du ma gyur par zad pa'i phyir ro/ /de'i phyir

'dir bris pa 'di dag ni sgro skur dang bral ba yin no/ /yang / zur du gsungs pa'i man ngag la/ rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gsum khug pa/ aShta'i byad
bzlog /go cha lnga bsrung / rten 'brel bsrung ba rnams so/ /rten 'brel bsrung ba'i cha lag rmi lam ngan pa zhi bar bya ba dang / nad zhi bar bya ba dang / dgra zhi bar
bya ba yang yod gsung bas btsal lo/ /lung gi brgyud pa ni/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor yan sgyi chu'i dbang brgyud bzhin la/ 'bum chen la mkhan chen ngag dbang dpal bzang
/ zha lu mkhan rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag la'o/ /da dung dpyad par bya'o/ /gsum pa ni/ nyi gling rjes dga' ldan grub chen kun dga' dpal bzang la/ lam zab
dang bir bsrung gnyis gsan pa'i brgyud pa/ grub chen pas dam chos gling dang mkhan chen byams pa bzang po gnyis ka la gsan pas shes/ lam zab lus dkyil ma/ bir bsrung dag
sbyar ma gnyis/ yig brgya'i bzlas lung / aShta'i bzlas lung / lus dkyil dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus pa gsum ga bskur ba/ dbang bzhi ngo sprod byin brlabs/ phyag rgya chen po
yi ge med pa'i byin brlabs lung bshad dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje lha dbang phrin las kyis sgyi chur gsan pa'i brgyud pa rje yon tan lhun grub yan 'dra zhing
/ de la mkhan chen byams pa bzang po| grub chen kun dga' dpal bzang / rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /nyi gling bla ma rin po ches lam skor phyi ma
brgyad kyi lung dpal gser gling pa la gsan pas/ gang zag bdun gyis mdzad pa'i lam skor brgyad las/ slob dpon padma badzras bskyed rim tshul dgus zab pa rje btsun gyis gsal
bar mdzad pa'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ don gnyis dbyer med rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / /thabs shes dbyer med

si la badzra dang / /spangs rtogs dbyer med lus yan lag med pa'i rdo rje yang ngo med rdo rje dang // bde stong dbyer med mtsho skyes rdo rje'i zhabs/ /gsal stong dbyer med
indra bhU ti ba/ / snang stong dbyer med lcam mo lakShmi/ /zab gsal dbyer med nag po spyod pa ba/ /'khor 'das dbyer med bram ze dpal 'dzin pa/ /dbyer med kun ston ga ya
dha ra ba/ / dbyings rig dbyer med shAkya ye shes zhabs/ /'gyur med bde ba brnyes pa'i se ston pa| |rdo rje rba rlabs thob pa'i dgon pa ba/ /myur mgyogs pho nya'i lam ston
sa chen pa| |byang sems gyen du rdzogs pa rtse mo'i zhabs/ /ye shes gtum mo 'bar ba'i rje btsun pa/ /rlung sems dbang du 'dus pa'i paNDi ta/ /gsung ngag nyi ma shar ba'i
'gro mgon pa/ /nyams myong zla ba rgyas pa'i dkon mchog dpal/ /mkha' mnyam lta ba mnga' ba'i na bza' ba/ /nyams dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag dkon rgyal ba/ /'khor 'das kun
gyi gtsug rgyan bu ston dbang phyug dar pa/ /mtho ris yon tan bdun ldan theg chen pa/ /srid zhi'i rgud pa drungs 'byin brag thog pa/ /snang srid kun la mnga' bsgyur rdor
gdan pa/ /mkhas grub kun gyis rjes bzung rnam mgon sde/ /ye shes tshogs rdzogs 'bras mo mchod khang bsod nams rgya mtsho ba/ /bstan srung bran 'khol tshe dbang bkra shis
pa/ /shes bya'i gnas la tshe dbang kun mkhyen pa/ /rigs brgya'i khyab bdag ye shes dbang po ba/ /bstan pa'i shing rta shAkya bsam grub pa/ /skyabs gnas kun 'dus tshul khrims
bkra shis zhabs/ /bla mar nyes skyon ma mthong phrin las par/ /yang na sa skya paNDi ta/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ gangs khrod pa grags pa dpal/ mkhas grub 'phags
pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen pa'o/ /yang / gangs pa/ sa bzang pa/ theg chen pa/ yang / sa paN/ grub thob yon tan dpal/ la ru ba bsod nams seng

ge |gangs pa'o/ ! /mchod rten drung thob 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi gzhung gi gsal byed rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mi rtog rnam kun mchog ldan rdo rje 'chang
/ /ye shes mthar phyin phyag na rdo rje'i dpal/ /phyag rgya chen po'i mnga' bdag sa ra ha/ /rnam par mi rtog mthar phyin klu sgrub zhabs/ /brjod med thugs su chud pa'i 'phags
pa lha/ /mnyam nyid mngon du gyur pa'i nag po pa/ /chos dbyings mkha' la spyod pa'i zla ba'i zhabs/ /thugs rgyud dbu mas grol ba'i dpal 'dzin pa/ /gdams ngag mdzod
'dzin ga ya dha ra ba/ /gzhan rnams sngar dang 'dra'o/ ! /Dombhi he ru ka'i lhan cig skyes grub phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid gnad khyad par can dang bcas pa tshan gsum gyi brgyud
pa ni/ chos kun lhan skyes rtogs pa rdo rje 'chang / /'khor 'das lhan skyes dbyer med DA ki ni/ /dbyings rig lhan skyes rtogs pa'i DoM bhi ba/ /bde stong lhan skyes
a la la badzra/ /snang stong lhan skyes rtogs pa'i nags khrod pa/ /gsal stong lhan skyes mngon gyur garbha ri/ /rig stong lhan skyes shrI pan dha pa/ /lhan skyes spang blang
med pa'i mi thub zla/ /snod bcud lhan skyes rig pa'i dpa' rdor rje/ /bdag gzhan lhan skyes dbyings mnyam ga ya dhar/ /skad mang lhan skyes smra ba 'brog mi'i zhabs/ /de
man gong bzhin no/ /yang / 'brog /gsal snying / sgyi chu ba/ sa chen/ ngo mtshar snang bar/ lhan cig skyes grub 'brog gis shes rab gsang bar gsan gsung ba brtag go /'di
gsal byed sa chen gyi yin nam snyam mo/ ! /indra bhU ti'i phyag rgya lam rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ mthar thug pho nya grub pa rdo rje 'chang / /ye shes pho nya grub pa bde
chen po/ /de stobs mthar phyin indra bhU ti'i zhabs/ /de nyid pho nya grub pa tshangs pa'i zhabs/ /de nyid pho nya rab mchog bram ze mo/ /de yi nus pa mthar phyin indra
ba/ /gsang chen pho nya

grub pa gos bral zhabs/ /de yi rtsa lag mthar phyin dznyA na pa/ /nang gi pho nya grub pa dpal 'byung ba/ /de mthu mthar phyin padma badzra dang / /phyi yi pho nya grub pa
he ru ka /de yi yan lag mthar phyin padma'i zhabs/ /bung ba'i padma lha mo pho nya mchog /myur mgyogs pho nya'i mtshan ldan lakShmi/ /pho nya kun sdud indra bhU ti ba/ /pho
nya'i lam sbyangs ratna badzra zhabs/ /pho nya'i man ngag mkhas pa sher bzang pa/ /pho nya shing rta'i srol 'byed 'brog mi ba/ /de man gong dang 'dra/ nye brgyud ni/ rdo
rje 'chang / indra bhU ti/ lcam lakShmi ka ra/ rin chen rdo rje/ shes rab bzang / 'brog mi'o/ /'di rgya gzhung rang yin no/ ! /slob dpon tog tse pa'i bsam mi khyab kyi
gsal byed sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'bras bu bsam gyis mi khyab rdo rje 'chang / /spangs pa bsam gyis mi khyab rta mchog pa// rtogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab bi
na pa/ /byang chub bsam gyis mi khyab indra pa/ /ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab lakShi pa/ /gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab sgeg pa'i zhabs/ / byin brlabs bsam gyis mi khyab gun
dhe ri/ /rlung sems bsam gyis mi khyab padma pa// lta ba bsam gyis mi khyab chos kyi pa/ /spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab bzang po'i zhabs// sgom pa bsam gyis mi khyab tog tse
pa/ /thabs lam bsam gyis mi khyab gu sha na/ / gdams ngag bsam gyis mi khyab padma pa/ /ting 'dzin bsam gyis mi khyab karNa pa/ / rnal 'byor bsam gyis mi khyab dpa' bo'i
zhabs/ /bsam mi khyab kyi srol 'byed 'brog mi ba/ /gzhan rnams sngar dang 'dra/ ! slob dpon nag po spyod pa'i gtum mo lam rdzogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ mthar thug gtum mo'i
lam rdzogs rdo rje 'chang / /de nyid gtum mo'i lam rdzogs rnal 'byor ma/ /gsang ba'i gtum mo'i lam rdzogs dza lan dha| |nang gi gtum mo'i lam rdzogs nag po pa/ /phyi yi gtum
mo'i lam rdzogs dpal

'dzin pa/ /gtum mo'i man ngag mnga' bdag ga ya dhar/ /gzhan rnams sngar dang 'dra/ ! yang / slob dpon de'i yon po srong ba'i brgyud pa ni/ 'bras bu yon po bsrang ba rdo rje
'chang / /ye shes yon po bsrang ba rnal 'byor ma/ /thig le yon po bsrang ba dza lan dha| |rlung sems yon po bsrang ba nag po pa/ /rtsa yig yon po bsrang ba dpal 'dzin pa|
|yon po srong ba'i lam ston ga ya dhar/ /gzhan rnams sngar dang 'dra/ gtum mo lam rdzogs dang yon po bsrang ba gnyis kyi gsal byed rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan
gyis mdzad pa'o/ ! /slob dpon ngag dbang grags pa'i phyag rgya chen po yi ge med pa'i gsal byed rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thabs mchog bla na med pa rdo
rje 'chang / /shes rab yi ge med pa sgrol ma'i zhabs/ /bzhi pa yi ge med pa ngag dbang grags/ /bde la yi ge med pa 'byung gnas lha/ /gsang ba yi ge med pa a mo gha/ /yi
ge med pa'i lam ston gha ya'i zhabs/ /gzhan rnams sngar dang 'dra/ de ltar brgyad do/ ! /yang / gong padma badzra'i lam gyi khog rdzogs rim mar me'i rtse mo lta bu 'brog
mis bsgyur ba'ang zhus/ 'di gsan yig rgya mtsho'i mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i rdzogs rim gy-i man ngag ces pa dang mtshungs sam snyam zhes/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims
zhabs kyi gsan yig na thugs dogs zos pa/ lu phu bla brang gi phyag dpe na/ mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa ga ya dha ra dang / 'brog mis bsgyur ba'i dpe tshan gcig 'dug
pas gsan yig rgya mtsho dang mthun no/ /de'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'brog mi/ gsal snying / sgyi chu ba/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ grags pa/ sa paN/ grub thob/ la ru/ de gnyis
la mkhan po grags pa dpal/ bla ma mgon po dpal/ de gnyis la rin po che grags tshul/ mkhan chen rgyal bzangs/ theg chen pa man gong bzhin no/ ! /rjes 'brang nyer

gsum gyi zhar la rje btsun mu srad pa'i dkar chag gi lung dang / rje btsun mu srad pa'i/ kye rdor rgyud kyi dkar chag dang / man ngag gi dkar chag tshigs bcad ma dang / phra
mo glegs bam gyi dkar chag rnams kyi lung brgyud ni byams pa yon tan lhun grub yan dbang brgyud bzhin/ de la mkhan chen byams pa bzang po/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/
rje ngag dbang dpal bzang / zha lu mkhan chen/ des bdag go /de'i nang bzhin rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i zur gsungs kyi yi ge bzhi tshar gsum khug pa lan gnyis/ aShta'i
byad bzlog /go cha lnga srung rnams kyi byin brlabs thob/ brgyud pa dbang dang 'dra'o/ /lam skor lhag ma brgyad kyi gsal byed yi ge bdun po/ lam skor zin bris bar ston
ma/ bsam gyis mi khyab kyi zin bris/ yi ge med kyi khrid/ gnad du che ba drug / lam skor 'byung khungs/ bsam mi khyab kyi lo rgyus/ bsam mi khyab kyi byin brlabs dang
sgo drug chos 'brel de rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa rjes 'brang nyer gsum bzhin/ mkhan chen zha lu pa'i bka' drin las thob bo/ /dri lan rmongs pa'i mun sel gyi lung
lan gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang gi rgyal po/ thugs sras rim gro pa shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rje rnam rgyal

rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang bsod nams mchog ldan/ chos rje phrin las rnam rgyal/ byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ bla ma bkra shis don 'grub/ chos rje phun tshogs rnam rgyal/

grags pa/ nub pa rig 'dzin grags/ skyo ston dri med/ bla ma dharma ye shes/ bla ma gzhon tshul ba/ mkhan chen sher rdor/ yang na| rje btsun sa paN/ khang ston/ kun bsod/

nas gzhi lhas te'o/ ! /rdo rje rnam 'joms lha don lnga'i byin brlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul gyi yi ge nA lendra pa kun dga' chos grags kyis mdzad pa nas byin brlabs dang lung
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje rnam 'joms/ birWa pa/ sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paN chen/ skyo ston dri med/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ dga'
ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ shar chen ye rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan/ de gnyis ka la mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ sems dpa' chen po ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rtsa ba'i
bla ma

gan pa ston dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa chos rin/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla chen kun rgyal/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po'o/
/yang / la lar 'phags pa rin po che/ gan pa 'jam dbyangs rin rgyal ba/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhes 'dug pa ni mi 'thad de/ gan pa rin rgyal dang 'jam dbyangs rin
rgyal mi gcig pas/ glang gi ya mchu dang / phag gi ma mchu sprad pa bzhin no/ /brag thog gsan yig dang / gsan yig rgya mtsho gnyis na med cing rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa'i
gur gyi dkyil chog khungs ma rnams na'ang de ltar med do/ /'di la'ang bla chen kun rgyal gyi gnas su sa bzang paN chen bcug kyang 'dra gsung ngo / / yang / lugs gcig
la/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje snying po/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ klu sgrub/ ma tanggi/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa/ rngog mdo sde/ ram glu gong pa/ gram phug pa dkon mchog
'khar/ tshul khrims skyabs/ 'phags skyabs/ ston gzhon/ chos 'od/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma 'phags pa'o/ /gsan yig rgya mtshor/ 'phags pa rin po che/ tshogs sgom
pa/ nyan chen pa/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ zhes 'di gzhan na min 'dug pas dpyad do/ /yang / bla ma dpal ldan legs dbang gi gsan yig las/ lugs gcig la/ rdo rje gur/ ti
lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa/ mes ston tshon po/ sgyi chu ba/ sa chen sogs/ yang / lugs gcig la/ sa chen yan man ngag brgyud pa dang mtshungs par yang bgrangs 'dug pa theg chen
chos rje'i dgongs pa yin par sems so/ ! /gur sgrol bcu gcig ma'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs par 'phags pa'i mngon dkyil nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ Dombhi he ru ka /'jam dpal grags pa/ dza landha ra pa/ se'u ri

pa| 'jigs med 'byung gnas/ dge ba'i 'byung gnas/ dpe med 'tsho/ a ba dhU tI pa| darpan A tsarYa/ glo bo lo tsA shes rab rin chen/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/
na bza' brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ lo chen skyabs mchog dpal/ bla ma nam mkha' 'od zer/ lo chen shes rab rin chen/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ mkhas
grub rigs pa'i glog phreng / bla ma ma Ni badzra/ rje dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag go /'di sgrol ma bcu bdun ma'i dkyil chog
la brten nas so/ ! /rta mchog gi rigs sgrol ma mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud/ slob dpon nyi ma sbas pa'i gzhung las lus dkyil phyi dkyil gnyis las phyi dkyil phyag 'tshal sgrol
ma nyer gcig gi rjes su 'brangs pa sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs par 'phags pa'i mngon dkyil nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ slob dpon nyi ma sbas pa/ tsandra garbha/ dgra las rnam rgyal/ slob dpon ngag dbang grags pa/ dad byed go cha/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsrung ba/ dA
na shrI/ manydzu shrI/ mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa paN/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa/ nyi thog pa/ mchog ldan legs pa'i
blo gros/ blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ gar thig pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams
cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ mkhas grub rig pa'i glog phreng / bla ma ma Ni badzra/ rje btsun dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'dzin pa bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag
go /brgyud pa gtso che ba 'og na'ang yod do/ /yang na/ mal lo/ sa chen/ rje btsun grags pa/ mchims chos kyi seng ge /chos rje 'jam

gsar/ bla ma rgwa lo/ bla ma shes rab seng ge /bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje'o/ /yang na/ rje btsun ma/ klu sgrub/
nyi ma sbas pa/ dA na shrI'o/ /yang na/ mal lo/ pu cer lo tsA ba rgyal mtshan tshul khrims/ la stod pa dbang phyug rin chen/ mchims chos seng / mchims blo gros brtan
pa| mchims nam mkha' grags/ 'phags pa rin po che/ bla ma bsod nams seng ge/ gu ru pra bha sidhi/ mnga' ris pa grags pa 'od zer/ rdo rje 'dzin pa dpal ldan blo gros/ brag
thog pa chen po'o/ /yang / gtso 'di che ste/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ nyi ma sbas pa/ dA na shrI| manydzu shrI/ mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/
rje btsun rin po che/ sa paNDi ta chen po/ 'phags pa rin po che/ bla ma ye shes rin chen/ bla ma 'khon ston/ bla ma klu byang pa/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod
nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ mkhas grub
rigs pa'i glog phreng / bla ma ma Ni badzra/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag la'o/ ! /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur
gyi mgon po la dbang rjes gnang / lung man ngag bsam gyis mi khyab kyang / dpal sa skya pa la brgyud pa bzhi las bka' babs pa ste/ bla ma ba ri lo tsA nas bka' babs/ bram
ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'i gzhung la brten pa'i mgon rkyang sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i nang du bzhugs pa dang / kIrti paN chen nas brgyud pa/ yar klung grags rgyal gyis
bsgyur ba rgya mtsho na bzhugs pa gnyis gcig tu bsdoms pa dang / ga ya dha ra nas brgyud pa lam 'bras mgon rkyang dang / mal lo tsA nas brgyud pa rnams

dang / paN chen shAkya shrI nas sa skya paNDi ta la bka' babs pa gsang sgrub spu gri skor gsum du grags pa'o/ /de yang gur gyi mgon po gri gug lha lnga'i dbang bram ze mchog
sred kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog la brten nas rgya gzhung lugs su grags pa'i rig pa'i dbang lnga/ slob dpon gyi dbang / sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las kyi rjes gnang
bzlas lung / gtor dbang dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi DA ki ma/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ indra bhU ti/ phun tshogs
bde ba/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ ga ya dha ra/ bla chen 'brog mi/ se ston kun rig /zhang ston chos 'bar/ sa chen kun snying / slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun
grags pa/ sa skya paN chen/ bla ma shes rab 'byung gnas/ bla ma rdo rje 'od zer/ 'phags pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma kun bsod pa/ bla ma gzhon tshul ba/ mkhan
chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ yongs
'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ nyi gling tshul khrims bkra shis/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang blo
gros dbang phyug / mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/ bla chen kun dga' chos 'phel/ byams pa ye shes rnam rgyal/ mtshungs med byams pa phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag
ngag ming la'o/ /paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / gri gug lha lnga thun mong ma yin pa/ ga ya dha ra nas brgyud pa man ngag lugs dbang bzhi dang
bcas pa'i yig cha mgon po rnam rol theg chen chos kyi rgyal po dang / 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i lhan thabs sbyar ba'i
steng nas rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dam

pa kun dga' grags yan gong bzhin las/ dam pa la rong mi ye shes/ tre bo rdo rje grags/ bag ston pa/ bla ma tshul rgyal ba/ bla ma ngag dbang pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po|
chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan nam mtshan gzhan 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i dpal/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo
rje gdan pa/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma rnam rgyal bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ nyi gling tshul khrims
bkra shis nas gong ltar bdag la'o/ /paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims/ des bdag go ! /yang / gur mgon lha brgyad ma'i dbang dang / lha bcu gnyis ma'i dbang rgya gzhung lugs
rig pa'i dbang lnga/ slob dpon gyi dbang sku gsung thugs phrin las kyi rjes gnang / bzlas lung dang bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje gur/ bram ze
mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje nas 'phags pa yan gur lha gsum ma'i rjes gnang brgyud pa bzhin/ 'phags pa rin po che/ bkras lung pa/ dge sdings pa chen po/ sangs rgyas dpal/
rin chen gling pa/ rin chen rdo rje ba/ theg chen pa/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / brag thog pa dpal 'dzin bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen
pa rdo rje gdan pa/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ dpal shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ paN chen tshul khrims bkra shis nas gong ltar bdag
la'o/ /paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims/ des bdag go ! /yang / gur gyi mgon po la gshin rje pho brgyad mo brgyad kyis bskor ba'i dbang dur khrod nag po'i rgyud kyi rjes su
'brangs pa/ rig pa'i dbang lnga/ slob dpon/ rjes gnang / bzlas lung bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i

rdo rje/ shraddha ka ra warma 'thad/ jo bo rje/ lcags ri gong kha ba/ rdzing bu kha pa/ spen phug pa zhang ye/ gze ba don grub seng ge /bar thang pa yab sras/ 'dar shag pa
slob dpon bsod nams dbang / bla ma mchog ldan/ kyi ston grags rgyal/ rin chen rdo rje/ mkhan chen nam mkha' ye shes/ byang seng pa/ de gsum ga la theg chen chos rgyal man
gong bzhin no/ /yang na shraddha ka ra warma yan lha gsum ma'i rjes gnang bzhin las/ jo bo rje| lo chen rin chen bzang po/ dge tshul purNa/ lcags ri gong kha ba nas lo mchog
gi bar/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang dpal ldan blo gros/ dmar ston
rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ byams gling bsod nams rnam rgyal/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ 'jam dbyangs byang dbang / bla chen shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug
rgyal mtshan/ nyi gling tshul khrims bkra shis/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang blo gros dbang phyug /mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/
bla chen kun dga' chos 'phel/ rong pa dkon mchog sbyin pa/ byams pa phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag ngag ming la'o/ /paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims/ des bdag go /de
'di man ser thal bas slar rgyag dgos so dag gi yig cha theg chen pa'i mgon po rnam rol/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i sgrub thabs bdud las rnam rgyal dang / dkyil chog la thams
cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i gsung mchan dang / lhan thabs thig rtsa sogs la brten nas legs par thob/ spro na gtor dbang mdzad pa yang rung tshul lo/ ! /bshad rgyud
thun mong ba saM bu Ti nas dngos su dkyil 'khor bcu drug gsungs pa las/ kye rdo rje mtshon cha can nam drag po gdan can lha bcu bcun gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du yig
cha sna tshogs shig gi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par

thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ Dombhi he ru ka /a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ dza ya shrI/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/
shAkya ye shes/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra bla 'bar/ sa skya pa chen po| slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa skya paNDi
ta/ khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ bka' bcu pa gzhon nu seng ge /kun mkhyen bde legs dpal/ bla ma dpal ldan don grub/ rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan nam mtshan gzhan 'jam
dbyangs grags pa'i dpal/ bla chen chos skyong bzang po/ rtsangs byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rje shes rab rin chen/ byams pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ byams pa nam mkha'
rgya mtsho/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor/ sgyi chu ba rdo rje 'chang byams pa bsod nams phun tshogs/ des bdag go ! /dpal kye rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa'i
bshad pa rgyud gsum sbags bshad kyi tshul du/ theg chen pa'i dag ldan snye ma dang / 'dzin chos rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i steng nas thob cing
/ yang / de'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag la'o/ /de'i rgyab chos
kyi lung la/ kye rdor rgyud gsum dang / rgyud sde'i dum bu rnam gzhag mngon rtogs dang / stong 'thun gnyis kyi bsdus don bstod pa gnyis/ bdag med bstod pa'i rnam 'grel dang
bcas pa| kun tu dgos pa'i gzhung bdun dang dag ldan snye ma rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan yan lam 'bras bzhin
las/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal/ rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rgyal mtshan dkon mchog / byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rje dkon mchog dpal/ paN chen lha dbang blo gros/

mkhas grub mang thos rab gsal/ rje bzang po bkra shis/ byams pa yon tan lhun grub/ mkhan chen byams pa bzang po/ dga' ldan grub chen kun dga' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs dbang
phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'dzin pa paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des phrin las pa la'o/ /yang na rje dkon mchog dpal/ paN chen lha dbang blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs shes
rab legs pa/ rje bzang po bkra shis/ bla chen chos dpal bzang po/ byams pa yon tan lhun grub man 'dra'o/ /(kha)! gnyis pa shes rab gtso bor ston pa rnal 'byor chen po ma

po'i zhabs/ gadgA dha ra gang gA 'dzin/ su ra ta badzra rab dga' rdo rje/ shrI dha ra dpal 'dzin/ dznyA na badzra ye shes rdo rje/ he ru ka badzra/ sa ha dzrananta badzra
lhan cig skyes dga'i rdo rje/ dharme shwa ra chos kyi dbang phyug /mA ra kaNDe de ba bdud 'dul lha/ ma hendha ra sa 'dzin/ birYa shrI mi tra brtson 'grus dpal bshes gnyen/
dharmA kIrti dhwa dza chos grags rgyal mtshan/ ratna kIrti rin chen rdo rje| shrI ba na ratna dpal nags kyi rin po che/ swa mi A nanta bi dza ya rje kun dga' rnam rgyal/
ma ti

aM sa blo gros thogs med/ shAkya A nanta kun dga'/ gu ru sangga'i mtshan dge 'dun legs grub/ shrI shI la mangga la dpal tshul khrims bkra shis/ karma bi dza ya'o phrin las
rnam rgyal lo/ /yang na/ shrI ba na ratna/ swa mi puNya bha dra pA da rje bsod nams bzang po/ dharma swa mi badzra A sa na pA da chos kyi rje rdo rje gdan pa'i zhabs/ gu
ru bla ma blo gros thogs med ma ti aM sa sogs so/ ! /lU hi pa'i lugs kyi rdzogs rim bde mchog dkar po lhan skyes kyi byin brlabs kha che paN chen gyi zab chos 'bebs chog

mchog grub/ bka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ mkhan chen rig 'dzin rgyal po/ bla chen chos rig rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsod nams dpal 'byor/
'jam dbyangs byang gling chos rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams
mchog ldan/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen rgya mtsho/ des bdag go /yang na/ 'jam dpal/ ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ tha ga na/ bhu sha na pa/ ngag dbang grags pa/ bhi la shAnti/
bhiM ga ra pA da/ shrAddha ka ra warma/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ rkyang po chos blo/ gcung po zhang khri/ gnyal pa skyogs ston/ khun tsi gzhon nu rin chen/ gtsang rong
pa shes rab gzhon nu/ slob dpon dkon mchog 'bar/ g.yag sde ba dbang phyug rin chen/ khams ston shAkya rdo rje man 'dra/ ! bka' babs gnyis pa jo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
'jam dbyangs/ ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ A nanta garbha/ tha ga na/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ jo bo rje/ mar me mdzad/ lcags ri gong kha ba/ rdzi'u kha pa/ spen phug
pa/ zhang ye shes/ gze ba don grub/ bar thang pa yab sras/ dar ma shAkya/ bsod nams dbang phyug /lo mchog pa man 'dra/ ! bka' babs gsum pa sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam
dpal rdo rje/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ paN grub mar me mdzad bzang po| dpal bde ba'i zhabs/ bi mA la gupta/ ratna badzra/ ratna kIrti/ ri sul gyi rnal

'byor ma/ bla ma penda pa/ gnyan lo dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paNDi ta/ 'phags
pa rin po che/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ khams pa rdo rje dpal/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa/ paN chen ma ti/ sa bzang
'phags pa/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ bya 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge /sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ thams cad mkhyen
pa mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ ! bka' babs bzhi pa rwa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ dpal bde
ba/ dri med sbas pa/ rin chen rdo rje/ rin chen grags pa/ sa manta pra bha/ dznyA na shrI mi tra/ ratna kIrti/ puNya shrI/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rdo rje sra brtan
man lo chen lugs dang 'dra/ ! bka' babs lnga pa gnyos lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bi mA gupta yan rwa lugs ltar la/ de nas yi ge'i rnal 'byor ma/ kahna pa/ badzra shrI/ ba lingta
A' tsarya/ gnyos lo tsA ba yon tan grags/ gnyos rdo rje bla ma/ gnyos dpal le/ gnyos grags pa dpal/ gnyos gzi brjid dpal/ ston mo lung pa ye shes mkhar/ kun mkhyen chos
sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa man sngar dang 'dra/ yang na gnyos rdo rje bla ma nas gnyos ston grags pa dpal/ gnyos lha nang
/ rin chen do pa mdog stod ser ma/ glas pa dpon rdo rje tshul khrims/ g.yas ru ba rdos ston rin chen rgyal mtshan/ don ri ba grags pa dpal bzang / ma ti paN chen man sa lugs
dang 'dra/ ! bka' babs drug pa kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs/ sangs rgyas ye shes

zhabs/ mar me mdzad nas rim par brgyud de/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ kha che'i paNDi ta ga ya dha ra/ paNDi ta bi na shrI/ de la go pa la'i pho brang du khams pa rdo rje
dpal gyis zhus/ de nas kIrti shrI/ kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa man sa lugs bzhin no/ ! /mi bskyod pa'i rigs drag po rnam gsum 'dul ba zhes bya ba le'u gsum pa nas gsungs
pa'i dkyil 'khor bzhi las/ grub chen dza ba ri pa'i lugs phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po dbang gis che ba lha bco brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor du 'dul 'dzin grags pa rgyal mtshan
gyi yi ge nas dbang bzhi thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong pa can/ grub chen sA wa ri pa/ paN grub dzA wa ri pa/
bal po'i paNDi ta de wa purNa ma ti/ 'gar lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po/ gshen ston rin chen dngos grub/ dmar sgang bu ba chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ dmar shes rab rdo rje/ dmar
thub pa shes rab/ dmar brtson 'grus rdo rje/ dmar chos kyi rgyal po/ dmar shAkya grub pa/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ bla ma tshul rgyal ba/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang
/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang / grub chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rje ngag dbang blo gros/ dmar ston tshul khrims rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa dge 'dun bkra shis/

rje 'chang pha bong kha pa dpal 'byor lhun grub/ zur thams cad mkhyen pa chos dbyings rang grol/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ zhabs
drung ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phrin las/ des bdag go /yang na dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan nas/ sgang ston rin chen bla ma/ sgang ston shes rab 'bum/ grub ston shes rab 'bum/

gru rdo rje seng ge /gru chos kyi mgon po/ khams ston lho tshad pa/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug /bla ma byang chub rin chen/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rje byams pa mgon po|

re'u mig dgu/ de'i phyi rol du snam bu zlum pos bskor ba/ de'i phyi rol gru bzhi sgo bzhi sogs gsungs ngor dang sgyi chu dang rgyud dang mthun/ la li ta badzra gyis mdzad pa'i
