bor ston pa dang / shes rab gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud gnyis kyi dang po la rtsa ba'i rgyud/ bshad pa'i rgyud/ 'phros pa'am cha mthun gyi rgyud gsum gyi dang po la dkyil
'khor nyis brgya bcu gsum gsungs pa las/ rdo rje dbyings rtsa ba'i lha so bdun/ bskal bzang sems dpa' dgu brgya dang dgu bcu rtsa drug bcas pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor

par thob pa'i brgyud pa yo ga smad lugs ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rA dza rab gsal zla ba| sgra gcan 'dzin/ dpa' bo ta pha la/ ye shes
rdo rje/ pradznyA siddhi dang bzhi la kun

dga' snying po/ pradznyA ba li ta/ pradznyA bo dhi/ mukti ko Sha/ shraddha ka ra warma/ jo bo rin chen bzang po/ rkyang po chos blo/ sum ston ye 'bar/ lce zhar ba/ spru ston
'bar thog / rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs smra seng / lce jo mdo/ bla ma chos 'od/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho/ rje btsun rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ bla ma yon tan rgya mtsho/ bla ma u rgyan rgyal po/ rje bsod nams rgyal po/ rdo rje
'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ chos rje phrin las rnam rgyal/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ mtshungs med blo gros dbang phyug /mkhan chen kun dga' rgya mtsho/ gser 'bum phun
tshogs rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen ye shes rnam rgyal/ bka' drin mtshungs med shA sa na dhA ra/ des bdag wA gindra shI la dhwa dza la'o/ /des phrin las par dgyes bzhin du gnang
ba'o/ /stod lugs ni/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad/ badzra satwa/ pra kA sha tsandra/ rA hu la/ dpa' bo ta pha la/ dznyA na badzra/ pradznyA siddhiH de bzhi ka
la A nanda garbha/ pradznyA ba li ta/ su bhU ti pa li ta/ dharma pA la/ lo chen rin bzangs/ gur shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ gnur nyi ma 'od
zer/ rtsa skya ston grags/ slob dpon shAkya 'bum/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma chos 'od/ bla ma 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ yang / su bhU ti pa li ta nas/ pradznyA bo dhi/
mukti ko Sha/ dharma pA la'o/ /yang / rtsa skya ston grags/ mnyam khad pa rgya gar 'phan/ bla ma shAkya 'bum/ yang / bla ma dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog /bla ma dpal
ldan seng ge /bu ston no/ /yang / rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang kha la/ dkyil chog rdo rje 'byung ba'i lugs kyi rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum dang / 'grel chen de nyid snang ba nas
'byung ba'i dbang shin tu rgyas pa lugs gnyis kyi dang po ni/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pas mdzad pa'i dkyil chog rin chen

bsam 'phel la/ byang gling pa chos rje dbon rgyal bas mdzad pa'i lhan thabs sbyar/ dbang chog gsal byed rgyas pa shar chen slob dpon chen po ye shes rgya mtshos mdzad pa dang
/ bsdus pa rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rjes mdzad pa'am/ chos rje dbon rgyal bas mdzad pa'i steng nas 'jug pa sngon du 'gro ba'i rdo rje slob ma'i dbang dang / rdo
rje slob dpon gyi dbang sogs phyag rgya gsang bar gdams pa/ dkyil 'khor mchod pa/ btsa' ru'i bza' ba'i bar smin rgyas su thob pa'i smad lugs su grags pa'i dbang gi brgyud
pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad/ dpal rdo rje sems dpa'/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ rgyal bu sgra gcan 'dzin/ dpa' bo ta pha la/ ye shes rdo
rje/ pradznyA siddhi/ de bzhi ka la slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ pradznyA wa li ta/ rab 'byor skyangs/ shraddha kA ra warma/ sangs rgyas zhi ba/ bod yul mun pa'i sgron me
lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ de gnyis ka la sgyang ro ba rkyang po chos blos gsan/ mkhyen rab chos rje dang / rin chen rgya mtsho'i gsan yig
na/ rkyang po chos blo la/ sum ston gyis gsan 'dug /lo chung la sum ston ye 'bar dang / lce zhar ba gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis la stag tshal gdong sngon gyi spru ston 'bar
thog /ro smad lha steng gi rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs ston smra seng / lce mdo sde seng ge /kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams
cad mkhyen pa chen po/ mkhas grub lotstsha ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ lcaie btsun rin chen nam mkha' mchog grub/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos
rje/ byang gling pa rin chen rgyal po/ sku zhang bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling 'jam dbyangs bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ lha 'o ba rdo rje 'chang rin chen rgya mtsho dpal
bzang po/ des mkhan

rin po che rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des phrin las pa la'o/ /! zangs dkar lugs ni/ yang / bcom ldan 'das rnam snang / phyag na rdo rje/ indra bhU ti che ba/ bar ma/ chung
ba/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ klu'i byang chub/ ye shes rdo rje/ kun dga' snying po/ rab dbyings bshes gnyen/ padma kA ra/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs shes/ zangs
dkar lo tsA/ 'phags pa shes rab bam gzhon nu tshul khrims/ klog skya seng ge rgyal mtshan la/ spyang tshang ston pa rtse mo dang / jo shes gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis
la rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs ston smra seng man 'dra/ yang na/ chos 'od la/ lce blo ldan seng ge /'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na byang gling 'jam
dbyangs rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ chos 'khor ba rje bsod nams dpal 'byor/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go
/yang na/ byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ rin lding pa sangs rgyas tshe dpal/ mkhan chen nam mkha' chos ldan/ dus 'khor ba bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis la rtsa ba'i
bla ma/ des bdag go /yang na rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ chos rje bkra shis dpal 'byor/ byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen rab chos rje/ sku zhang
bsod nams mchog grub/ chos rje 'brog sgang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis la byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen rab rje/ byang gling pa rin chen
rgyal po/ chos rje bkra shis dpal 'byor/ byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs man 'dra/ ! stod lugs su grags pa'i dbang brgyud ni/ rab 'byor skyangs/ dharma pA la/ 'jig rten
mig mkhan lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ gur shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/

rtsa skya ston pa dkon mchog grags/ slob dpon shAkya 'bum/ rtsa skya ston pa'ang zer/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na/ snur
nyi ma 'od zer/ snur badzra sing ha/ glan chos 'byung / slob dpon shAkya 'bum/ rtsa skya khri stan/ snur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ snur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ 'phags 'od man
'dra/ ! kha che lugs ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ dpa' bo ta pha la/ ye shes rdo rje/ pradznyA siddhi dang bzhis A nanta
garbha la gnang / de nas pradznyA wa li ta/ pradznyA bo dhi/ mukti ko Sha/ shraddha ka ra warma/ bod yul snang byed lo chen rin chen bzang po/ rkyang po chos blo/ sum
ston ye shes 'bar/ lce zhar ba| spru ston 'bar thog /rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs smra seng man 'dra/ ! dbus 'gyur 'chang lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ mukti ko Sha/ sangs
rgyas zhi ba/ bstan pa'i srol gtod lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ de gnyis ka la rkyang po chos blo man 'dra/ rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa 'di nyid kyis/
nyi gling rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis la yang gsan no/ ! /gnyis pa bshad pa'i rgyud rdo rje rtse mo las dngos su dkyil 'khor dgu gsungs pa'i/ rdo rje rtse mo
rigs thams cad bsdus pa gsang ba mchod chen gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho'i ngag 'don la/ bskur chog kun mkhyen bu'i dkyil chog mkhas
pa'i yid 'phrog nas kha bskang stai dbang rdzogs par thob pa'i gzhi'i dkyil 'khor sgo nyis sbrag /dbus dkyil la rnam snang lha sum cu rtsa gsum/ shar du sangs rgyas gzugs
can lha so gsum/ lhor sangs rgyas nyi ma lha so gsum/ nub tu sangs rgyas sna tshogs gzugs can lha so gsum/ byang du sangs rgyas chos 'dzin rgyal po lha so gsum/ shar lhor
zla ba'i dkyil

'khor la rdo rje sems dpa' lha lnga/ lho nub tu padma'i dkyil 'khor la padma'i sems dpa' lha lnga/ nub byang du nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor la rin chen sems dpa' lha lnga/ byang
shar du utpa la'i dkyil 'khor la rdo rje las lha lnga/ gzhi dkyil nang ma'i grwa bzhir 'byung bzhi'i lha bzhi/ gzhi dkyil phyi ma'i grwa bzhir mchod lha nyi shu/ sgo bzhir
sgo ba nyi shu| 'jig rten pa bzhi bcu zhe drug /skal bzang dgu brgya dgu bcu go drug dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du/ dkyil 'khor so sor 'jug pa'i dbang bskur ba rgyas par

rA hu la bha dra/ A nanta garbha/ wA g-I shwa ra kIrti/ akSho bhya badzra/ ba manta pa/ ratna A ka ra shAnti/ bram ze ka ra wa ti/ shraddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen

rong pa chos mgon/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ bu ston rin po che'o/ /yang na/ sangs rgyas/ rdor snying / indra bhU ti che ba/ bhi na shrI/ indra bhU ti
bar pa/ lcam lakShmi ka ra/ padma badzra/ slob dpon klu sgrub/ Arya de ba/ nA ga bo dhi/ dge slong a mo gha pA sha /rnal 'byor ma ka ma la bi ta/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ bri

rgya mtsho/ grwa thang snyan mkhar slob dpon/ kun dga' chos dar/ bka' drin mtshungs med bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag shI la dhwa dza la'o/ /des phrin las pa'o/ /'di

bcu rtsa bzhi dang bcas pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho'i ngag 'don la/ kun mkhyen bu'i dkyil chog 'jig rten gsum rgyal 'byung ba nas dbang

gros dbang phyug /mkhan chen kun dga' chos 'phel/ byams pa kun dga' brtson 'grus/ byams pa bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag wA gi ming can la'o/ /yang / snur nyi nas/ spru
ston 'bar thog /rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ de sras 'byung gnas seng ge'am smra seng / lce mdo sde seng ge /chos 'od/ lce blo ldan seng ge /'phags 'od/ bu ston rinachen
grub/ de gnyis yo ga stod lugs so/ /smad lugs ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ rab gsal zla ba/ de'i slob ma'i mchog bzhi ni/ pad dkar ye shes/ ye shes rdo rje/ rgyal bu sgra
gcan 'dzin bzang po| nyi ma'i snying po/ de bzhis rgyal ris sa ra ha pa kun dga' snying po la gsungs/ de nas tha ga na pa/ ngag dbang grags pa/ bha lendra shAnti/ mi bskyod
rdo rje/ shraddha kA ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung / shangs kyi sum ston ye 'bar/ g.yag sde'i gnyan ston tshul 'bar/ thod pa dben tsha grags/ dge bshes
jo phur/ thod pa 'od zer/ rong pa chos mgon/ lce blo ldan seng ge /'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ ! gnyis pa la de nyid bsdus pa'i cha mthun
pa'i rgyud dpal mchog dang po zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rgyud las/ slob dpon kun snying dkyil 'khor brgya bcu rtsa bzhir bzhed/ slob dpon padma badzra bdun cu rtsa brgyad
du bzhed pa las/ dpal mchog rigs bsdus slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho'i ngag 'don dang lhan thabs/ kun mkhyen bu'i dkyil chog don yod pa'i dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor 'byung
ba nas/ gzhi

dkyil sgo nyis sbrag la sgo bsrungs 'khor los bsgyur ba brgyad/ nang dkyil dbus mar rdo rje sems dpa' lha so gsum/ 'jig rten pa zhe bzhi/ shar mar hU~M mdzad lha dgu/ 'jig
rten pa zhe gnyis/ mtshams ma bzhi/ mtshan ma bzhi yang ngo / /lho mar nam snying lha dgu/ mtshan ma brgyad/ nub mar spyan ras gzigs lha 'di lha bcu gsum dang mtshan ma bzhi
thang bcu bdun/ byang mar rdo rje khu tshur lha bdun/ shar lhor 'jam dpal lha dgu mtshan ma brgyad/ lho nub nam mkha' mdzod lha bcu gsum mtshan ma bzhi/ nub byang rdo
rje 'khor lo lha bcu gsum/ de'i grwa bzhir yang / shar lhor zhi mdung / lho nub ming po/ nub byang sring mo/ byang shar nag chen rnams/ lha grangs gzhi dkyil gyi 'jig rten
pa lta bu/ byang shar gnod sbyin lha dgu mtshan ma bcu gnyis/ gzhi dkyil phyi ma'i grwa bzhi'i lhor zhi mdung gi dkyil 'khor du/ dbang phyug chen po lha sum cu yi ge dang
bcas pa/ lho nub ma mo'i dkyil 'khor lha bcu gsum/ nub byang ming po gsum lha bcu gcig /byang shar sring mo'i la lha bzhi mtshan ma bzhi dang bcas te yongs sgril lha
sum brgya dang sum cu so dgu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ bu'i dkyil chog chen mo dang / slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho'i ngag 'don dang / rje thams cad mkhyen pa chen
pos bskul te/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i lhan thabs la yang brten nas dbang bskur ba yang dag par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ smad lugs/ buddha bai rau tsa na sangs
rgyas rnam par snang mdzad/ badzra pA Ni phyag na rdo rje/ ra bi shrI nyi ma'i dpal/ badzra warma rdo rje go cha/ A nanta garbha kun dga' snying po/ manydzu shrI bi
ma la kIrti 'jam dpal dri med grags pa/ su bhu ti pa li ta rab 'byor bskyangs/ shraddha kA ra warma dad byed go cha/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/
skyang po chos kyi blo gros/ sum ston ye 'bar/ lce zhar ba/ spru

ston 'bar thog /rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs smra seng / lce jo mdo/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ nam mkha' dbang phyug /ngag dbang grags pa rnam rgyal/
bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ 'khrul
zhig blo gros thogs med/ bla ma bde ba can pa mkhyen rab rnam rgyal/ bla ma dge 'dun legs grub/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ gar thig dbyangs sogs la mi 'jigs
pa'i spobs pa dge ba can shAkya'i dge slong rnam rgyal bkra shis/ rdo rje 'chang blo gros dbang phyug /mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/ rnal 'byor blo gros dpal ldan/
rnam grong ye shes rnam rgyal/ 'du shes gsum ldan khyab bdag byams pa phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag wa g-indra la'o/ /des bdag go ! /yang / stod lugs ni/ sangs rgyas/
badzra pA Ni/ pra kA sha tsandra/ rA hu la bha dra/ slob dpon kun snying / pradznyA wa li ta/ pradznyA bo dhi/ dharmma pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ rgya ye shes tshul
khrims/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ rtsa skya dkon mchog grags/ bla ma shAkya 'bum/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston man gong bzhin no/
/ ! dpal mchog rdo rje sems dpa' dbus dkyil rdo rje 'chang gi rigs/ rtsa ba'i lha so gsum/ phyi dkyil 'jig rten pa zhe bzhi bcas pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ ngag
'don zha lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub dang / kun mkhyen bu'i dkyil chog dam tshig chen po'i de kho na nyid 'byung ba nas/ slob ma'i dbang med pa'i lugs rdo
rje slob dpon gyi dbang sogs rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/ de la slob ma bzhi ste/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ swasti pha la/
ye shes rdo rje/ pradznyA siddhi dang bzhi la/ slob dpon kun snying gis zhus/ de la

pradznyA wa li ta/ rab 'byor skyangs/ pradznyA bo dhI/ mukti ko Sha/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ rgya ye tshul/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ rtsa skya ston
grags/ mnyam khad pa chen po/ rtsa skya ston 'bum/ rtsa skya khri brtan/ snur ye rgyal/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che/ dbang
rnon rgyal ba mchog grub/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan can/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ byang gling pa rin chen rgyal po/ gnas brtan bstan
pa bzang po/ byang gling 'jam dbyangs bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bla ma dpal ldan chos bzang / bla ma lha bo pa dam pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin
chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des phrin las rnam rgyal la'o/ /rdo rje 'chang blo gros dbang phyug /bla ma kun dga' bsam grub/ bla chen kun dga' chos 'phel/ sbal ston blo gros
dpal ldan/ byams pa kun dga' chos dbang / gsum ldan phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag ngag ming la'o/ /! chos dbyings gsung dbang 'jam dpal mtshan brjod nas gsungs pa slob
dpon 'jam dpal grags pas rnal 'byor rgyud du bkral ba dkyil 'khor sgo sbrag bzhi lha grangs nyis brgya dang nyi shu rtsa dgu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ slob dpon
ye shes rgya mtsho'i ngag 'don/ kun mkhyen bu'i dkyil chog mkhas pa'i dga' ston nas dbang rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ dznyA na pa/
'jam dpal grags pa/ dpal sbas bzang po/ bram ze ye shes rdo rje| shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pa/ bram ze bzhad pa rdo rje/ padma ka ra dang / shraddha ka ra warma gnyis la/
lo chen rin chen bzang po/ de la lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ rngog ge ser ba/ skyang po dar ma grags/ khri ston kun dga' 'od/ mkhan po chos rin/

bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon ye shes rgya
mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa chen po rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po/ mkhas grub rigs pa'i glog phreng ngam/ 'khrul zhig blo gros thogs med gnyis brtag
/bla ma ma Ni badzra/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims/ des phrin las so/ ! /bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa las kyi sgrib pa
thams cad sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs las gsungs pa bya rgyud rdo rje'i rigs las rdo rje'i rigs kyi gtso bo/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po'i rnal 'byor rgyud kyi cho ga
bsdus pa'i lugs su/ 'chi bdag 'joms pa dang gtso bo 'pho ba'i rigs las lha bcu gsum gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho'i ngag 'don kun mkhyen
bu'i dkyil chog las sgrib rgyun gcod nas/ slob ma'i dbang dngos gzhi/ dbang rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa chen po/ kun dga' bo/ rje kun dga' grol mchog gsan
yig na/ nyi ma gung pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen/ klu sgrub/ ces 'dug pa nges par dgos pa 'dug /klu sgrub/ Arya de ba/ a ba dhU tI pa/ a bhya ka ra gupta/ gser
gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ jo bo a ti sha /'brom ston pa/ po to ba/ sha ra ba/ rgya ye sgom/ grub thob hU~M 'bar/ zhang dge slong / dge slong dkon shes/ bla ma 'khun ston/
rong pa dkon mchog 'bar/ mkhan po dbang rin/ khams pa sa phug pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ chos 'od/ 'phags 'od/ yang na/ 'khun ston nas/ 'phags 'od/ yang na| dkon
yes nas mkhan po 'brom/ g.ya' lung dgon gsar ba/ rin bla/ 'ong chung pa gzhon nu 'od/ grags chen pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ yang na mkhan chen

ye shes rdo rje/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ rje sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ nub pa rig pa 'dzin grags/ bo dong ra lung pa/ shab lung phug pa/ nam
mkha' bsod nams/ nub gog pa/ dge bshes dar gzhon/ mdo stod pa ston pa don yod/ g.yas ru rgya sde ba slob dpon rin rgyal/ bla ma grags chen pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ kun
mkhyen bu ston/ yang na/ sangs rgyas/ dze tA ri/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje/ lo chen rin bzang / rkyang po chos blo/ rkyang po zhang khrid/ gnyal pa rgog ston/ 'khun ston
gzhon/ rong pa dkon mchog 'bar/ mkhan po dbang rin/ shAkya rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA mchog ldan/ 'ong chung pa gzhon nuu 'od/ bla ma grags chen pa/ 'phags
'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen mahA lotstsha ba bu ston/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan can/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ sku zhang mkhyen
rab chos rje/ chu mig kha pa dkon mchog dpal bzang / 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ de la mkhas grub sangs
rgyas tshe dpal dang / chos rje bsod nams dpal 'byor gnyis ka la/ chos rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen blo gros dbang phyug /rnam grong
chos dbang rgya mtsho/ dge slong kun dga' sbyin pa/ mkhan chen bskal bzang dge legs/ rong pa dkon mchog sbyin pa/ mkhan chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag ngag dbang
tshul khrims rgyal mtshan la'o// rtsa ba'i bla ma rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /yang na/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas tshe dpal/ mkhan chen nam mkha' chos ldan/
rtsa ba'i bla ma mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /spyod pa'i rgyud la/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang / padma dang / rdo rje'i rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud
sde gsum las/ dang po ni/

rnam par snang mdzad chen po mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa rnam par sprul pa byin gyis rlob pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyud dang rgyud phyi ma nas gsungs pa/ dkyil 'khor sgo gsum
sbrag lha brgya dang bcu dgu'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho'i dkyil chog la/ kun mkhyen bu'i dkyil chog sngags 'grol mas brgyan pa nas dbang
rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ dze tA ri/ ashokashrI/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ mchims brtson
seng / mchims don ne/ mchims chos seng / mchims blo brtan/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ slob dpon dar ma rgyal mtshan/ byang chen pa bsod nams 'phel/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan
legs blo/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen grags pa gzhon nu/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ dbur stod pa yon tan dpal/ rong pa blo bzang grags pa/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ slob dpon sangga shrI/ slob dpon tshul khrims 'od zer/ slob dpon bsod
nams dpal 'byor/ byang gling rje/ slob dpon rdo rje bzang po/ slob dpon lha bo ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon
po bsod nams mchog ldan/ sngags 'chang kun dga' lhun grub/ bla chen chos grags dar rgyas/ dge legs 'jam dbyangs mgon po/ bslab gsum kun dga' chos 'phel/ nor gling ye shes
rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen shA sa na dha ra/ des bdag wA gindra la'o/ /des bdag go /'jam dbyangs lha lnga de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi 'khor lo bsgyur ba dpa' bo gcig tu
grub pa'i rgyud nas gsungs pa ngo bo bya rgyud la/ cho ga spyod rgyud du bkral ba/ mngon rtogs sa skya paNDi ta/ dkyil chog rje btsun grags

pa'i steng nas dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ mkhas pa rab 'byor bskyangs/ slob dpon kun dga'
snying po/ paNDi ta shes rab bskyangs/ zhi ba'i snying po/ dge mtshan bshes gnyen/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddha kA ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ mnga' ris pa/ brag
stengs pa/ mal lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ 'jam dbyangs sa paNDi ta chen po/ slob dpon mi pham pa/ rgan mo lhas pa/
byang chen pa bsod nams 'phel/ bla ma gzhon tshul ba/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ bla ma bsod nams bzang po/ rje btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal/
bla ma bsod nams mchog ldan/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma urgyan rgyal po/ rje bsod nams rgyal po/ paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des phrin las pa la'o/
/yang / lotstsha chen po/ dbus pa ge ser/ kha'u pa sku mched/ sa skya pa chen po/ yang / mi pham pa/ bla ma khams pa/ rtas te seng rgyal/ bla ma shes rab seng ge rgyal/
bla ma gzhon tshul ba'o/ /yang / rgan mo lhas pa/ rtas te seng rgyal/ nam mkha' bzang po/ lo mchog /blo chen pa/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon po/ bde ba can seng rgyal/ mkhan
chen shes rab rdo rje'o/ /gza' yum lha bcu bzhi khor yug tu rgyal po bzhi sogs yod pa rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i man ngag /mkhan po zhi ba 'tsho nas brgyud pa/
ngo bo bya rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs las brgyad pa gnas gtsang ma'i lha la sogs pa'i rigs yin zhing / cho ga spyod rgyud du bkral ba/ mngon rtogs sa skya paN chen/
dkyil chog rje btsun grags pa'i 'jam dbyangs lha lnga la brten pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ rdo rje

gdan pa/ rdo rje gdan pa don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba chen po rin chen grags/ bla ma sa chen/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paN chen/ chos rgyal 'phags
pa| shar pa sher 'byung / rdo rje 'od zer/ e pa 'jam dbyangs/ bag ston tshul rgyal/ kun mkhyen pa/ bla ma nam mkha' 'od zer/ sgra pa shes rab rin chen/ rje btsun rdo rje
gdan pa chen po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rje btsun tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma urgyan rgyal po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra
shis/ mtho ris yon tan bdun ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa byams pa dge ba'i dbang po/ chos rje phrin las rnam rgyal/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ grwa thang
snyan mkhar slob dpon/ tshe dbang kun dga' chos dar/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bstan dar/ mkhan chen kun dga' dbang rgyal/ byams pa bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag ngag
ming la'o/ /des bdag go /yang / birWa pa/ zhi ba 'tsho/ padma 'byung gnas/ 'khon klu'i dbang po/ rdo rje rin chen/ shes rab yon tan/ yon tan 'byung gnas/ tshul khrims rgyal
po/ rdo rje gtsug tor/ dge skyabs/ dge mthong / 'khon bal po/ shAkya blo gros/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po
sogs so/ ! /rgyud thams cad kyi rtsa ba/ bya ba'i rgyud las dkyil 'khor chen po bkod pa'i le'u las rigs gsum spyi'i dbang / rigs gsum rig gtad gsang ba spyi rgyud la brten
pa/ bya spyod thun mong ba'i cho ga /rje btsun grags pa'i dkyil chog ngo bo la/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa'i gsung mchan gyis ngag 'don phal cher la/ 'jam dbyangs lha lnga
nas cung zad kha bskang ba'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'di'i stod kyi brgyud pa rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog gi gsan yig las rnyed
pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ indra bhU

ti che 'bring chung gsum/ paNDi ta smra ba'i nor bu/ kun snying / rab zhi bshes gnyen/ kha che ye shes rdo rje/ pu hrangs lo chung / sa chen/ grags pa sogs/ kha che ye shes
rdo rje/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod rtse/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paN chen/ de pa ston tshul/ yar klung pa rgyal tsha lung
mangs pa/ lotstsha ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje btsun rdo
rje gdan pa chen po| bla ma yon tan rgya mtsho/ bla ma tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma urgyan rgyal po/ rje bsod nams rgyal po/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ drin
can rtsa ba'i bla ma byams pa dge ba'i dbang po/ des bdag go /! tshe dpag med lha dgu bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi rgyud las/ rigs kyi gtso bo 'phags pa tshe dang ye shes dpag
tu med pa zhes bya ba'i snying po 'chi med rnga sgra'i gzungs nas gsungs pa slob dpon dze tA ri'i man ngag bzhin sngags kyang 'chi med rnga sgra kho na dang / spro lung
pa kun dga' smon lam gyi yi ge nas rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang / bkru byab srung mtha' rten bkra shis rdzas brgyad dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa sa lugs ni/
mgon po tshe dpag /grub thob snying po'i zhabs/ dze tA ri pa/ byang chub bzang po/ ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ sa chen kun
dga' snying po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ lo mchog /lo chen/ rtse mo/ mkhan po bkra shis rin chen/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/
brag thog pa chen po/ rje btsun rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ de gnyis kar

bla chen shAkya kun dga'/ rje dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ chos rje phrin las rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen blo gros dbang phyug /'jam dbyangs
mgon po/ rnam rgyal rgya mtsho/ kun bzang chos 'phel/ kun bzang dbang 'dus/ byams pa kun dga' dbang rgyal/ gsum ldan byams pa phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag ngag ming la'o/
/des bdag go /yang na 'phags pa/ 'dzims pa rin shes/ bla ma blo gros bzang po/ bla ma bsod nams dpal ldan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal lo/ /yang na/ ba ri ba/ mchims brtson
seng / mchims thams cad mkhyen pa| rgya zhang phug pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ cha gan/ grags chen pa/ sa bzang paN chen/ 'tshal min pa/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal lo/
/yang na/ rgya zhang phug pa/ 'jad pa shes rab rin chen/ e pa 'khon ston/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ rgyal ye/ grags pa dpal bzang / snur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ yang
rtse ba rin chen seng ge/ bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ bzad pa rin rgyal/ brag thog pa chen po/ yang / sangs rgyas 'bum/ gzhon nu 'bum/ cha gan/
yang / gzhon nu 'bum/ gsal ba la/ grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ thugs sras rin rnam/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa
chen po'o/ / yang na mchims thams cad mkhyen pa/ dbang phyug mgon po/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma rgyal ba don grub/ rin po che bkra shis dpal/ bla ma dkon mchog rdo
rje/ rin po che don grub dpal/ rngog ston byang chub dpal bzang / thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'o/ /yang na/ dzi nA pA ri mi tA yuH garbha pA dA/ dze tA ri pa/ pu dznyA na/
dhya na pradznyAH padma shrIH rwa ga badzraH ga dza gho ShaH A nanta pA daH bA di rA Ta/ dzi na bha tra/ bA gI shwa raH bi dza kIrti/ shraddha tsA ri/ ratna sA ga raH
ratna ma tiH dI pangka raH rA hu la bha draH dharma shrIH dznyA na

sA ga raH shrI dharma rA dza/ shrI ba na ratnaH mahA sarba dznyAH A nanta bi dza ya/ gu ru bi dza ya ratna/ manydzu gho Sha bo dhindra ra dzA/ de gnyis kar/ mahA gu ru shAkya
A nanta/ dharma swa mi shwa ra dhwa dzaH badzra dha ra shI la mangga la pA' da/ karmA bi dza ya'o/ /yang / mgon po tshe dpag med/ slob dpon snying po'i zhabs/ grub chen
dze tA ri/ slob dpon byang chub bzang po/ slob dpon ting 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ chung ba a mo gha badzra/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen
grags/ brtse chen snying po'i zhabs/ slob dpon rin po che| rje btsun rin po che/ paN chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ bla ma bkra shis 'od/ e pa 'khon
ston thugs rje rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs chen po rin chen rgyal mtshan/ byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ spang khang pa grags pa dpal/ spro lung pa kun dga' smon lam/ rgyal
ba brag phug pa/ de la bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang brag phug pa chung ba blo gros brtan pa gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka nas chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar
chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ khyab bdag kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug /yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rje lha mchog seng ge /rje sangs rgyas seng ge
/thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ chos rje bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po
ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ des phrin las par gnang ba'o/ /yang na/ ngor chen nas/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po| rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug /dkon mchog 'phel man
'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ gu ge paN chen/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra/ yang na ngor chen nas/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ rje dkon
mchog 'phel

man 'dra/ yang na yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel nas/ 'jam dbyangs sa lo/ rje kun dga' dpal ldan/ nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na mus chen nas/ grub chen dkon mchog blo
gros/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo man gong bzhin no/ / yang na lha mchog seng ge nas/ rkyang dur rab 'byams pa dge legs bshes gnyen/ rje shes rab rgyal mtshan man 'dra/
yang na ba ri lo tsA nas/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge /rgya zhang phug pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ gzhon nu 'bum/ bla ma cha gan pa| grags pa dpal man 'dra/ yang na
rgya zhang phug pa nas/ 'jad pa rin chen ye shes/ e pa 'khon ston man 'dra/ yang na grags pa dpal nas/ chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen seng ge /bu ston thams
cad mkhyen pa/ lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan man gong bzhin no/ /yang na gzhon nu 'bum nas/ gsal la ba/ grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od/ kun mkhyen
bu ston man 'dra/ yang na mchims brtson 'grus seng ge nas/ spug thams cad mkhyen pa/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan
seng ge /kun mkhyen bu ston man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dpal ldan seng ge nas/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o/ /! bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha
dgu bya rgyud rdo rje'i rigs las/ rigs kyi gtso bo las kyi sgrib pa thams cad sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs nas gsungs pa jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha'i lugs kyi cho ga
dkon mchog lhun grub pa dang rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhal snga nas kyi yig bca' nas ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du/ dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ yang dag par rdzogs

pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ dznyA na garbha/ dznyA na shAnta/ buddha shAnta/ buddha gu hya/ ku sa li che chung gnyis/ su warNa dwi pa dharma kIrti/ dpal dI paM ka
ra/ go mi sgom chen/ kyi nor dznyA na/ gnyag ldom bu ba/ spug thams cad mkhyen pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bya rin chen 'od/ blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa ye shes
mgon po/ bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ lo tsA ba ma Ni ka shrI dznyA nA/ sa bzang 'phags pa| rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab
kun dbang / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge /thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ rdo rje
'chang mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ bka' 'gyur ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen bka' drin mnyam med 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ des dgyes pa chen pos phrin las pa la'o/
/ yang bco brgyad chos rje/ rtsa ba'i bla ma/ zur rigs kun bdag po chos dbyings rang grol/ thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ pha bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs
grags pa/ mkhan chen ngag dbang bstan 'dzin/ pha bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs grags pas rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho la ma gsan nges pa yin 'dug pas brgyud pa e yod
brtag rgyu/ des bdag go /yang na bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan nas/ rje lha mchog seng ge /sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra/ /yang na dkon mchog 'phel nas/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya
lo tsA ba/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse pa man gong bzhin no| |yang na jo bo chen po nas/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje btsun
sa chen/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ snur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ snur chos 'phags/ gar thig pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan
chen shes rab rdo rje/ thel

chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ thel mkhan po grags rdor ba/ drung byang chub rdo rje/ 'jam dbyangs rin rgyal ba/ mkhan chen zla blo ba/ mkhan chen nyi ma/ mkhan chen kun blo
ba/ paN chen ngo mtshar rgya mtsho/ mar ston sems dpa' chen po/ rdo rje 'chang sngags rams pa dge 'dun bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ brag dgon spyan
snga/ gzhon nu chos dpal bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang 'khon ston dpal 'byor lhun grub/ zur thams cad mkhyen pa chos dbyings rang grol/ thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngag dbang
blo bzang rgya mtsho man 'dra'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ dze tA ri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / jo bo rje man 'dra'o/ ! /rdo rje rnam 'joms dkar
po lha bco lnga'am bcu dgu/ bya rgyud rdo rje'i rigs las/ rdo rje'i rigs kyi bdag po rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs dang / de'i bshad rgyud ri rab chen
po'i rtse mo'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzungs nas gsungs pa/ slob dpon sa wa ri pa'i man ngag rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus kyi yi ge nas dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rigs
brgya'i khyab bdag sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / /ye shes mkha' 'gro'i dbang mo seng gdong ma/ /mchog gi dngos grub brnyes pa'i sa wa ri/ /srid zhi'i gtsug rgyan gsum
la gsol ba 'debs/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug dza wa ri pa'i zhabs/ /de sras de wa purNa ma ti rje/ /'jig rten mig mkhan dpyal lo chen chos bzang mchog /gsung rab mtsho las rin
chen dngos grub thob/ /thar pa'i sa mkhan bzhi la gsol ba 'debs/ /'chad rtsod rtsom la dbang bsgyur dmar ston chos rgyal zhabs/ /bdag med rtogs pa'i shes rab bla mar grags/
/gzhung lugs rgya mtshor mnga' 'byor shes rab 'bum/ /sa gsum snyan pa'i grags pa rdo rjes khyab/ /bstan pa'i bya bar dar ma byang chub che/ /bstan pa'i

rgyal mtshan lnga la gsol ba 'debs/ /gsung rab gangs rir yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge'i rgyal/ /skal bzang sangs rgyas bdun pa rin chen grub/ /de sras thu bo rin chen rnam
rgyal zhabs/ /'chad rtsod rtsom la grags pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /ye shes rgya mtshor rin chen bsod nams 'phel/ /chos rje chos kyi rgyal po chos dpal ba/ /'dus pa'i phyag
'od mkhan chen rin rgyal ba/ /thar pa'i ded dpon drug la gsol ba 'debs/ /bstan 'gro'i gnyen mchog mtshungs med chos rin rje/ /phan bde'i 'byung gnas bsod nams dpal 'byor
can/ /tshogs gnyis rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan bsgreng / /mkhas grub chen po mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang zhabs/ /mchog 'di man la nA lendra'i bla ma legs rdo rje bstan
'gro padmo'i gnyen/ /dngos grub mchog brnyes sku zhang mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang / /rdo rje 'chang dngos sku zhang ngag dbang lhun grub zhabs// bstan pa'i bdag po
rnams la gsol ba 'debs/ /de ltar gsol ba btab pa'i byin brlabs kyis/ /bdag dang phrin las pa mkha' mnyam 'gro ba ma lus pa/ /'chad rtsod rtsom las thub bstan rgyas byed
cing / /phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub myur thob shog /ces pa 'di ni dpal zha lu'i mkhan rin po che rdo rje 'chang dang mi gnyis pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub gang gi
zhal snga nas bskul ba ltar/ phrin las rnam par rgyal bas rdo rje gdan nyi ma gling du bris pa dge legs 'phel/! gtsug tor gdugs dkar lha zhe gnyis kyi dbang dang legs ldan
nag po grong khyer sum brtsegs 'jigs par byed pa ma mo'i tshogs kyis bskor ba'i rjes gnang gnyis karma pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i steng nas thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ dga' rab rdo rje/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ shrI singha / dznyA na ku mA ra/ rma rin chen mchog /ling nams lo tsA ba/ ling nams lo/ rog ston
pa/

sman ston gung pa/ chos brag mkhar pa/ brag dkar dbon po/ yon tan byang chub/ gdugs dkar ba gzhon nu rin chen/ rang byung rdo rje/ rta bkra ba dbang brtson/ yor pa rin chen
dpal/ sog dbon rig ral/ mthong ba don ldan/ gu shri rin chen/ sangs rgyas mnyan pa/ mi bskyod rdo rje/ dkon mchog yan lag /grags pa don grub/ rnam rgyal dpal bzang / rje
ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rtsa ba'i bla ma byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag go /! gtsug tor gdugs dkar lha bcu bdun
gyi steng du sngags 'chang shAkya dpal nyid kyi zhal gzigs ltar rnam 'joms dkar po'i khro bo bcu bsnan nas lha nyer bdun gyi yig bca' sngags 'chang shAkya dpal gyis mdzad
pa'i steng nas dbang rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar mo/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon bsam gtan
bcu pa/ mkhas pa tsandra go mi/ slob dpon gi ra wa ti/ slob dpon rdo rje rnon po/ slob dpon padma lcags kyu/ bram ze rin chen rdo rje/ slob dpon dze tA ri pa/ rdo rje gdan
pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ ldan ma kyu ra a skyabs/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ de la stod lung gad ser ba dang / pho rog mdo
sde dpal gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka la khams pa rgan mo lhas pa byang chub dpal lo/ /bla ma ye shes rin chen/ rje rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma cha rgan pa/ bla ma grags
chen pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam rgyal/ sngags 'chang shAkya dpal ba/ chos rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ chos rje rgyal
mtshan bkra shis/ slob dpon dbang chen rgyal po/ bla ma byang chub bzang po/ mkhan chen rin

chen kun ldan/ rigs 'dzin kun dga' don grub/ rje byams pa kun dga' 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /yang na nye brgyud ni/ bcom ldan 'das gdugs dkar
mo'i lha tshogs/ sngags 'chang shAkya dpal ba/ rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan nas gong bzhin no/ ! /sbyong rgyud nas gsungs pa sa lugs kyi yo gar grags pa thar rtse nam mkha'
dpal bzang gi yig cha nas dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor sgo rkyang rtsa ba'i lha so bdun mgron thabs dang bcas pa/ shAka thub sku'i dkyil 'khor
lha bcu bdun/ tshe dpag med gsung gi dkyil 'khor lha bcu gsum/ phyag na rdo rje thugs kyi dkyil 'khor lha bcu gsum/ 'khor lo sgyur ba yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor lha zhe
brgyad 'jig rten khor yug dang bcas pa/ me ltar 'bar ba phrin las kyi dkyil 'khor lha bcu bdun pa ste 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor drug dang / 'jig rten pa'i dkyil
'khor drug las phyag na rdo rje klu chen brgyad kyis bskor ba/ me ltar 'bar ba lha chen brgyad/ me ltar 'bar ba gza' chen brgyad/ phyag na rdo rje zhi ba la phyogs skyong
bcu sgo ba dang bcas pa/ me ltar 'bar ba la 'jigs byed dgu chung ma dang bcas shing sgo ba bzhi/ phyag na rdo rje zhi ba la rgyal chen bzhi sgo ba bzhi dang bcas pas bskor
ba'i dkyil 'khor rnams kyi so sor dbang rdzogs pa ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla
ba/ bram ze dzi na mi tra/ swasti pha la/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ pradznyA wa li ta/ ye shes rdo rje/ pra hi ta/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ kha che dharma
pha la/ dznyA na shrI/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ gshen rdor seng / rgya gsar ba/ 'brom 'dzin ri pa/

snye mdo ba bsod nams dpal/ gnyal pa chos grags/ bya rin chen 'od/ blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ khyung chos rgyal/ snyer ston thogs rgyugs pa/ shAkya grub bzang / thugs sras
bsod nams bzang po/ chos rje nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ kun dga' legs grub/ kun dga' chos grags/ ngag dbang mchog
legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje sems dpa' byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag go /yang na blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bla ma dpal ldan pa/ ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang / dpal ldan rdo rje/ mgon po dbang phyug /gnyan lo grags pa blo gros la/ buddha singha / pradznyA dhwa dza gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis la paN chen nam
mkha' dpal bzang / des mchog legs rdo rje'o/ /yang na mkhyen rab rje/ 'jam dbyangs chos rje/ rin chen don yod rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams lhun grub/ mchog legs rdo rje man gong
'dra'o/ /gtsug tor dri med lha lnga'i sgo nas mchod rten 'debs pa'i cho ga thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ de'i sngon du| dbang bskur thob dgos pas/ bla
chen grags rin pa dang / zha lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis mdzad pa'i yig bca' nas dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ jo bo rje/ nag tsho
lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba/ phyag sor ba/ bya yul ba/ skar chung byin pa/ gze ba don ye/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon
po/ bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ meg ston grags pa 'od zer/ bla chen grags pa rin chen/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' 'od/ chos rje nam mkha' tshul
khrims/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje btsun rdo ring pa/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang

phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rtsa ba'i bla ma chen po rin chen bzang po/ des bdag phrin las rnam rgyal la'o/ /! 'phags pa 'od
zer dri ma med pa'i dkyil 'khor du dkyil chog bus mdzad pa/ lha btsun rnam rgyal ba'i yi ge'i rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi lhan thabs steng nas dbang thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs/ mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho/ chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan/ lha sras mu khri btsan po/ sad na legs/ lha sras gtsang
ma/ 'od srung / dpal 'khor btsan/ skyid lde nyi ma mgon/ khri bkra shis mgon/ lha bla ma ye shes 'od/ lha btsun byang chub 'od/ pho brang zhi ba 'od/ mnga' bdag 'od lhe/
mnga' bdag rtse lhe/ mnga' ris dgra bcom pa tshul khrims byang chub/ zhu lhan pa shes rab grags/ ra sa chu lhas pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ gro mo che bdud rtsi grags/ sangs
rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon/ bu ston lo tsA ba/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po/ chos rgyal nam mkha'i mtshan can/
bla ma rin chen don grub legs pa/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ byang gling pa rin chen rgyal po/ zha lu pa rin chen bkra
shis/ gnubs sgom sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ zha lu mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub dpal bzang po/
rtsa ba'i bla ma chen po rin chen bzang po/ des bdag phrin las pa la'o/ ! /rigs kyi yum las bsrung ba lnga'i dkyil 'khor du thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal bas mdzad pa'i
dkyil chog la lhan thabs bco brgyad 'jam dbyangs chos rjes mdzad pa'i steng nas rig gtad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na

rdo rje/ dze tA ri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba/ chung ba don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ gnyan ston grags/ gnyan rin grags/ lha sa'i gnas brtan dkon seng /
de'i sras rdog ston bya'u rgyal/ bla ma rgyal tsha lung mang po/ bla chen rong pa shes rab seng ge /'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ chos rje bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras
rin chen rnam rgyal/ yab sras gnyis ka la chos rgyal nam mkha'i mtshan can gyis gsan/ de nas bka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ sku
zhang bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ thar gling 'og pa bsod nams dpal 'byor/ ri phug dbu mdzad rin chen rgya mtsho/ zha lu mkhan chen rin chen
bsod nams mchog grub dpal bzang po/ rtsa ba'i bla ma zha lu'i chen po rin chen bzang po/ des bdag la gnang ba'o/ /yang na byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med
dpal ldan chos bzang / mkhan chen nam mkha' chos ldan/ zha lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ chen po rin chen bzang po/ des bdag la'o// yang na bkra shis rgyal
mtshan/ de la dbang phyug rab brtan gyis tshar brgya rtsa gsan/ de la glang bu chos rje 'jam dbyangs chos skyong dbang phyug /zha lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog
grub dpal bzang po/ rtsa ba'i bla ma chen po rin chen bzang po/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na mkhyen rab chos rje nas/ zha lu mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul khrims/ gung pa mgon
po rgyal mtshan/ dge slong ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /dbang phyug rab brtan man gong 'dra'o/ /yang na bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa nas/ mkhan chen
shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma a mo gha/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rin chen/ chos lung mkhan chen don yod rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen kun dga'

blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ rje bshes gnyen bkra shis/ dge slong ngag dbang rnam rgyal man 'dra'o/ /'di dag gi brgyud yig rgyas pa ni/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen
pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyi gsan yig chen por gsal/ ! bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi bdag po cho ga zhib mo nas gsungs pa'i kun mkhyen bu'i dkyil chog yid bzhin gyi
nor bu dang / byang chub phrin las pas mdzad pa'i lhan thabs kyi steng nas/ don zhags lha mangs rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs/
bla ma e ra pa ti/ lho phyogs kyi rigs ngan gyi rnal 'byor pa/ rdo rje gdan pa don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ des bla ma lho pa/ mkhan po thang pa/ snub ban dang gsum
la gnang / de gsum gyis grub thob nyi phug pa la/ de nas grang po lung pa grags pa tshul khrims/ slob dpon tshul khrims grags/ mkhan po kun ra ba rgyal mtshan mgon/ slob
dpon bsod nams sgrub/ slob dpon kun dga' tshul khrims/ chos lung mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/ kun mkhyen bu rin po che/ slob dpon gzhon nu 'bum/ sku mtshams pa rin chen
rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bsod nams 'phel/ shar chen ye shes rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bkra shis
rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan chos bzang / rdo rje 'chang rin chen rgya mtsho/ zha lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ de gnyis ka la/ dkar po slob dpon klu sgrub
rgyal mtshan/ zha lu chen po rin chen bzang po| rje mang thos rgya mtsho/ bla ma chos grags dar rgyas/ dge slong kun dga' sbyin pa/ chos rje kun bzang chos 'phel/ bla
ma kun dga' chos dbang / mkhan chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag shI la dhwa dza la'o/ /yang na kun bzang chos 'phel yan gong bzhin/ des kun dga' dbang rgyal/ byams
pa bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des

bdag ngag ming la'o/ /des bdag phrin las rnam rgyal la dgyes bzhin du gnang ba'o/ /yang na bla ma lho pa yan gong bzhin la/ grub thob nyi phug pa/ grang po lung pa grags tshul/
dkon mchog grags/ 'jam dpal rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen klu sgrub/ bka' bzhi pa dkon mchog gzhon nu/ bu ston rin po che man gong ltar ro/ /yang na thugs rje chen po/ dge
bsnyen zhi ba'i go cha/ shI la A ka ra/ bai ro tsa na rakShi ta/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje man chad gong dang 'dra/ yang na thugs rje chen po/ dha byang chub sems dpa'/
byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ grub thob nyi phug pa man gong bzhin no/ /! bstan pa phyi dar la/ ma rtogs pa dang / log rtog dri mas thub pa'i ring lugs sbags pa bsal ba'i
ched du lha bla ma khu dbon gyi lhag bsam gyi mthu dang sbyor byung gi brtson pa la brten/ mgon po snang ba mtha' yas kyi ye shes kyi sgyu 'phrul dpal mar me mdzad gdan
drangs/ gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir rgyal ba'i bstan pa ches cher 'phel bar mdzad/ chos zab pa las kyang ches zab pa bka' gdams glegs bam rin po che'i skor gsungs pa las
lung gi skor dang / dbang gnyis las dang po lung cha shas tsam thob pa rgya gzhung gi sdebs su yod/ de yang rgya chen spyod rgyud/ zab mo lta rgyud/ nyams len byin brlabs
kyi brgyud pa gsum ni yongs grags ltar yin la/ brgyud gsum chu bo gcig tu 'dres pa bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang dkyil chog lag len gsal byed nges don rgya mtsho
rje kun dga' legs grub kyis mdzad pa nas dbang legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ jo bo rje dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na/ 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ gsang phu ba rngog
legs pa'i shes rab/ mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ phu chung ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ ka ma ba 'brom rin chen rgyal

mtshan/ zhang dar ma rgyal mtshan/ 'brom byang chub bzang po/ ston pa nam mkha' rin chen/ 'brom gzhon nu blo gros/ snar thang mkhan chen nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ gling kha rin
chen byang chub/ sga lung rigs kyi bdag po'i dpal/ sga lung byang chub dpal/ nyug pa bsod nams 'od zer/ sangs rgyas bzang po/ bya bral bsod nams bzang po/ bla ma dpal ldan
pa/ stag tshang chos 'khor nam mkha' 'od zer/ dga' gdong pa ye shes tshul khrims/ nub chos lung mkhan chen ratna A ka ra shAnti/ gnyug la paN chen ngag dbang grags pa/
lo pa spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/ rje kun dga' legs grub/ rje kun dga' chos grags/ bco brgyad pa mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ bla
ma dam pa mkhyen rab ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag phrin las rnam rgyal la'o/ /thob yig bum pa bzang po las 'bras bu'i theg pa gsang sngags gsar ma'i sngags sdom thob
pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// //(ca)! gsang sngags snga 'gyur dang / phyis gter kha nas byung ba'i dbang / byin brlabs bcas pa'i skor las/ sgrub pa bka' brgyad kyi yang dag
lha dgu thugs kyi dkyil 'khor mi bskyod pa'i rigs kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ dkyil chog hU~M mdzad zhal lung steng nas/ sa skya pa sngags 'chang chen po kun dga'
rin chen gyi yi ge nas dngos sta 'brel ba'i dbang rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun bzang dpal chen he ru kaH /rdo rje sems dpa' dga' rab rdo rje dang / /'jam
dpal bshes gnyen ro

langs bde ba dang / /buddha gu hya slob dpon hU~M kA ra/ /padma thod 'phreng bi ma la mi tra/ / shI la manydzu rdo rje bdud 'joms dang / /gnyags chen dznyA na 'khon ston klu
dbang srung / / rdo rje rin chen yon tan 'byung gnas dang / /tshul khrims rgyal po gtsug tor shes rab dang / /'khon rigs dge skyabs 'khon ston bal po dang / /'khon rigs
dge mthong shAkya blo gros zhabs/ /shes rab tshul khrims dkon mchog rgyal po dang / /brtse ba chen po slob dpon rin po che/ /rje btsun grags pa chos rje paNDi ta/ /chos
rgyal 'phags pa 'od ldan kha'u pa/ /bu lung kun rdor lo chen mchog ldan pa/ /dga' ldan kun bsod gan pa rin rgyal rje/ /bsod nams rgyal mtshan shes rab rdo rje dang / /chos
dpal shes rab seng ge rgyal mtshan dang / /klu pa bsod dar dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od/ / nam mkha' blo gros chag lo gsum pa dang / /sa lo 'jam rdor rje btsun kun dga' legs/
/mkhyen brtse'i zhabs dang dbang phyug rab brtan dpal/ /sa chen kun bsod 'jam dpal rdo rje zhabs/ /mkhas btsun bzang po phrin las rnam rgyal ba/ /rdo rje 'chang dngos
blo gros dbang phyug zhabs/ /chos dbang rgya mtsho bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal/ /bka' drin mnyam med ye shes rnam rgyal zhabs/ /gang dang dbyer med phun tshogs chos 'phel
des/ /shI la dhwa dza bdag la legs par bstsal/ /'di la brgyud srol mang du mchis so/ /rmi ltas bzang po dang bcas bdag gis thob/ /de yang / rdo rje gdan 'dir slob ma nyer
lnga re'i bgrangs kyis bcad pa'i dbang tshar bcu gnyis gnang ba'i dus su'o/ /slob dpon rin po ches grags pa'i zhabs la 'dud de/ dam bca' ba'o/ ! /rdo rje phur pa lha
khra bka' ma lugs stod las byang chub sgrub pa dang / smad las drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang / rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan
gyi mngon rtogs gsum dang dkyil chog nas dngos sta

'brel ba'i lugs phyag len chu babs su byung ba thams cad mthun par srung skud skyes pa'i dpung pa g.yon du 'dogs pa sogs dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kun tu
bzang po/ rdo rje gzhon nu/ karma he ru ka /rigs kyi rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon u pa rA dza/ pra wa ha ti/ dha na saM skr-i ta/ padma saM bha ba/ sna rnam rdo rje bdud
'joms/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ shes rab yon tan/ yon tan 'byung gnas/ tshul khrims rgyal po| rdo rje gtsug tor/ dge skyabs/ dge mthong / 'khon ston bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo
gros/ 'khon shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ bla ma sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs
sa paNDi ta chen po/ chos rgyal 'phags pa rin po che/ 'od ldan dpal/ go lung pa kun dga' rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gan pa ba rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa chen po/ thams cad mkhyen
pa chen po rdo rje gdan pa/ chos rje phun tshogs gling pa/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ bla chen ye shes mtshan can/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ bka' 'gyur
ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ de gnyis kar/ rdo rje 'chang blo gros dbang phyug /mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/ bla chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/

kun bsod do/ /gzhan yang / rdo rje sems dpa'/ padma 'byung gnas/

rdo rje bdud 'joms/ kham sgom mchog gi legs pa/ shes rab tshul khrims/ mchog gi sems dpa'/ dkon mchog rgyal po/ mtha' bzhi ston pa/ rdo rje drag po/ rdo rje thod phreng / rol
pa'i rdo rjai/ glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ /'phags pa'o/ /yang / glo bo lo tsAs bal po'i paNDi ta ratna shrI la'ang zhus so/ ! /sa lugs phur pa lha khra snyan
brgyud dam zhal ngo nang brgyud lugs/ rdul tshon kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs par lan gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po thog ma'i mgon/ / longs
sku rdo rje sems dpa' rigs kun bdag /sprul sku padma 'byung gnas rdo rje'i sku// snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i nor 'dzin klu'i dbang po/ /chos kyis 'phongs sel rdo rje rin
chen dang / /gnyis snang 'khrul spangs shes rab yon tan gter/ /nyes rdul dri med tshul khrims rgyal po'i zhabs/ mchog tu mi 'gyur rdo rje gtsug tor gtsug tor shes rab kyang
zer mtshan/ /gdams pa'i mdzod mang 'dzin pa'i dge skyabs dang / /chos kun de nyid gzigs pa'i dge mthong dpal/ /brag la phur pa'i zhal gzigs bal po'i mtshan/ / snga 'gyur

po'i zhabs/ /'ja' lus mngon gyur slob dpon bsod nams rtse/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal/ /gzhan la brtse ba'i thugs mnga' dpal chen 'od/ /bstan pa'i bdag
po kun dga' rgyal mtshan zhabs/ /'dren mchog dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal/ /'gro mgon 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan bsgrengs/ /'khrul med gdams pa'i mdzod 'dzin 'od
ldan dpal/ /bdud dpung tshar gcod kun dga' rdo rje 'dzin/ /'jig rten mig mkhan legs pa'i blo gros can/ /

blo gros rje/ /'jam dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug /sku 'bring kun dga' dbang rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang dngos kun dga' bsod nams gter/ /'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug /dkon

gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub byams pa bzang po/ mkhas grub blo gros mchog ldan/ rdo rje 'chang dngos sgyi chu sha lung nas byams pa bsod nams phun tshogs/ des bdag go !
/tshe dbang mda' 'phel ma lha bcu bdun gyi rdul tshon dkyil 'khor du slob dpon chen po padma'i gsung rab la phyag len gyi mchan bu yod pa'i steng nas dbang thob pa'i brgyud

du gsol/ /skye 'chi gnyis spangs mchog gi dngos grub brnyes/ /slob dpon padma'i zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /mi shigs= rtag brtan= mkha' 'gros dngos su byin brlabs bde stong

'dzin mdo sngags rgya mtsho'i

ma/ rdo rje dbyangs can ma dkar mo phyag gnyis ma/ khro gnyer can gyi sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /rtog pa nas gsungs pa'i ku ru kulle phyag bzhi ma'i sgrub thabs drug
la gcig/ kye rdor nas gsungs pa'i ku ru kulle'i sgrub thabs bzhi la gcig /ku ru kulle phyag drug ma'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /ku ru kulle dmar mo phyag brgyad ma gtso
'khor bcu gsum ma/ ku ru kulle dkar mo phyag gnyis ma/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba stong phrag bcu drug pa'i

rgyud nas gsungs pa'i ku ru kulle dkar po phyag drug ma/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal phyag brgyad ma/ ngan 'gro sbyong ba'i gtsug tor rnam rgyal lha dgu'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig
/bcom ldan 'das ma gdugs dkar mo can/ rdo rje tsartsi ka /rnam snang sgyu 'phrul dra ba nas srung ba lnga'i gtso rkyang rnams las so 'brang gi sgrub thabs gsum la gcig
/rma bya chen mo/ stong chen rab 'joms/ gsang sngags rjes 'dzin/ bsil ba'i tshal/ gzungs grwa lnga'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /phyir bzlog ma chen mo/ rgyal mtshan rtse
mo'i dpung rgyan/ rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan zhal bzhi phyag bzhi ma/ gzhan gyis mi thub ma/ rdo rje gandha ri'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /bsrung ba lnga'i cho ga
la rjes gnang gcig zer/ rdo rje lcags sgrog phyag drug pa/ rdo rje lcags sgrog phyag brgyad ma'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /nor rgyun ma lha lnga/ rdo rje gur nas gsungs
pa'i nor rgyun ma'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /rdo rje phag mo lha lnga/ phag dkar shes rab gsal byed/ rdo rje phag mo'i rtog pa don thams cad grub pa lha lnga/ rnam snang
sgyu 'phrul dra ba nas gsungs pa slob dpon thogs med kyi zhal gzigs byams pa mgon po'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /dzambha la nag po/ dzambha la ser po lha dgu/ gang ba
bzang po'i rgyud nas dzambha la 'khor bcas kyi sgrub thabs rgyas pa gnyis la gcig /dzambha la phyag drug pa/ rdo rje gur nas gsungs pa'i dzambha la ser po'i sgrub thabs
gnyis la gcig /rta mgrin dmar po zhal gsum phyag brgyad pa/ rtog pa bdun pa nas rta mgrin zhal gnyis phyag gnyis/ rta mgrin gtso 'khor lnga pa/ rta mgrin dmar po zhal bzhi
phyag brgyad pa/ khro bo 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba zhal bzhi phyag brgyad pa/ rdo rje me nyi 'bar ba zhal bzhi phyag brgyad pa/ gshed dmar yab yum/ gshin rje
mthar

byed sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /gdong drug gi rgyud rgyas pa las gshin rje dgra nag zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /gshin rje gdong drug phyag drug zhabs
drug pa/ bgegs mthar byed/ rdo rje hU~M mdzad/ stobs po che/ kye gshin rje gshed nag po'i rgyud las byung zhes jo nang pa gsung bas brtag rdor rtsa bshad nas gsungs pa'i
kye rdor/ dgyes pa rdo rje phyag gnyis yum bcas/ rdo rje bdag med ma gnyis la gcig / phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed kyi sgrub thabs gnyis la gcig /rdo rje gur nas
gsungs pa'i gur mgon/ mgon po sngon 'byung nas gsungs pa'i mgon po phyag bzhi pa ste de rnams kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor
ma/ slob dpon a bha ya ka ra/ shu bhaM ka ra/ pu dza ti/ ratna rakShi ta/ go taM shrI/ kIrti paN chen/ lo tsA ba grags rgyal/ rgyal mtshan rin chen/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/
gzhon nu seng ge /mgon po 'bum/ dpal ldan pa/ ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun bzang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge /dkon mchog 'phel/
dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin/ rdo rje 'chang bco brgyad pa byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub dpal bzang po/ des
bdag phrin las rnam par rgyal ba la'o/ /yang na lo tsA ba grags rgyal/ rong pa sher seng / bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen sher rdor/ rin chen 'phel/ kun dga'
bsod nams/ mkhan chen byang seng / chos kyi 'od zer/ bsod nams bzang po/ nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab rje/ shAkya don lum par 'khrungs grub/ 'jam dbyangs stong ra

des bdag go /yang na/ dkon mchog 'phel gyi rjes su/ sa lo tsA ba/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin/ rtsa ba'i bla ma/
des bdag go /sgrub thabs rgya rgyam gnyis kar bla ma gong ma rnams rgya gzhung gi steng nas rjes gnang re dang gzhung de'i lung re gnang zhing / phyis su/ bla ma la la'i
snyan du rgya gzhung gi ming tsam yang ma gsan/ gsan yang ma gzigs/ gzigs kyang lung ma thob/ thob kyang 'chad mi mdzad/ slob mas kyang nyan mi nus pa mang / da lta'i phyag
len la bod gzhung gi lung re rjes gnang re mdzad pa dang mi mdzad pa gnyis kar zhus/ brgyud srol shin tu mang ba ganggA'i chu rgyun na bzhugs/ rgya bod kyi gzhung thos
pa'i lung brgyud 'og na'o/ ! /phyag 'tshal nyer gcig sgrol ma'i rjes gnang jo bo rje'i rgya gzhung la sa lugs kyi sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i lung gsum gyi chings kyis rjes
gnang thob/ de yang mnyam med jo bo chen po bod du 'byon pa'i dus phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi zhal 'don dang bcas rdo rje gdan du bskor ba mdzad pa'i tshe rje btsun sgrol
ma dngos su zhal mjal te bod du bzhud cig par lung bstan/ 'di la yi dam byas na bar chad mi 'byung zhes shlau ka re dang las tshogs re sbyar nas gnang ba'i sgrol ma nyer
gcig la thog mar thams cad kyi gzhi seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol 'di zur bka' na yod pa ma'o/ /dgra bgegs log 'dren gyi 'tshe ba zhi bar byed pa myur zhing dpa' ba'i sgrol
ma 1/ nad gdon bgegs sdig pa mi mthun pa'i phyogs zhi bar byed pa ston ka'i zla ltar dkar ba'i sgrol ma 2/ tshe dang longs spyod 'phel bar byed pa gser mdog can gyi sgrol
ma 3/ tshe lo bcu yang brgyar 'phel bar byed pa tshe 'phel sgrol ma ser mo 4/ bud med sogs dmigs bya dbang du bya ba hU~M sgra sgrog pa'i sgrol ma 5/ dbang

phyug lha dang sa bdag sogs dbang chen thams cad bran du byas nas 'byung po 'dul ba 'jig rten gsum rgyal sgrol ma 6/ rig sngags kyi gnod pa dang rbod zor bzlog par byed pa
gzhan gyi 'phrul 'khor 'joms pa'i sgrol ma 7/ bdud dang dgra bgegs sgrol bar byed pa bdud dgra rnam par 'joms pa'i sgrol ma 8/ 'di phyi'i gnod pa dang 'jigs pa thams cad
bsrung ba phyag rgya dkon mchog gsum mtshon sgrol ma 9/ bdud dang mu stegs log lta can rnams dbang du bsdus nas bar gcod 'dul bar byed pa 'jig rten dbang mdzad sgrol ma 10/
mkho dgu'i 'byor pa thams cad spel te phongs pa las rnam par skyob pa 'gugs shing phongs pa sel ba'i sgrol ma 11/ bkra shis dang dngos grub thams cad 'grub par byed pa

pas bar gcod sel bar byed pa sgrol ma khro gnyer can ma 14/ sdig sgrib bag chags mi gtsang ba rnams zhi bar byed pa sgrol ma zhi ba chen mo 15/ gzhan gyi rig sngags kyi

gsum g.yo'i sgrol ma 17/ klu'i dug dang gnod pa thams cad las grol bar byed pa dug rnams rab tu zhi byed sgrol ma 18/ 'thab rtsod dang btson du tshud pa dang rmi lam ngan
pa sogs duHkha las thar bar byed pa sdug bsngal thams cad sel ba'i sgrol ma 19/ rims nad dang yams thams cad zhi bar byed pa rims nad sel ba'i sgrol ma 20/ zhi rgyas dbang
