'phel/ chos rje phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen kun dga' dbang rgyal/ byams pa kun dga' brtson 'grus/ des gnyis ka la gsan/ mkhan po bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag
shI la dhwa dza la'o/ /bkra shis gnyis kyis bdag go /yang na/ 'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ chos rje bla ma/ yang na 'phags pa/ paNDi
ta shes rab rdo rje/ 'phags rgyal/ bla ma bzang po pa/ chos rje bla ma/ yang na sa paN/ bla ma khang gsar ba/ blo chen seng ge dpal/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen
sher rdor/ yang na 'phags pa/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /chos rje bla ma nas gong bzhin no/ /yang / gsan yig 'ga' las/ 'phags pa/ tshogs sgom/ la
ru ba/ nyan chen pa/ sa bzang pa/ theg chen pa/ brag thog pa zhes kyang 'dug go /de brag thog pa'i gsan yig na/ mi snang bas dpyad do| |yang na thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje
gdan pa/ sngags 'chang yon tan rgya mtsho/ bla

ma urgyan rgyal po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /yang na 'phags pa yan gong bzhin las/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug
pa/ bla ma dam pa/ yang na 'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal/ bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen sher rdor/ chos sgo ba/ brag thog pa/ rdo rje gdan
pa/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /dbang phyug rab brtan/ bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog
ldan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis zhabs/ des bdag go /yang na bla ma dam pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs pa/ A nanda pa/ mu srad pa/ shes rab rin chen/ tshar chen
man gong bzhin no/ /yang na/ dpal shAkya kun dga'/ bla chen ye shes dbang po/ slob dpon rdo rje blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /yang na rdo
rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma rnam rgyal bkra shis/ slob dpon rdo rje blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang
tshul khrims bkra shis zhabs/ des bdag go / ! gur mgon lha brgyad ma bla ma dam pa'i lha gsum ma'i yig bca' la brten pa'i rjes gnang dang / lha bcu gnyis ma'i rjes gnang
de gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa yan lha gsum ma dang 'dra ba las/ zhang dkon dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa| chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla ma bsod nams 'od zer/ bla
ma dpal ldan legs dbang / brag thog pa chen po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma rnam
rgyal bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis dang / paN

chen kun dga' bkra shis/ de gnyis ka la bdag gis zhus so// ! //dpal sa skya pa'i zhal ngo nang brgyud kyi gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ a mes kun dga'
bsod nams zhal snga nas la thob/ gur mgon lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang la slob ma'i spyi bor mgon po dang brgyud pa'i bla ma bskyed zhu bstim pa tshar chen
chos kyi rgyal po'i yig bca' nas bla ma paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan gyi drung du thob pa'i brgyud pa slar bri/ gur mgon khro bcu'i rjes gnang dang / srung 'khor rdo
rje brag rdzong ma'i nyams khrid zab mo sbyar byang bar kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma dang / mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi yi ge nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang /
bram ze mchog sred nas/ 'phags pa rin po che'i bar gur mgon lha gsum ma'i rjes gnang brgyud pa bzhin/ 'phags pa rin po che/ rga a gnyan dam pa kun dga' grags/ bdag nyid
chen po bzang po dpal/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ bla ma nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen blo gros
rgyal mtshan/ kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ de gnyis kar/ tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ bla ma
bsod nams chos 'phel/ de gnyis kar/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub pa'i bka' drin gyis phrin las pa la dgyes bzhin du gnang
ba'o/ ! /yang / mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che yan gur lha gsum ma bzhin la/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bdag nyid chen po bzang
po dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal/ rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge

ba rgyal mtshan/ rje sangs rgyas mchog pa/ skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje bkra shis seng ge |tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs dbang
phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'dzin pa kun dga' bkra shis/ des bdag go /yang na rje bzang po rgyal mtshan nas/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal 'byor gyi bar/ sgyi chu lugs kyi
kye rdor man ngag lugs bzhin no/ /sa chen kun dga' bsod nams kyi zhabs drung du yang thob/ ga ya dha ra'i mgon rkyang ngam lam 'bras kyi mgon po lha gcig gi rjes gnang thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ nag po pa/ Da ma ru pa/ a ba dhU tI/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ se mkhar chung pa/ zhang dgon pa
ba chos 'bar/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paNDi ta| 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis la mkhyen rab chos
rje rin chen mchog grub/ ngag dbang chos grags/ kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rtsa ba'i bla ma bco brgyad chos rje byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/
des bdag go /yang / theg chen chos rje/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ mthu stobs dbang phyug kun dga' bkra shis/ chos rje karma
phrin las/ chos rje rgya do ba nam mkha' dpal bzang / /kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ stong ra ba 'jam dbyangs kun legs/ byams pa kun dga' chos grags/ mkhyen rab bstan
'dzin bzang po/ rtsa ba'i bla ma byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des phrin las rnam rgyal la'o//

! zhabs drung a mes kun dga' bsod nams la gur mgon bse 'bag gi rjes gnang bya ba lha gcig pa thob/ ba ri lo tsA dang / yar klung lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gnyis nas brgyud
pa'i gur lha gcig gi rjes gnang lan gnyis re brgya rtsa dang rgya mtsho'i skabs su thob/ dpal ldan tshul khrims kyi yig bca' nas/ dam can pu tra khyad par ba'i rjes
gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa rin po che yan gur lha gsum bzhin la/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ bla ma bsod nams 'od zer/ brag nag pa dpal
ldan legs dbang / brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs
dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'dzin pa bsod nams mchog ldan/ des phrin no/ ! /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa'i skor la/ brgyud pa'i srol mi 'dra ba gnyis/
dpal ldan sa skya pa yab sras la bka' babs pa/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta nas brgyud pa dang / ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma nas brgyud pa'o/ /rdo rje nag po chen po zhal bzhi phyag
bzhi/ rtsa zhal mthing nag g.yas dkar g.yon dmar/ steng zhal dud kha gtso 'khor lnga/ 'khor dam can rgya mtsho'i dmag tshogs kyis bskor ba sgrub dus kyi mgon po'i rjes
gnang lan gsum thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon klu sgrub/ ba liM ta pa/ sangs rgyas ye zhes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dpal sde/ bi ma la gupta/ rin
chen rdo rje/ ratna kIrti/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ kha'u pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che rtse mo/
rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs sa paNDi ta/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ brag phug pa

bsod nams dpal ba/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bzhi thog pa kun dga' rin chen/ gcung grags pa blo gros/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen
pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ yongs 'dzin shAkya'i mtshan can/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims
bkra shis/ des bdag go /yang na yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ bla chen ye shes dbang po/ slob dpon rdo rje blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims zhabs/ chos rje phrin las
rnam rgyal/ sgyi chu blo gros dbang phyug /bla ma kun dga' chos 'phel/ chos rje phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ byams pa kun dga' dbang rgyal/ bka' drin mtshungs med bstan 'dzin
tshul khrims/ des bdag shI la dhwa dza la'o/ / yang 'du shes gsum ldan bla chen phun tshogs chos 'phel la yang zhus/ des bdag go /yang na 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal
mtshan/ paN chen kun dga' bkra shis dpal bzang po/ des bdag go /yang na 'phags pa yan gong dang 'dra ba las/ zhang dkon dpal/ brag phug pa'o/ /yang / bla ma dam pa/ sngags
'chang gzungs pa/ chos rje dge bzang pa| chos rje A nanda ma ti/ rgya bka' bzhi ba dpal ldan grags pa/ rngog bsod nams don grub/ rje thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'o/
/la lar 'di 'dug ste gsan yig na khyung zhal can gyi sgrub skor dang zhal gyi rjes gnang yi ge /rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i lung gsan brgyud yin 'dra 'dug go /yang
/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ bla ma shAkya kun dga'o/ /yang / nye brgyud ltar na/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang chen po/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro
ma/ bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa/ sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa/ sa paNDi ta kun
dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'gro mgon

chos rgyal 'phags pa nas gong bzhin no/ /yang na/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa| sngags 'chang yon tan rgya mtsho/ bla ma uu rgyan rgyal po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal
po/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis zhabs/ des bdag go /'di la chos rje bla ma'i kye rdor mngon rtogs gsham ltar las/ zhal gyi thad bcos nas gtso 'khor lnga'i rjes
gnang gcig dang / brag thog pa'i mngon rtogs ltar dam can rgya mtsho sogs kyis bskor ba rjes gnang gnyis gnang byung yang / gsan yig rgya mtshor dbye ba mi 'dug pas/ gang
ltar byas kyang 'dra zhing rgyas bsdus tsam du mngon no/ ! /yang / sgrub dus kyi mgon po gong bzhin la gri snying 'khor lo dang bcas pa gtod pa'i rjes gnang yi ge tshar
chen dang / sngags 'chang tshe bkras pa'i yin nam snyam pa'i yig bca'i lung dang / yi ge dngos gzhi yar klung seng rgyal gyi yin/ rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ yongs 'dzin
shAkya kun dga'/ bla chen ye shes dbang po/ slob dpon rdo rje blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims zhabs/ des bdag go ! /gnyan mgon zhal nor sgrub gtso 'khor dgu pa'i
rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mahA de ba/ paNDi ta shrI siM ha/ a tsa ra mnyan chen dpal dbyangs/ rgya gar kA ma rU pa/ gnyan lo dar ma grags/ glang
ban ga rod pa/ rtogs ldan mtsho dkar ba/ spyan snga bsod nams grags pa/ chos rje bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ mkhas grub dge ba rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs
med shes rab zla ba/ rje btsun rdo rings pa chen po/ grub mchog sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma rnam rgyal
bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag go /bsnyen dus kyi mgon po zhal khra can rtsa zhal mthing nag g.yas

g.yon gnyis ljang nag /steng zhal dud kha gtso 'khor lnga'i rjes gnang / sa chen a mes drung la yang thob/ ! rje dbang phyug rab brtan gyi yig bca' nas/ bram nag shan pa drug
bskor gyi rjes gnang dang de'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon klu sgrub/ rgya gar gyi grub thob ka ma ru pa/ zhang mdo sde dpal/ rje 'jam skya
nam mkha' dpal ldan/ bla ma grang mo che pa/ rje re ta zla ba/ grub pa'i dbang phyug thang stong rgyal po/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa 'jigs
med dpa' bo/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog /bstan 'dzin nyi zla bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba
mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ 'khor lo'i mgon po chos dbyings rang grol/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ zha lu mkhan chen gnyis kar bdag gis thob bo/ /! gnyan mgon bram
gzugs mngags gtad chig brgyud kyi rjes gnang lan gsum thob pa'i tshar chen gyi yi ge /bla ma lha dbang phrin las kyi lhan thabs kyi lung bcas/ brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa
rin po che yan sgrub dus mgon po'i brgyud pa bzhin la/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bzang po dpal/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bzhi thog
pa kun rin/ bzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ grwa thang pa shes rab zla ba/ rje rdo rings pa chen po/ tshar chen/ rje tshe dbang bkra
shis/ rje rnam rgyal bkra shis/ bla ma lha dbang phrin las/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims zhabs/ des bdag go /zhal gyi dgra bo 'ching byed zhags pa nag po zhes pa shog bu gnyis
pa zhig gi lung yang thob/ ! dpal ye shes kyi mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i rgyud mgon po mngon par 'byung ba dang / bde

mchog gi bshad rgyud thun mong ba mgon po dngos grub 'byung ba dkyil 'khor bdun gsungs pa las/ lha bcu gsum ma'i rjes gnang mtshal lugs zhang g.yu brag pa nas brgyud pa rjes
gnang dus/ sku'i gtor ma/ gsung bdud rtsi/ thugs rdo rje/ phyag mtshan bzhi/ sngags lung / bka' gtad dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'khor lo sdom
pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ klu sgrub snying po/ Arya de ba/ dus zhabs pa che chung gnyis/ rdo rje gdan pa/ tsa mi sangs rgyas grags/ a bhya ka ra/ rje btsun rgwa lo/ zhang
g.yu brag pa/ shAkya ye shes/ btsan khang pa/ sangs rgyas gzhon nu/ gser khang steng pa/ grags pa bzang po/ shAkya bsod nams/ chos bzang pa/ dpal ldan rgyal mtshan/ grags
pa bsod nams/ dge 'dun dpal ldan/ spyan snga grags pa rgya mtsho/ spyan snga ngag dbang rgya mtsho/ spyan snga bsod nams rab brtan/ spyan snga skal ldan rgya mtsho/ zur
chos dbyings rang grol/ rdo rje brag rig 'dzin padma phrin las/ rnam sras gling paNDi ta chen po dkon mchog chos grags/ des bdag go /! myur mdzad ye shes mgon po phyag
drug pa'i chos skor la/ rgyud ni bu ston rin po ches the tshom gyi gzhir bzhag kyang / bla ma phal cher tshad mar 'dzin pa'i mgon po gsang ba dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud
kyi le'u bcu bzhi par/ mgon po kun gyi gnas 'di ni/ /zhal gcig pa la phyag drug pa/ /dang po gri gug thod khrag 'dzin/ / spyan gsum mthing nag rngam pa yi/ /g.yas g.yon
bar pa phreng ba dang / /Da ma ru ni 'dzin cing brdung / /mtha' ma gnyis kyis kha TwAM dang / /sdigs mdzub zhags pas 'ching bar mdzad/ /ces dang / shangs pa rnams kyi rang
skad la rgyud tshad ldan rta mgrin gyis gsungs pa'i le'u brgyad pa'i le'u gnyis par/ nag po zhal gcig phyag drug pa//

gri gug bgrang phreng Da ma ru/ /thod pa mdung dang zhags pa bsnams/ /zhes dang / rwa 'gyur mgon po gsang ba mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud le'u lnga bcu pa las/ zhal gsum phyag
drug pa lha mo bzhi'i 'khor dang bcas zur tsam bstan no/ /mkhas grub khyung po gdub bu pas ko sa la bikSha'i dur khrod du/ rje btsun mai tri pa la gser srang bdun phul
nas zhus/ mkhas grub khyung po 'phan yul 'jog po'i ri la sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe grub chen rA hu las chos sgo skyel gyi tshul du gnang ba'i skor rnams bsdoms pas mnyam
med ri bo dga' ldan pa la mgon po'i bka' bcu gsum du grags pa/ rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa dge 'dun bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas/ gtor dbang bar gcod kun
sel/ rjes gnang bar gcod kun sel/ dbang bzhi byin brlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba/ bla mgon dbyer med kyi skor la zhi ba grib sel/ rgyas pa bla ma mgon po dbyer med/ mkha' 'gro
dbang sdud dang gnad dbab gcig tu byas pa/ gsang sgrub mgon po mchin kha/ mgon po dbang rgyal/ sa ra ha'i mgon po khrag 'thung ste bcu'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen sha wa ri'i dbang phyug /rje btsun mai tri pa chen po/ shangs pa lo tsA ba khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog
lcog pa rin chen brtson 'grus/ skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge / gnyan ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ chos rje sangs rgyas ston pa/ mkhas grub shangs ston chen po/ mus chen
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / sngags 'chang rdo rje gzhon nu/ mnyam med nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang / mtshungs med bzang po rgyal mtshan/ grub chen
ngag dbang blo gros/ mar ston tshul khrims rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa dge 'dun bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya

mtsho/ brag dgon spyan snga gzhon nu chos dpal bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pa dpal 'byor lhun grub/ rigs kun bdag po chos dbyings rang grol/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen
po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ pha bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ mkhyen rab mnga' bdag ngag dbang bstan 'dzin/ des bdag go /yang na mkhas grub rje nas/ 'brom
rtse lha btsun rin chen rgya mtsho blo gros/ paN chen ngo mtshar rgya mtsho/ mar ston tshul khrims rin chen man 'dra/ yang na 'brom rtse chos rje nas/ grub chen ngag dbang
blo gros/ mar ston sems dpa' chen po man 'dra/ yang na mkhas grub shangs ston pa nas/ mkhas btsun rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal/ 'jag pa blo gros dpal/ grub
chen ngag dbang blo gros man 'dra/ yang na byams pa dpal nas/ kun dga' dpal/ ngag dbang blo gros man 'dra/ yang na mkhas grub rje nas/ rong ston blo bzang grags pa/ thon
pa mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho/ paN chen bsod nams grags pa/ gu ge ba nyi ma bzang po/ khri rin po che rgyal khang rtse pa dpal 'byor rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang pha
bong kha pa man 'dra/ yang / rjes gnang bar chad kun sel gyi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal nas/ snar thang lo tsA ba don grub bzang po/ rgyal ba tsong kha
pa chen po/ shar pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ byang gling pa grags pa rin chen/ snar thang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen ye shes rtse mo/ rje chos grags pa/ mar ston
sems dpa' chen po/ rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa man gong ltar ro/ /yang na rgyal ba tsong kha pa chen po nas/ rgyal sras bzang skyong ba/ rin po che chos dpal ba/ chos rje
blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa man 'dra/ yang na 'jag chen byams pa dpal nas/ kun mkhyen

shes rab dpal bzang / sems dpa' chen po tshul khrims dpal bzang / mkhas grub rin chen bshes gnyen/ chos rje legs pa'i blo gros/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang sngags
ram pa man 'dra/ dbang bzhi byin brlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba bar gcod kun sel gyi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ mkhas grub shangs ston nas rje rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag chen byams
pa dpal/ rje bsod nams blo gros/ bla ma kun dga' bzang po/ dran mchog don yod rgyal mtshan/ yab chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho/
chos rje rin po che thub bstan pa/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal man gong bzhin no/ /yang na mtshungs med bzang po rgyal mtshan nas/ rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang
/ mkhas grub rje nas/ ba so chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ gnas rnying pa kun dga' bde legs/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho man gong ltar ro/ /yang na mtshungs med bzang
po rgyal mtshan nas/ 'jam dbyangs dge 'dun 'phel/ rgyud pa bkra shis 'phags/ rgyud chen brtson 'grus 'phags/ sras khang sngags ram pa bzang po rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang
pha bong kha pa man 'dra/ mgon po rgyan can/ tshe bdag /lha bzhi'i dril sgrub/ mgon dkar bzhi'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang slob dpon dha na saMskr-i
ta/ grub chen rA hu la gupta/ mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor man brgyud tshul gong mtha' dag dang 'dra/ sa ra ha'i mgon po khrag 'thung gi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo
rje 'chang / sa ra ha 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon chen po padma thod phreng / grub chen sha ba ri pa/ mnga' bdag mai tri pa| khyung po rnal 'byor man gong ma rnams dang
'dra/ bcu gsum pa'i grangs su mi the ba'i shangs lugs gtsang ma/ phyag 'tshal drug chas gos sindhu ra rnams kyi rjes

gnang mgon po snying zhugs thun mong ba'i rjes gnang tshar chen dang mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags pa'i yi ge'i steng nas dbang bzhi byin brlabs su bskur ba shin tu rgyas
pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhas grub rgyal mtshan 'bum yan gong ltar la/ khyung po tshul khrims mgon/ bya btang ri khrod ras chen/ sprul sku sangs rgyas rdo rje/ pha rgod
thar pa dpal bzang / drin can sangs rgyas rnam rgyal/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ gnyan ston rnam sprul gzhon nu blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab
bdag zha lu pa chen po/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ pha bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ mkhyen rab mnga' bdag ngag dbang bstan 'dzin/
des bdag go /yang na tshar chen nas/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rje dbang phyug rab brtan man 'dra/ yang na tshar chen nas/ bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub
rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ khyab bdag dbang rab man 'dra/ ! ye shes mgon po phyag drug pa'i chos skor po ti kha longs las chos skor 'ga' zhig
gi lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs ni/ rgyud le'u brgyad ma rang byin gyis brlabs pa nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs dpal sha ba ri pas mdzad pa/ rang byin gyis brlabs pa
nag po chen po 'di nyid nyams su len tshul dpal phyag drug pa'i mngon rtogs rgyas pa'i yi ge |'bring gi yi ge /bsdus pa'i yi ge /be bum nag po'i skor zer ro/ ! /be bum
dkar po'i skor nas/ nag po chen po sgrub pa'i thabs/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med du sgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba bla ma mgon po dbyer med kyi byin brlabs zhes pa nas/ slob ma
rjes gzung rdzogs sau'i mtha' can/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med la/ /grib thog dam tshig 'gal gyur na/ /zhes pa nas/ gsol 'debs bya'i mtha' can/ bla ma

mgon po dbyer med du/ nas/ gnad dbab lags sau'i mtha' can/ bla ma ye shes mgon po yis/ /nas/ dbang du bsdu zhing gnad la dbab pa rdzogs so'i mtha' can/ ye shes mgon po phyag
drug pa'i rten bca' ba la gsum/ nas/ bka' rgya btab nas gshegs gso'i mtha' can/ dgra bgegs gang dmigs brlag mdzad pa'i/ nas/ mang po la med do'i mtha' can/ rdo rje 'chang
dang dbyer med pa'i/ nas/ bla ma mgon po dbyer med du rtogs par bya'o/ /gnad gsum gyi gdams pa la/ nas/ shangs ston gyis yi ger bkod pa'o'i mtha' can/ na mo mahA kA lA
ya/ thun mong min pa'i rten bca' ba la/ nas/ gzhan su la'ang mi 'dug go'i mtha' can/ mgon po phyar dar ni/ nas/ ri gong dpal gyi dgon par yi ger bkod do'i mtha' can/ rab
gnas la sngon du bsnyen pa gal che gsung / nas/ me tog gi zhal gdams/ rab gnas kyi zhal gdams/ dus kyi zhal gdams/ gu gul gyi zhal gdams/ nyung dkar gyi zhal gdams/ ye shes
pa dngos su bzhugs pa'i zhal gdams/ zhabs bsdam gyi zhal gdams/ mgon po yid bzhin nor bu'i rjes gnang gi yig rnying / bla ma dkon mchog DA ki'i zhabs la btud ces pa/
nas/ chig brgyud dag las ma spel cig mtha' can/ bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /las kha tshar ba 'di la/ nas/ gnam stong gi bar du bya'o'i mtha' can/ mgon po gzi
ldan dbang phyug gi zhal shes gsum pa kha yangs shing / nas/ dpe su la'ang mi ston no'i mtha' can/ dbang sdud kyi 'khor lo/ nas/ athi-i'i mtha' can/ na mo dang po byin gyis
brlabs pa'i/ nas/ hU~M gri ba ma yin no'i mtha' can/ mgon po'i sbyin sreg bum pa bca' thabs/ lha mo'i phyag bzhi'i gnad yig snying gi yang thig /'di'i rten bca' ba/ lha
mo phyag gnyis ma'i srog

sgrub che chung mnga' bdag mai tri pa'i lugs/ sbags sgrub dug lta bu'i man ngag gi lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs rlung stod du 'tshang ba phan pa'i mtha' can/ 'khor lo'i sgo nas dgra
legs bsad pa/ mnan pa'i 'khor lo bca' thabs/ bsrung ba'i 'khor lo bya ba/ zla ba nyi ma nag po la/ nas/ man ngag kyang 'di yin no'i mtha' can/ mgon po la brten nas rmi
lam ngan pa bzlog thabs/ lam srungs dang bsrung skud/ ngag gnon 'grol thabs/ mtshon bzlog /gsha' bzlog /ser bsrung / spos sbyor byin brlabs mgon po'i las sbyor drug gi gdams
pa/ slob ma'i snying gar chos kyi 'khor lo/ nas/ ma mthong bar byed kyi mtha' can/ mgon po'i bskang mdos bya ba'i lag len/ sri'u gso ba'i man ngag /gtor ma'i rnam bshad/
be bum nag po'i gtor chen skor bsnyen sgrub las gsum/ shog ril dmar nag rnams kyi lung brgyud ni/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang yan rjes gnang brgyud pa dang 'dra/
mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang nas/ ba so chos kyi rgyal mtshan sbyin pa dpal/ se ra rje btsun pa/ gang po slob dpon nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon ratna bha tra/ slob
dpon sangs rgyas bsam grub/ slob dpon dpal 'byor dar rgyas/ pha bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang bstan 'dzin/ des bdag go /! dpal sa skya pa'i
gser chos bcu gsum las dmar chen skor gsum du grags pa'i/ kye rdor rtsa bshad nas gsungs pa ku ru kulle'i rjes gnang dga' ldan pa kun bsod dang sgrub thabs rje btsun grags
pa'i yi ge nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ nag po pa/ Da ma ru pa/ a ba dhU tI/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ bla ma se mkhar
chung ba/ zhang dgon pa ba/ bla ma sa skya

pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ 'jam dbyangs sa paN/ 'u yug pa rig pa'i seng ge /nyi thog pa kun smon/ bla ma yon tan dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla
ma gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen sher rdor/ chos sgo ba/ brag thog pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ snyug la paN chen/ de gnyis ka la mkhas grub rigs
pa'i glog phreng / yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ rje btsun dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis dang / paN chen kun dga' bkra shis dang /

'dra'o/ ! /lung thob pa'i chos skor la rgyal po lhan skyes rol pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ zhi ba 'tsho'i man ngag dA na shI la'i 'gyur/ snying po

gar mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros/ rje dbang rab man 'dra/ yang na tshar chen nas/ rin po che bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya
mtsho/ skyed tshal mkhan chen thar pa bzang po/ khyab bdag zha lu pa/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang dbang rab nas/ zha lu pa dge 'dun dpal bzang / mkhan chen
zha lu pa/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'ba' ra ba nas/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge /'jam dbyangs chos kyi rgyal po/ shangs dkar ba rin chen rgyal mtshan/ pha rgod bsod nams bzang
po/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po man 'dra/ yang na 'ba' ra ba nas/ chos rje bde legs lha do rtogs ldan yang zer rin chen/ gnas rnying pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen
gangs khrod pa kun dga' dpal bzang / chos rje rin chen rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje man 'dra/ yang na rdo rings rin po che/ rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga'
legs pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ yab sras gnyis ka la 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses gsan pa man gong ltar ro/ /yang na sgo rum pa nas/

de dbon sgo rum pa ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen rab rje nas/ sku zhang bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal
mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rab man 'dra/ yang na rje sgo rum pa dang tshar chen gnyis la mnga' ris ru thog pa nam mkha' gzi brjid/ de nas kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse man
'dra/ yang na ras chung pa nas/ gsum pa seng ge dpal/ lo ston kun dga' dar/ gling ras pa padma rdo rje nas rim par brgyud de/ rtses dang sman tshul khang pa slob dpon bkra
shis dar/ dgung lo brgya lhag pa bzhes pa yin/ rje btsun rdo rings pa man 'dra/ yang na 'ba' ra ba nas/ g.yag sde kha rag ri pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ 'bri gung lo tsA
ba nam mkha' grags/ mnyam med sangs rgyas dpal bzang / rje nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rje rin chen rnam rgyal/ paN chen gzhung lugs 'bum phrag brgya pa dngos grub dpal chos
'khor lhun po'i mkhan po 'bar/ bla chen nam mkha' gzi brjid man 'dra/ yang na rje btsun rdo rings pa chen po nas/ rje kun dga' grol mchog /'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man
'dra/ yang na lha do rtogs ldan bde legs rin chen nas/ dbu ma chos shes bzang po/ dge slong dpal mgon pa/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ ngor pa lha mchog seng ge |grol mchog
man 'dra/ yang na 'ba' ra ba nas/ gnyan ras nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ karma pa chos grags rgya mtsho/ tre bo chos kyi rgya mtsho/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog man 'dra/
yang na rje btsun grol mchog nas/ gser mdog can gyi mkhan po 'bum ram pa dge 'dun nyi ma/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ yang na kun mkhyen gangs khrod
pa kun dga' dpal yan gong ltar la/ dbu ma pa dpal ldan bzang po/ drin can dpal ldan mgon po/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ bdag

chen 'jam dpal dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug /kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ yang na 'ba' ra ba nas/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma/
rong ston shes bya kun rig /lha 'bri shes rab rdo rje/ mi nyag grags pa rdo rje/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug man gong ltar ro/ /yang na 'ba' ra ba nas/ grub chen rin chen
bzang po/ lung mang po chos grags dpal bzang / mkhan chen zla ba blo gros/ skyes mchog tshangs pa rgyal mtshan/ mal gro grub chen blo gros dpal ldan/ chos lung mkhan
chen nam mkha' lhun grub rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na 'ba' ra ba nas/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge /klong mkhar ba kun dga' shes rab/
mon rtse pa kun dga' dpal/ gri byang chub sdings pa kun dga' dpal/ de'i gdan sa pa byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun grub man gong bzhin no/ /yang na ras chung pa
nas/ gru ston rdo rje 'od/ chag dgra bcom/ chag lo chos rje dpal/ bla brang steng pa nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun dpal chen bzang po/ rgyal sras blo bzang dpal 'byor/
chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang na ras chung pa nas/ sum pa seng ge dpal/ lo ston kun dga' dar/ gling ras padma rdo rje/ grum ston
dar ma shes rab/ sprag phug pa shes rab dpal/ grub thob legs ldan 'od/ rje btsun dpal chen bzang po man 'dra/ yang na gangs khrod pa kun dga' dpal bzang nas/ mus chen
dpal ldan mgon po/ chos rje nyi zla seng ge /yol mo sprul sku shAkya bzang po/ bkra bzang sngags 'chang chos skyong bsod nams/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na
chag lo gsum pa nas/ thugs sras don yod dpal/ rin po che bshes gnyen bkra shis/ grub brnyes sdom brtson chos

kyi 'byung gnas/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang nye brgyud ni tshe dpag med/ rje btsun mi la ras pa/ chos rje ye shes dpal bzang man gong bzhin
no/ /yang na ras chung pa nas/ mnga' ris pa byang chub rdo rje/ bla ma kun dga' shes rab/ bzang yul ba rin chen ldan/ 'gro mgon ston pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu grub/ bla
ma byang chub shes rab/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ 'khrul zhig grags pa tshul khrims/ mnyam med rgyal ba bzang po/ rje bkra shis ye shes/ bla ma tshul khrims
dbang phyug /rje bshes gnyen bkra shis/ bla ma ngag dbang rnam rgyal man 'dra/ yang na ras chung pa dgung lo 82nas/ 'gos ri khrod dbang phyug 88nas/ gnyan sgom rgyal ba
96seng ge /byang chub gling 92pa/ slob dpon dge'u 86pa| mngon pa dbang phyug brtson 99'grus/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa/ mkhan chen mchims/ mkhas grub gzhon nu grub man
'dra/ yang na 'gos ri khrod dbang phyug nas/ yar lungs kyi gnyag dmar po/ rje btsun yon tan bzang po/ rig pa 'dzin pa gnyos a seng / gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa nas/ bla ma rnal rgyal dpal bzang / mkhan chen dpal 'byor ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo
rje gdan pa/ phun tshogs gling pa rnam rgyal rin chen/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na/ gan pa rin rgyal nas/
mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ brag thog pa man 'dra/ yang na ras chung pa nas/ mnga' ris pa byang chub rdo rje/ grub thob rgyal tsha mgon po/ bla ma bzang yul ba/ sangs
rgyas ston pa/ rin chen seng ge /slob dpon lha gzhon/ mkhan chen dang ma ba/ mkhan chen shes rab

rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa man 'dra/ yang na/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa nas/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ bla ma shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs
dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ nyi gling tshul khrims bkra shis/ khyab bdag zha lu ba/ de gnyis kas bdag go /yang dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra
shis dang / rdo rje 'dzin pa paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan de gnyis kar mang du zhus so/ /yang na nyi ma gling pa nas/ rdo rje 'chang mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ de
la kun mkhyen chos dbyings rang grol dang khyab bdag zha lu ba gnyis dang / bdag gis zhus so/ /yang na 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang yan gong ltar la/ de nas skyes
mchog A nanda pa/ chos rje dpal 'byor rgyal mtshan/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ chos rje yon tan mchog/ thams cad
mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ gyi re lha btsun lha dbang rgya mtsho/ de gnyis ka la 'khon ston rdo rje 'chang dpal 'byor lhun grub/ de nas zur thams cad mkhyen pa man
'dra'o/ /yang na thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho nas/ paN chen bsod nams grags pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho man gong ltar ro/ /yang na thams cad
mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho nas/ brag dgon spyan snga gzhon nu chos dpal bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pa man 'dra/ yang na gangs can pa kun dga' dpal bzang yan
gong ltar la/ de nas 'brong rtse lha btsun rin chen rgya mtsho blo gros/ grub chen ngag dbang blo gros/ mar ston tshul khrims rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa dge
'dun bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na yang dgon pa thugs kyi rdo rje nas/ mkhan po rin chen rdo rje/ sprul sku bsod nams

rin chen/ byang sems khyung dkar ba chen po/ ri pa dkon mchog 'byung gnas/ bla ma smon lam snying po/ mkhas btsun chos dpal mgon po/ ri khrod pa seng ge dpal bzang / paN chen
ngo mtshar rgya mtsho/ mar ston sems dpa' chen po tshul khrims rin chen man gong ltar ro/ /yang na 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang nas/ chos rje shes rab dpal/ bla
ma tshul khrims dpal bzang / rje rin chen bshes gnyen/ mtshungs med sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ rje skyabs mchog dpal/ rje blo bzang don grub/ dben sa bla ma sangs rgyas ye shes/
mkhan rin po che blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho nas gong bzhin no/ /yang na rje bsod nams rgya mtsho nas/ khri rin po che rgyal khang
rtsi pa/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog chos 'phel/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ yang na dbu ma pa dpal ldan bzang po nas/ rje dpal ldan mgon po/ rje sangs rgyas
rin chen/ ngor chen lha mchog seng ge /rje sangs rgyas seng ge /thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ khyab bdag
zha lu mkhan chen/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ yang na thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ de dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ khyab bdag zha lu pa/ rgyal dbang blo bzang
rgya mtsho/ yang na thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ zha lu pa chen po/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya
mtsho/ yang na rje sangs rgyas seng ge nas/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis man 'dra/ yang na rje sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA ba| ngor chen dkon
mchog lhun grub/ rje dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen man 'dra/ yang na mi nyag grags pa rdo rje yan sngar ltar la/ de nas 'jam dbyangs sa lo

man 'dra/ yang na sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje nas/ sku khang bsod nams mchog grub/ sku zhang rin chen bkra shis bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ri sbug dbu mdzad rin chen rgya mtsho/
khyab bdag zha lu pa/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ brgyud lugs gcig la/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku thugs rje chen po/ sprul sku padma 'byung gnas/ ma
cig grub pa'i rgyal mo man 'dra/ yang dpal sa skya pa mthu stobs dbang phyug dang a mes drung dang 'jam pa'i rdo rje dang / bsam sdings pa dang / lcags thang pa rnams la
yang zhus so/ /'di spyan snga zhwa dmar ba thams cad mkhyen pa chos kyi grags pa dang rdo rje 'chang sngags ram pa dge 'dun bkra shis kyi gsan yig na 'dug cing / lha lcam
man da ra ba rgya gar du dus ring mo zhig nas ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mor grags zhes gsung ngo / ! /'jam dpal gshin rje gshed dgra nag rgyud nas gsungs pa'i dbyangs can
ma phyi sgrub zhal gsum phyag drug dang / gsang sgrub sa la'i pho nya'i dbyangs can ma lha mo dmar mo'i rjes gnang gnyis las/ gsang sgrub shin tu zab pa thob pa'i brgyud
pa sa lugs ni/ sgra dbyangs lha mo/ des yang nas yang du rjes su bzung ba'i paNDi ta bikSha pA ra ma/ paNDi ta shrI ta thA ga ta rakShi ta| kha che'i paNDi ta dza ya ka
/paNDi ta bha ska ra de wa/ 'od byed 'byung gnas yin zhing thar rtse shar pa gnyis kyi gsan yig na 'di dang dza ya ka go ldog tu snang la 'dir rdo rje gdan pa dang mkhyen
brtse'i gsan yig btsan par byas te bkod/ kha che'i paNDi ta shAkya shrI| paNDi ta dA na shI la/ 'jam mgon sa skya paN chen/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug
/mkhas pa yon tan khri/ drin can seng ge bzang po/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rgyal mchog /bsam gtan gling pa nam mkha'
bsod nams/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ paN chen phyogs

las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ rje btsun bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ brag dgon spyan snga gzhon nu chos dpal bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang pha
bong kha pa dpal 'byor lhun grub/ zur thams cad mkhyen pa chos dbyings rang grol/ /rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ mkhan chen dge ba'i dbang po/ yi ge rnying ma
nas sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang lo rgyus/ brgyud yig bcas pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa rjes gnang dang 'dra'o/ /des bdag go|yang na bsam gtan gling pa/ nam mkha' bsod nams
nas/ lha ri ba dpal ldan rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga shAkya rgyal mtshan/ tshar chen man 'dra/ yang na yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan nas/ klu pa mkhan po bsod nams dar/
bla ma dmar ston pa/ rin po che kun bzang rtse pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ rig 'dzin tshe dbang
bkra shis/ tshar chen man gong dang 'dra/! dpal dur khrod bdag po yab yum ni 'khor lo bde mchog dang / sgos rgyud dpal he ru ka dngos grub chen po gsang ba snying gi 'khor
lo'i rgyud rgya gar lho phyogs ko sa lar 'khrungs pa rnal 'byor dbang phyug bai ro tsa nas bsgyur ba dang / des mdzad pa'i gzhung nas gsungs pa/ dpal sa skya pa'i gsang
ba'i chos skyong 'di nyid kyi rjes gnang dang chos skor gyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma| padma badzra/ shrI badzra rA hu la/ sgeg
pa'i rdo rje/ dznyA na siddhi/ dpal dam tshig rdo rje/ 'chi med blo gros bzang po/ bai ro tsa na/ khams pa rga lo/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun
grags pa/ bla chen yar sgom/ bla ma rgyal tsha/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen

bsod nams rgyal mchog /brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje btsun rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ kun mkhyen shAkya kun dga'/ rje dbang phyug
rgyal mtshan/ nyi gling tshul khrims bkra shis/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ dge slong kun dga' sbyin pa/ bla ma kun dga' chos 'phel dang blo gros dpal ldan gnyis su gsan slar
brtag dgos/ rong pa dkon mchog sbyin pa/ byams pa phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag shI la dhwa dza la'o/ /rdo rje 'chang paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag go ! /phur
bsrungs dkar mo nyi zla stong gi phreng ba can dang / bdud rgyal thod phreng can gyi rjes gnang gnyis sngags 'chang kun dga' zla ba'i yi ge nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
'phags pa yan phur pa'i dbang brgyud dang 'dra ba las/ lo mchog /bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /kun spangs chos grags dpal/ ma ti paN chen/ bla ma dam pa/ byang seng pa/ theg
chen chos rje kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ mkhas grub rnal rgyal rin chen/
yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga' la/ rje btsun ye shes dbang po dang / dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis kar/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /yang / rdo
rje gzhon nu/ slob dpon padma/ 'khon klu'i dbang po/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen nas/ lo mchog gi bar/ phur pa'i dbang brgyud gong ma bzhin/ de nas dpal ldan seng ge nas sngar
ltar ro/ ! /bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' gcig gi rjes gnang nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'jigs byed/ sgo rum pa chen po/ tshar chen/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse/ byams
pa rab brtan/ rje dbang rab/ rje bka' 'gyur ba/ des bdag go ! /las gshin nag po'i rjes gnang rwa lo'i yig cha nas lan gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal gshin rje gshed/
ye shes kyi

mkha' 'gro ma/ ku ma ra tsandra/ nA ga bo dhi/ li la badzra/ dznyA na kirti/ m-i nyag ston sgom/ lo sgom zhig po/ zhang bsod nams rin chen/ thang stod pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/
bla ma rdo rje bzang po/ bla ma Arya de ba/ chos rje kun blo ba/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa chen po/ rje btsun rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ 'jam dbyangs byang
chub dbang rgyal/ bla ma shAkya kun dga'/ rje dbang phyug mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis dang / paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan gnyis ka la/ chos rje phrin
las rnam rgyal/ sgyi chu blo gros dbang phyug /mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/ dge legs rnam rgyal tshul khrims/ chos rje dkon mchog sbyin pa/ dge slong bstan 'dzin
shes rab la yang gsan/ byams pa bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag ngag ming la'o/ / ! 'dun legs ma las/ gsang ba spyi rgyud legs par grub pa dang / /dpung bzang gis zhus
bsam gtan phyi ma sogs/ /bya rgyud rigs gsum spyi dang bye brag gi /rgyud sde rnams la ring du 'dris par byas/ /zhes pa ltar/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bor rtogs
pa'i bcom ldan 'das sman gyi bla bde bar gshegs pa brgyad mtho brtsegs su bzhugs pa'i rjes gnang nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ mgon po 'jam dbyangs/ mkhan
chen bo dhi satwa/ chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan/ sad na legs mjing yon/ mnga' bdag khri ral/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje/ mnga' bdag 'od srung / mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan/
khri skyi lde nyi ma mgon/ mnga' bdag bkra shis lde/ lha bla ma ye shes 'od/ mnga' bdag lha lde/ mnga' bdag 'od lde/ mnga' bdag rtse lde/ mnga' ris dgra bcom/ dge bshes
zhu ldan shes rab grags/ ra sa chu las pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan gro bo che/ sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ gnyag snying po rgyal mtshan/ spro lung pa kun
smon/ spang sgang pa grags pa dpal/ mkhan

chen bsod nams grags pa/ mkhan chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal ba phyag na/ mkhan chen kun dga' blo gros/ mkhan chen tshul
khrims dpal 'byor/ chos lung shar gling pa 'khrul zhig kun bzang mthu stobs dpal 'bar/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab
bdag bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rab 'byams pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /! de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi
bdag po'am 'khor los bsgyur ba 'jam dbyangs dmar ser a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang sa skya paNDi ta dang sa lo kun dga' bsod nams dang / rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra
shis rnams kyi yig cha nas lan mang du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po 'jam dpal dbyangs/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba
rin chen grags/ 'jam dbyangs rnam 'phrul sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs sa paNDi ta chen
po/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ bla chen rong pa/ sras a ka ra siddhi/ chos rje brag kha ba grags pa seng ge |chos rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje btsun rdo rje gdan pa chen po kun dga' rnam rgyal/ snyug la paN chen
ngag dbang grags pa dpal bzang / brag thog pa gsum pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i ba dan/ dpal mkhyen rtse gsum pa 'jam dbyangs tshe dbang kun mkhyen/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug

rgyal mtshan la/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis dang / mahA paNDi ta shrI mAn shI la/ de gnyis kar bdag gis thob bo/ /yang / khri chen kun dga' bsod nams dang / khri
chen kun dga' bkra shis dang / rtse gdong zhabs drung 'jam dbyangs bsod nams bstan 'dzin rnams la thob pas des na sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud phal cher brgyud pa'o// rje bka'
'gyur bar yang thob/ ! dpal sa skya pa'i gser chos shin tu zab pa 'jam dpal nag po'i rjes gnang dang / yig cha sa skya paNDi ta'i sgrub thabs las tshogs rjes gnang bcas
lan mang du thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ bla ma sa chen/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs sa paN/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/
zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma ye shes dpal/ bla ma blo bzang dkar mo/ dkon mchog thugs rje/ gra ston shes rab dpal ldan/ rje btsun rdo rje gdan pa
kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po/ slob dpon chen po chos mchog /mdo khams pa yon tan rgya mtsho/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs tshe dbang kun mkhyen/
rje I shwa ra dhwa dza/ badzra dha ra shI la mangga la/ rje karma bi dza/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ bla ma ngag dbang o rgyan/ kun dga' don gsal/ mkhan po bskal bzang
dge legs/ byams pa kun dga' bstan dar/ gsum ldan kun dga' dbang rgyal/ mkhan chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag wA gindra la'o/ /des bdag go ! /gang blo ma'i rgya
gzhung la brten nas 'jam dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po'i rjes su gnang ba bya rgyud rang skad kyi phyag len ji lta ba bzhin dang / rtsa ba rgya gzhung gang blo ma/ de la
brten pa'i rjes gnang gi yi ge tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa rnams thob pa las rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs/ paN chen dhi ra pA la/ rngog lo
tsA ba blo ldan shes rab/ khyung

rin chen grags/ rgya dmar ba byang chub grags/ phywa pa chos kyi seng ge /gtsang nag pa thugs brtson 'grus seng ge rje seng ge /dan 'bag pa dar ma seng ge /gnyal zhig 'jam

bkra shis rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams legs 'byung / sa lo thams cad mkhyen kun dga' bsod
nams pa/ rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ bka' 'gyur ba chen po 'jam mgon bsod nams
mchog ldan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ de la lan gnyis thob/ yang na/ gnyal zhig 'jam dpal rdo rje/ zad pa dar tshul/ dge bshes gra thang pa/ bla ma dam pa
bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge nas sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa gong bzhin la/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje sangs rgyas seng ge /rje blo gros
chos 'phags/ kun dga' lung rigs/ rje sbyin pa grags pa/ sa chen kun dga' bsod nams la yang zhus so/ /gang blo ma'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ sgo rum pa nas/ tshar chen/ rje
mkhyen rtse/ rje dbang rab/ bka' 'gyur ba/ nyi gling rje tshul khrims zhabs/ des bdag go /slob dpon chen po dze tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal ba'i bzhed srol 'jam dpal dkar
po kha che paN chen gyi thugs dam bzhi'i nang tshan gyi ya gyal du brtsi ba'i rjes gnang / kha che paN chen shAkya shrI'i phyag len ltar khro phu lo tsA snubs byams pa'i

nor bu gling pa chung ba/ paNDi ta 'byung gnas sbas pa/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ grags pa gzhon nu/ mkhan chen bsod grags/
bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ lo chen skyabs mchog dpal/ nam mkha' 'od zer/ bcom ldan grags 'phel ba/ stag tshang lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ gnas brtan 'od 'phro
ba/ 'jam dbyangs sku skye shes rab rin chen/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab

brgyud lugs gcig ni/ kha che paN chen yan gong ltar la/ de nas khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal/ mkhan po dbang phyug grags/ rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ mkhan chen
dang ma ba/ rin po che shes rab grags/ lung pa dkon mchog rdo rje/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ byang sems 'phags pa blo 'phel/ spyan snga tshul
khrims dar/ lo pa spyan snga bsod nams lha'i dbang po/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan/ gur rdzong chos 'byor dpal bzang / rigs 'dzin chen po gzhon nu don
grub/ drin can bla ma 'jam dbyangs chos dbyings rang grol/ thams cad mkhyen gzigs ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal

bkra shis/ spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang man 'gre/ yang / rjes gnang gi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ ngor

chen nas/ gu ge paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams legs 'byung / sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang
na spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan nas/ rin po che bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ zur chen gzhon nu don grub man 'dra/ yang na tshar chen nas/

po| 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra/ yang na gu ge paN chen nas/ glo bo mkhan chen legs 'byung / sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/

phyug /lo mchog /bla ma kun bsod/ bla ma tshul rgyal/ rje chos grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rin chen/ ri lung sbug thugs rje dpal/ rje bshes gnyen bkra shis man 'dra'o/
! /rje btsun tsong kha pa chen po blo bzang grags pa'i zhabs la/ skyid shod dga' ba gdong du/ bla ma dbu ma pa dang / grub chen dpa' bo rdo rje gnyis kyis lo tsA ba'i
tshul du bsgyur nas byung ba'i 'jam dbyangs chos bskor du grags pa'i rjes gnang thob pa la/ dang po dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes gnang thugs kar dhIHdhIHdrug gis bskor ba/

rgyas rigs lnga sogs la/ mdun bskyed dang bla ma'i lha rnams kyi thugs ka nas sngags 'phros lus kyi lha so sor thim pa'i bzlas lung brgya rtsa/ gsum pa 'jam dbyangs gsang

ka'i hrIHla/ hrIHgu gu la thim pas dbang bzhi pa/ de ltar nang sgrub gsang sgrub gnyis kar Da ru 'khrol/ bum pa'i dbang thob/ lus kyi dri ma dag /sprul sku thob pa'i rten 'brel
mngon du byas sogs/ lnga pa/ ! rdo rje phag mo khros pa khros ma nag mo/ sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor chos 'byung nyis brtsegs/ mdun bskyed bla ma slob ma gsum gar pho brang

des bdag la bka' drin du bstsal to/ /! khro bo'i rgyal po mi g.yo ba dkar po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi pho nya'i rjes gnang mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa nas thob
pa'i shin tu nye brgyud ni/ khro bo'i dbang po mi g.yo ba/ kun mkhyen g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla mas mi g.yo ba'i sgrub pa mdzad pa'i zhag bdun thog zhal dkar nang du
mi g.yo ba'i sku mtheb sor tsam pa mang po byung ba bgegs kyi sprul par mkhyen nas/ lhag med gsol bas thul zhing khro bo'i dbang po zhal gzigs pa'i lo rgyus snang ngo /

brgyud pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa/ phyag na rdo rje/ grub chen dze tA ri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen
grags/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog
dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ ri khrod pa blo brtan/ chos rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan
rdo rje/ grub chen bsod nams seng ge /rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse dbang phyug /khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ gnas gsar
rdo rje 'chang mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag go ! /'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs kyi yi ge dang / gong ma'i phyag len ltar/ sangs rgyas klu dbang
gi rgyal po/ gtso 'khor lnga pa'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas klu dbang gi rgyal po/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ jo bo a ti sha/

'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ bshes gnyen po to ba/ dge bshes sha ra ba/ gtum ston blo gros grags/ zhang ston rdo rje 'od zer/ gro ston shes rab grags/ mchims nam mkha'
grags/ bcom ldan rig pa'i ral gri/ dpal sding pa/ 'dul 'dzin grags pa dpal/ mnga' ris byang chub bla ma/ rgya gar rgyal mtshan/ bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ rong ston
shes bya kun rig /thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub/ paN chen bzang po bkra shis/ rje stobs ldan pa/ paN chen na bza' pa/ gnas pa paN chen/ rje nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/
slob dpon buddha pa/ rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pa/ bka' drin mnyam med chos dbyings rang grol/ rgyal dbang thugs rje chen po/ des bdag go /yang rjes gnang gi brgyud lugs
gcig ni/ rong ston nas/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ brag dkar ba bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang dkon mchog legs pa/ mkhas grub dpal
ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ khyab bdag zha lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ des bdag go /bcom ldan rig
ral gyi sgrub thabs/ rong ston gyis bstod pa/ gzhan yang las tshogs mang du mchis so/ ! /bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa shin tu rnam
par nges pa gzi brjid kyi rgyal po sku mdog dkar po tshe mdo mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa nas gsungs pa/ sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad
pa nas rjes gnang dang lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa sangs rgyas/ lo ke shwa ra/ grub chen mi tra dzo ki / paN chen buddha shrI/ chag lo dgra bcom/ grum ston
dar ma shes rab/ grub chen shes rab dpal/ grub thob legs ldan 'od/ dpal ldan bzang po/ ye shes dpal bzang /

blo bzang dpal 'byor/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mchog legs rdo rje/ bco brgyad pa mkhyen rab bstan
'dzin bzang po/ rtsa ba'i bla ma ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag go/ yang na dkon mchog lhun grub/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mchog legs rdo rje man gong 'dra/ yang
na dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams man gong 'dra/ sa chen a mes drung dang / rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis la yang zhus so/ !
/sgra mi snyan pa'i tshe sgrub de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa'i sgom bzlas dang bcas yod pa'i sgom lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ lha'i dge bsnyen/
dgra bcom pa blo gros dpal/ bal po ha ngu tsandra/ slob dpon dar ma grags/ mnga' ris pa dpal chen rgyal ba grub/ slob dpon ye shes rgyal po/ slob dpon shes rab grags/
bsod nams mgon po/ kun mkhyen bu ston/ thugs sras sems dpa' chen po/ bar 'dir bla ma 'ga' zhig ma rnyed/ de nas dge steng pa kun dga' dpal bzang / nyi gling rdo rje 'chang
tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go ! /padma'i rigs kyi bdag po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs bcu gcig zhal dpal mo lugs/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub pa'i sgrub thabs rjes
gnang gi steng nas rjes gnang lan gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen po| dge slong ma dpal mo/ paNDi ta tsandra ku mA ra/ paNDi ta shrI dznyA na bha
dra/ bal po paNDi ta pe nya ba/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ grub thob nyi phug pa chos grags/ spru pa rdo rje rgyal po/ zhang ston dgra 'jigs/ mkhan chen rtsi 'dul
ba thugs rje byang chub/ mkhan chen bde ba can pa/ byang sems chu bzang pa byang chub 'bar/ rin po che shes rab

'bum/ rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal/ grub chen buddha shrI/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug /yongs
'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub/ mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sa chen ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras
bsod nams dbang phyug /khyab bdag mkhan chen zha lu pa chen po/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po/ des bdag go /yang na mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod
nams seng ge nas/ bya btang kun dga' mchog ldan/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ ! thugs rje chen po spyan ras gzigs lha gsum ma skyer sgang lugs kyi rig gtad thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ grub chen rA hu la gupta badzra/ jo bo chen po dI paM kA ra shrI dznyA na/ nag tsho lo tsA tshul khrims rgyal ba/ rong pa phyag
sor shes rab 'bar/ wa yu ba shes rab tshul khrims/ lce sgom shes rab rdo rje/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge / gnyan ston chos kyi shes rab/ chos rje ston pa
brtson 'grus seng ge /'gro mgon shangs ston tshul khrims 'bum/ gnyan ston rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / sngags 'chang rdo rje gzhon nu/ mus chen nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ sems dpa'
chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge /rje btsun rdo rings pa chen po/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
/khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ paN chen ngag dbang chos grags/ yangs can mkhan po ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ rgyal ba ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ des bdag

go |yang na shangs ston nas/ mkhas btsun rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal bzang / 'jag pa blo gros dpal bzang / 'jag chen kun dga'/ rje chos rgyal dpal bzang / 'khrul
zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rdo rings rin po che man 'dra/ yang na mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan nas/ chos rje zur khang pa dpal
ldan rin chen/ rje btsun sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan nas/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ rje
lha mchog seng ge /rje sangs rgyas seng ge /mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / ngor sgrub khang pa mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ mkhan chen zha lu pa/ rgyal dbang blo bzang zhabs/
yang na mus chen nas/ kun mkhyen go bo rab 'byams pa/ dkon mchog 'phel man 'dra/ yang na mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang nas/ bla ma nam mkha' dbang phyug /mus chen
nam mkha'i rnal 'byor man 'dra/ ! spyan ras gzigs seng ge sgra'i rjes gnang gdon 'grol gnyis lung bcas ngor mkhan chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gi yig cha nas thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ dmar chos rgyal gyi yi ge nas rnyed pa/ rje btsun seng ge sgra/ tsandra go mi/ nA ro ta pa/ pham thing pa sku mched/ a thu la badzra/ men dza gling pa/ de gsum
gar mal blo gros grags pa/ sa chen man/ yang men dza gling pa/ blo gros grags pa/ shraddha ka ra warma/ bod skad dad byed go cha/ lo chen rin chen bzang po man 'dra'o/ 'di
la klu sgrub kyi gter ma/ shrI ku mA ra'i gdon 'grol/ tsandra go mi'i sgrub thabs/ rje rtse mo'i bsnyen thabs/ dmar dang / rin chen rgyal mtshan sogs kyi yi ge nas/ slob
dpon shraddha ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo blo gros grags/ brtse chen/ gnyan gtsug tor rgyal po/ rje btsun chen po/
sa paN/ shar pa ye 'byung / shar pa dus 'khor ba/ kun dga' byang chub/ mkhan po rgyal

bzang ba/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ chos rje rdo rje 'chang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / dkon mchog 'phel/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse nam
mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ thar rtse nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ khyab bdag zha lu pa chen po/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ gu ge paN chen/ glo
bo mkhan chen/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon rgyam/ sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ a mes zhabs drung / des
bdag phrin las pa la'o/ ! /sgrub khang pa slar zhu rgyu dpal ldan don grub kyis gon ba chos rje'i don du mdzad pa'i seng ge sgra'i bsnyen thabs kyi brgyud pa ni/ mkhas
pa dpal ldan don grub/ thar rtse nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ drin can zha lu pa chen po/ des bdag la'o/ ! /padma'i rigs kyi yum seng ldeng nags sgrol gtso rkyang gi rjes gnang
lung gsum gyis 'ching ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ chung ba

chen/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ des bdag go /yang na rje btsun sgrol ma/ jo bo chen po

dpal mar me mdzad/ 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ bshes gnyen po to ba/ dge bshes sha ra ba/ bya 'chad ka ba/ skyer sgang pa/ sangs rgyas sgom pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ ze'u
sku mched/ mchims blo bzang grags pa/ gro ston kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ kun mkhyen rong ston chen po/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ brag dkar
sems dpa' chen po bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma bsod nams dpal 'byor/ gnub sgom sbas pa'i rnal 'byor/ smon lam rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man
gong bzhin no/ ! /rje btsun ma dbang gi sgrol ma dmar mo dpal sa skya pa'i zab chos ngor dpal ldan don grub pa'i sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang gi cho ga nas rjes gnang dang lung
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun sgrol ma/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ chung ba don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen/ rtse mo/
rje btsun pa/ sa paN/ slob dpon shAkya 'od zer/ rgyal tsha lung mang po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug yar klung pa seng ge
rgyal mtshan/ klu pa mkhan chen bsod nams dar/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ gong ma grags pa 'byung gnas/ dpal ldan kun bzang rol pa/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ bla
ma don yod dpal/ grub brnyes dge slong ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ bstan pa'i nyi ma mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /grub pa mchog gi ded dpon dbang phyug rab brtan/ bstan pa'i mnga'
bdag mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ bka' drin 'khor med zur thams cad mkhyen pa/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ des bdag
la'o/ /lung gi brgyud pa ni/ chag lo nas/ sa lo 'jam dpal rdo rje/ mtshungs med dkon mchog lhun grub/ rje

sangs rgyas seng ge /rje btsun brang ti pa/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ thar rtse nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ khyab bdag zha lu pa chen po/ des bdag la'o/ ! /rta mchog gi rigs
kyi sgrol ma mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud la brten nas slob dpon klu sgrub kyis legs par bkral zhing lo chen dar ma grags kyis spyan drangs pa'i gnyan sgrol yan lag drug
pa rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i mngon par rtogs pa yan lag drug ldan dang rjes gnang gi cho ga ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i steng nas rjes gnang dang
/ de dang 'brel ba'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i mdo'i lung rjes gnang gi skabs nges par mdzad dgos pa'i phyag bzhes ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ slob

po/ gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ bde ba dpal/ bka'

sa lo/ dkon mchog lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na lha mchog seng ge nas/ ngor chen sangs rgyas seng ge /thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i
sgrub skor la/ lo rgyus/ bsnyen pa/ sgrub pa/ thun mtshams su bya ba gtor ma 'phrul 'khor/ chom rkun 'ching ba/ mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa dang gzungs kyi lung blang ba
dang bcas pa rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kha'u pa yan gong ltar la/ de nas gong ma lnga/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan/

pa/ btsun pa rnam mgon dri med sde/ rje byang chub dbang rgyal/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma rnam rgyal bkra shis/ thu btsun kun dga' bsod nams/ dpal 'byor
gling pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ rab 'byams pa chos rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs rnam rgyal/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na 'phags pa nas/ tshogs nyan gnyis/ brag
phug pa/ bla ma dam pa man 'dra/ yang na 'phags pa nas/ zha ston khu dbon/ bla ma dam pa man gong ltar ro/ /yang na 'phags pa nas/ shar pa sku mched/ 'jam dbyangs chen
po/ bla ma gzhon tshul ba/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa man 'dra/ sa chen kun dga' bsod nams la gong bzhin thob cing / rgya
gzhung bstod ring zhig kyang zhus so/ /! tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i tshe khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun nyams len

snying po bsdus pa dang rjes gnang gi yi ge kun mkhyen mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i steng nas rje btsun bcom ldan 'das ma sgrol ma dkar mo spyan bdun yid bzhin 'khor lo tshe sbyin
ma'i 'od zer drug sbrags kyi rjes su gnang ba thun mong ma yin pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma dkar mo/ paN grub ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/
bla ma rdo rje gdan pa/ rje btsun ba ri lo tsA ba/ grub chen sle nag pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen sgre pa/ mnyam med sgam po pa/ dwags sgom tshul khrims snying po/ sgom chung
shes rab byang chub/ dwags po 'dul 'dzin pa/ rje 'bri khung gling pa/ rje dam chos gling pa/ bla ma chos kyi tshul khrims/ mnyam med lha lung pa/ thog gnas pa chen po/ bla
ma chos kyi dbang phyug /'dren mchog byang chub bzang po/ kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal/ lo pa spyan snga bsod nams lha dbang / spang gshongs ha ri kha pa dpal ldan
rgyal mtshan/ dwags po paN chen phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i lha/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa
mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag zha lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag la'o/
/ yang na mkhyen brtse'i zhabs la/ mkhan chen bslab gsum pa/ dgon gsar ba bsod nams chos 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs byang gling rje gsum gyis gsan/ yab sras bzhi ka la rdo rje 'chang
dbang phyug rab brtan gyis gsan no/ /yang na tshar chen nas/ bod mkhar ba mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen thar pa
rgyal mtshan/ khyab bdag zha lu pa/ des bdag la'o/ /yang yig cha de kha'i steng nas thun mong ba'i rjes gnang thob pa'ang bshad ma thag pa bzhin no/ /tshe khrid zla ba'i
chu

rgyun gyi nyams len snying po bsdus pa'i steng nas nyams khrid zab mo smin rgyas dang de nyid kyi yig cha 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i rjes gnang rje dbang phyug rab brtan gyi
sgrub thabs yig cha'i lung dang bcas nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan nas/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams
mchog grub/ des bdag go ! /sgrol ma'i man ngag lha mo shra ma Na'i sgrub thabs kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ dze tA ri/

pa bsod rgyal/ shes rab rdo rje/ grags pa rdo rje/ grags pa don grub/ grub chen ri khrod pa/ shar dwags po'i paN chen bkra shis rnam rgyal/ yongs 'dzin bde legs bzang po/

mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mkhas grub byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen zha lu pa/ des bdag go ! /sgrol
dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo bka' babs dgu dang ldan pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa la bka' babs dang po jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ ngag gi dbang phyug /mgon
po gser gling pa/ jo bo rje a ti sha / 'brom ston pa/ spyan snga ba/ bya yul ba gzhon nu 'od/ dwags po lha rje bsod nams rin chen/ zhang sum thog pa/ zhang bka' stsal
ba/ bla ma lha/ slob dpon rin chen bzang po/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ byang sems bsod nams grags pa/ dpal

ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal ba phyag na/ kun bzang rtse pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chag lo rin chen chos
kyi rgyal po/ khra ri ba rin chen rgyal mchog /kun mkhyen rdzong dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dpal dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab
brtan/ bka' drin mnyam med mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ de bdag go /yang na mkhan chen
bde ba dpal nas/ bka' bzhi pa grags pa gzhon nu/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na spyan snga ba chen po nas/ dge bshes
sgre pa/ sgam po bsod nams rin chen/ phag mo gru pa/ nye gnas stag lung thang pa/ bla ma ba lam pa/ slob dpon tshal pa/ slob dpon shAkya gzhon nu/ don zhags pa sangs rgyas
rin chen/ rtsegs pa bsod nams rdo rje/ ma ti pha la/ bla ma rang grol lhun grub/ mtshungs med nam mkha' blo gros/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal man 'dra/ yang na sgam po
pa nas/ lho la yag pa/ slob dpon brtan pa/ slob dpon tshal pa ba/ slob dpon shAkya gzhon nu man 'dra/ yang na slob dpon shAka gzhon nas shangs pa grags pa seng ge /bla ma
mgon rgyal ba/ mkha' spyod dbang po/ 'khrul zhig bsod nams 'bum/ bla ma rgyal mtshan/ zhwa dmar bzhi pa spyan snga thams cad mkhyen pa| chag lo man 'dra/ yang na spyan snga
ba nas/ bya yul ba gzhon nu 'od/ dge bshes sle nag pa/ bshes gnyen sgre pa/ dwags po zla 'od gzhon nu man 'dra/ yang na zla 'od gzhon nu nas/ dus gsum mkhyen pa chos
kyi grags pa/ khams pa dbang phyug rdo rje/ bla ma dbang phyug seng ge /khams pa bya bral ba/ bla ma shes rab gzhon nu/ spyan snga chos

kyi rgyal po/ de gnyis ka la ri khrod pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ de nas ras chen gzhon nu dpal/ grub chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ de la sgo rum pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang
kun dga' rgya mtsho gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka nas rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zhabs man 'dra/ yang na chos rje bla ma dam pa
yan gong ltar la/ de nas ri khrod pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan man gong bzhin no/ / yang na bla ma dam pa nas/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/
bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sangs rgyas dpal/ rje btsun sgo rum pa man 'dra/ yang na bdag chen rdo rje 'chang nas/ rje btsun rdo rings
pa chen po/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan nas/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ lo chen grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ bo dong paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rtag lung ngag dbang grags pa/ chos rje 'chi med dpal bzang / mkhas mchog sangs rgyas lhun grub/ bo dong sngags
ram pa yon tan rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na chag lo rin chen chos rgyal nas/ rje bshes gnyen bkra shis/ grub pa'i khyu mchog dge slong ngag dbang
rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa nas/ rje dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun
dbang / glo bo mkhan chen legs 'byung / rje kun dga' grol mchog /'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man gong bzhin no/ /yang na ngor chen nas/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po/ paN chen
chos rin dpal ba/ rje blo gros rgya mtsho/ thugs rje can rin chen bzang po/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams/ sngags 'chang dkon mchog

legs 'dzin/ sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ zha lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na bya yul ba gzhon nu 'od
nas/ dge bshes 'chad ka ba/ skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge /sangs rgyas sgom pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ skyo ston smon lam tshul khrims/ rgyang ro byang chub 'bum/ mchims
blo bzang grags pa/ gro ston kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ dpang ston grub pa shes rab/ spyang lung pa gzhon nu blo gros/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ spyang lung pa gzhon nu
mchog grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog /rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang dkon mchog legs 'dzin man 'dra/ yang na bo dong phyogs las rnam rgyal nas/ thams cad
mkhyen pa dge 'dun grub/ paN chen ye shes rtse mo/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ de nas bla ma gsum tsam zhig ma rnyed/ de nas mkhan chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal
mtshan dang 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog chos 'phel/ de gnyis ka la rgyal dbang mchog gi zhabs/ nye brgyud ni/ rje btsun sgrol mas mkhas grub nor bzang rgya mtsho la dngos
su gnang zhing bstod pa shlau ka gang mang rtsom zhig de'i grangs dang mnyam pa'i tshe'i dngos grub ster bar zhal gyis 'ches pa bzhin rje btsun mar bstod pa brtsams pas
dgung lo brgyar nye bar bzhugs/ de la thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtshos gsan no/ ! /bka' babs gnyis pa sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ paN grub wA gI
shwa ra/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i
mgon po 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/

rje btsun dpal chen bzang po/ chos rje ye shes dpal bzang / chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba rin chen rgyal mchog /rjong dkar ba shes rab rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man sngar ltar ro/ /gzhan yang jo bo lugs kyi skabs smos pa'i bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan brgyud par bzhugs phyin de man chad 'dir yang
bgrangs chog go /der ma zad sa lugs 'di sa chen kun dga' bsod nams la yang thob pa'i brgyud pa slar 'dir bri rgyu/ ! bka' babs gsum pa paN chen lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje
btsun sgrol ma/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ byang sems bsod nams grags pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal ba phyag na/ mkhan chen kun dga' blo gros/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba man gong bzhin no/ /yang na/ bla ma
dam pa nas/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ mtshungs med nam mkha' blo gros/ chag lo/ khra ri pa man 'dra/ yang na paN chen
shAkya shrI nas/ paN chen dA na shI la/ tsang thang pa/ bla ma ka pa ba/ rtogs ldan grags seng / g.ya' bzang pa bsod nams 'od/ bsod nams rdo rje/ gtsang pa blo bzang pa/
rang grol lhun grub/ nam mkha' blo gros/ chag lo/ khra ri ba man 'dra/ 'dir ma zad mkhan chen byang chub dpal brgyud par bzhugs phyin de man chad 'dir yang bgrangs chog
go ! /bka' babs bzhi pa a bha yA ka ra lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ slob dpon a bha yA ka ra/ shu bhaM ka ra gupta/ legs spyod 'byung gnas/ ratna rakShi ta/
gau taM shrI/ kIrti tsandra/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rong pa shes rab seng ge /bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen

shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan chen rin chen 'phel/ bla ma ye shes 'phel/ rje kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma byang seng ba/ rgya ma ba yon tan 'od/ shangs dkar ba rin chen rgyal mtshan/
skungs lung pa sangs rgyas dpal/ rje 'phags pa rin chen/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba man 'dra/ ! bka' babs lnga pa gnyan lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol
ma/ paNDi ta ma ti/ gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun sa chen man 'dra/ sa chen brgyud par bzhugs phyin de man gyi brgyud pa
rnams tshang ma ded chog ! /bka' babs drug pa dpyal gyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ rdo rje gdan pa niska laM ka /dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po/ dpyal a mo gha/
mkhan chen gzhon nu dpal ye shes/ thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ rje btsun dpal chen bzang po/ rje ye shes dpal bzang / chag lo rin chen chos
rgyal/ khra ri ba rin chen rgyal mchog man 'dra/ bu ston rin po che brgyud par bzhugs phyin de man gyi brgyud pa gong ma rnams kyang bgrangs chog ! /bka' babs bdun pa rngog
lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ ngag dbang grags pa/ mar pa lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros/ rngog chos sku rdo rje/ rngog mdo sde/ rngog kun dga'/ rngog gzi brjid
grags pa/ rngog rin chen bzang po/ rngog chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ gnag ra ba sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ rngog byang chub dpal/ byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam par rgyal
ba/ lo chen bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde/ zhwa dmar bzhi pa spyan snga chos kyi grags pa/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba man 'dra/ ! bka' babs brgyad pa sgar lugs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ karma pa rol pa'i rdo rje/ rje mkha' spyod dbang po/ karma pa de bzhin gshegs pa/ mkhas grub bsod nams 'bum/ slob

dpon rin po che bla ma rgyal mtshan/ zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa bzhi pa chos kyi grags pa ye shes dpal bzang po/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal/ khra ri ba man 'dra/ ! bka' babs
dgu pa nags rin lugs ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ paNDi ta ngag dbang grags pa/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen/ chos rje kun dga' mchog grub/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog /chos
rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang dkon mchog legs 'dzin/ mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/
des bdag go /! gong dkar lugs kyi sgrol dkar bla ma dam pa'i yig cha nas rjes gnang dang nyi gling rjes mdzad pa'i tshe khrid rgyun khyer nas nyams khrid du thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun sgrol ma/ slob dpon ngag dbang grags pa/ gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ dpal ldan mar me mdzad/ rgyal ba 'brom/ spyan snga ba/ dge bshes sle nag
pa/ dge bshes sgre pa/ sgam po pa bsod nams rin chen/ dbu se dus mkhyen/ khams pa dbang rdor/ dbang phyug seng ge /khams pa bya bral ba/ bla ma shes rab gzhon nu/ spyan
snga chos kyi rgyal po/ de gnyis la ri khrod gzhon nu rgyal mtshan dang ras chen gzhon nu dpal ldan gnyis kyis gsan/ gnyis ka nas rje grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rje rnam rgyal
mgon po/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ bla ma shAkya kun dga'/ rje dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub nyi ma gling pa tshul khrims bkra shis/ phrin las rnam rgyal/
sgyi chu blo gros dbang phyug /mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/ bla ma kun dga' chos 'phel/ rje phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ byams pa kun dga' dbang rgyal/ mkhan chen bstan
'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag shI la dhwa dza la'o/ /yang / rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ rje blo chog rdo rje/

rgyal ba ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ rtsa ba'i bla ma rnam sras gling gi mahA paNDi ta dkon mchog chos grags zhabs/ des bdag go /yang / spyan snga/ bya yul ba/
dwags po/ zhang sum thog pa/ bla ma ka tshal ba/ slob dpon rin chen bzang po/ mkhan chen bde ba dpal/ mkhan chen bka' bzhi pa grags gzhon/ bu ston rin chen grub/ bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ yang sle nag pa/ bsam bstan dar/ rje mi nyag pa/ rje chos 'byung ba/ chos rje ra pa/ sha ra rab 'byams pa/ rje rnam
rgyal mgon po man 'dra'o/ ! /padma'i rigs kyi khro bor gtogs pa'i dpal rta mgrin nag po lcags ral can byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan gyi zhal gzigs ma yig rnying dang / thar
rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang gi gsal byed steng nas rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal rta mgrin/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ zhang skyi tsha 'od chen/ zhang dbu
dkar ba/ zhang lo tsA ba/ zhang byang chub rin chen/ dpal rgyal ba grub/ 'dzims pa rgyal mtshan dpal/ spang sgang pa grags pa dpal/ sgrub pa po bla ma rin chen brtson 'grus
chen po/ mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge /sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor pa rdo rje 'chang / kho phyar mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen go bo
rab 'byams pa/ dkon mchog 'phel/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang lhun grub/ des
bdag go ! /rta mgrin gsang sgrub zhal gsum phyag drug pa zhabs brgyad pa'i rjes gnang ni/ bskur chog tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtshos mdzad pa nas zha lu mkhan chen la
thob cing / skyer gang pa ni shangs pa'i brgyud pa rin chen sna bdun gyi lnga pa/ rmi lam bzung nas urgyan rin po che la lan gsum gsan/

slar yang slob dpon padma'i lung bstan ltar snye mo'i gter bton la gsan pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni slar bri/ rjes gnang zha lu mkhan chen la zhus/ ! rje ras chung rdo
rje grags pa nas brgyud pa'i padma gar dbang gi rigs su gtogs pa rta mgrin dmar po pad dbyug can gyi rjes gnang tshe rta zung 'brel du grags pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal rta mgrin/
o rgyan rin po che/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ grub chen ti pu pa/ rje ras chung pa| dbang phyug mi la ras chen/ sgam po zla 'od gzhon nu/ dpal phag mo gru pa/ 'bri
gung skyur ra rin chen dpal/ spyan snga grags pa 'byung gnas/ yang dgon pa thugs kyi rdo rje/ thugs sras spyan snga rigs ldan/ zur phug pa rin chen bzang po/ 'ba' ra ba
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / chos rje rin chen 'phel/ mkhan chen tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ grub mchog rdo rings pa chen po/ tshar chen chos

go |yang 'ba' ra ba'i yig cha nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mgon po tshe dpag med/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo/ ras pa badzra kIrti/ dbang phyug mi la ras pa/ yar klung gi gnyags
dmar po/ rje btsun yon tan bzang po/ rig pa 'dzin pa gnyos a seng / bla ma gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rnam rgyal dpal

shAkya kun dga'/ rje dge 'dun legs grub/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis zhabs/ ! rdo rje'i rigs kyi bdag po'i skor la/ khro bo phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed kyi
rgyud stong phrag bcu drug pa las gsungs pa sems dpa' sum brtsegs sngags hU~M badzra phaT/ kho na'o/ /gur nas gsungs pa dang mi bsre'o/ /kyi sgrub thabs thams cad mkhyen
pa rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa nas rjes gnang lu gsum gyis 'ching ba thob pa'i nye brgyud ni/ gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed/ so'i sngags 'chang
chen po shAkya dpal/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ chos dpal pa/ chos rje rin chen dpal bzang / chos rje lha dbang blo gros/ mkhas pa'i dbang po gzhung lugs rab 'byams gsung
ba rab 'byams pa dpal ldan don grub/ rje dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun kun dga' bkra shis/ des bdag go ! /rdo rje gur nas gsungs pa'i 'byung 'dul ba ri lo tsA nas brgyud
pa/ sa chen sngags 'di kho na gur nas gsungs shing dag pa ni/ oM bhu ta Da ma ra/ bhu ta a dhi pa ti| akSho bhya ki ri Ti na/ sarbba bhu ta pre ta pi shA tsi sAdha
ya hU~M phaT kun dga' bsod nams la yang zhus pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ DA ki dri med gzi brjid/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA

tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen man gong bzhin no/ /

! dpal phyag na rdo rje'i u tsa gsar ma'i rgyud 'bum na ma bzhugs pa'i rgyud chung zhig le'u bcu pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis klu'i yul nas spyan drangs par bshad nas gsungs
pa sgrub thabs sngags 'chang shAkya dpal ba/ rjes gnang 'ba' ra bas mdzad pa nas me dbang dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang lan gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/
dpal phyag na rdo rje/ padma badzra/ nA gardzu na/ tsandra go mi/ rgyal po dharma pha la| bla ma bzang gling pa/ khams pa a seng / jo sras gnyal pa/ bla ma dkon mchog
rgya mtsho/ jo sras me 'bar/ bla ma don zhags pa/ bla ma lha rje chos grags/ mkhan po chos sdings pa/ bla ma zur phug pa/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / chos sgo
ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ bla chen yon tan rgya mtsho/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma o
