go /yang na rdo rje gdan pa nas/ rje rnam rgyal rin chen/ rgya ston byang dbang / bla ma shAkya kun dga'/ slob dpon rdo rje blo gros/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra
shis/ des bdag go /yang na jo sras gnyal pa nas/ bla ma dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ ston dbyangs/ bya ston bsod nams 'od/ grags pa seng ge /gar thig pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan
chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab man 'dra/ yang na khams pa a seng nas/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ ru smon mkhar ba skyi ston grags rgyan/ ru zhang
dkon mchog blo gros/ bla ma chos grags man 'dra/ yang na lha rje chos grags nas/ e pa 'khon ston/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma sangs 'od/ slob dpon smra seng /

mkhas btsun byang seng / brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po man 'dra/ yang na mchog ldan pa nas/ skyi ston pa/ jo nang kun mkhyen/ byang seng pa man gong ltar ro/ /yang na brag
thog pa nas/ 'tshal min ngag gi dbang po/ rdo rje gdan pa man gong bzhin no/ khrus byabs srungs med dbang bcas/ sa chen kun dga' bsod nams la yang zhus so// ! rdo rje sa
'og gi rgyud le'u nyer lnga sogs nas gsungs pa phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po'i sgrub thabs sogs nas rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni| rdo
rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ dpal ldan kun tu bzang po| slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ bram ze sadzdza na/ jo
bo te dza de wa/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab/ g.yor po jo ston/ pur bsod nams rin chen/ 'byed phu ba padma bkra shis/ lha rje stag pa jo bzang / gnubs lo tsA
ba byams pa'i dpal/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug /khro phu rin chen bsod nams seng ge /yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge /thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston chos rje/ thugs sras

po/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ bka' drin mnyam med khyab bdag rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ de gnyis kar khyab

pa rin po che'i sgrub thabs bum chog rjes gnang bkru byabs bsrung gsum dang bcas pa'i steng nas rjes gnang lung tshang ma thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/
phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri lo tsA ba/ brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/
bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug /bla ma rin chen dpal/ bla ma byang chub gzhon nu| mkhan chen byang chub seng ge /shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun ngor chen/ mkhas
grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ bya 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge /rdo rje 'chang sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /khyab bdag dbang phyug rab
brtan/ bka' 'gyur ba chen po mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen zha lu pa/ badzra dhA ra/ rje phrin las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang blo gros dbang phyug /byams pa bsod
nams blo gros/ mtshungs med phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen kun dga' dbang rgyal/ mkhan po bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag ngag ming la'o/ /des phrin las par gnang
ngo / /yang / rjes gnang rkyang pa'i brgyud lugs gcig ni/ 'phags pa rin po che nas/ 'u yug pa bsod nams seng ge /shAkya seng ge /bla ma sdings pa dbang rgyal/ sa bzang
paN chen/ rin po che rgyal dbang pa/ bla

ma yon tan dpal/ rong ston blo bzang grags pa/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ bar 'dir bla ma gcig gnyis ma rnyed/ de nas sku zhang rin chen bkra shis/ lha bo pa rin chen rgya
mtsho/ khyab bdag zha lu pa chen po/ des bdag la'o/ ! /zhang blon rdo rje'i rigs kyi bdag po'i phyi sgrub gtso bo zhal gcig phyag gnyis yum dang 'khor lnga/ nang sgrub
gtso bo zhal gcig phyag gnyis 'khor dgu/ gsang sgrub gtso bo zhal gsum phyag drug 'khor lnga rnams kyi rjes gnang so sor thob pa'i yig cha jo gdan padma bzang po/ brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / gsang ba'i bdag po/ slob dpon chen po padma saM bha wa/ chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan/ lo chen bai ro tsa na/ gter bton gra pa mngon shes/ pu
reng mgon po rin chen/ dge slong smon lam 'bar/ gung chung ston pa/ sha mi sgom chen/ dol pa badzra pA Ni/ rgya byang chub sems dpa'/ brag dkar sman bla ba/ jo sras dkon
mchog gzhon nu/ mgar btsun tshul ston/ mkhas grub chos dpal bzang po/ bla ma sangs rgyas rin chen/ 'gos lo gzhon nu dpal/ rje nam mkha' shes rab/ mnga' ris rig 'dzin nyi
zla 'od zer/ bla ma u rgyan rgyal po/ bla ma paN chen kun dga' bkra shis/ bla ma rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /yang lo chen
bsod nams rgya mtsho'i yig cha nas phyi sgrub kyi rjes gnang bla ma paN chen kun dga' bkra shis kyi zhabs drung du yang zhus so/ /de'i nang sgrub phal cher 'dra zhing gtor
dbang bka' bsgo bcas pa'i rjes gnang chag lo rin chen chos rgyal lugs kyi rjes gnang yang thob/ de thams cad la slob dpon dang mdun bskyed gnyis ka'i mngon rtogs brjod
pa gnang gi 'dug ! /rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nya pho mo las khro bo rme ba brtsegs pa dud kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa dang khro mo rme brtsegs kyi rjes gnang

mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi zin bris nas rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri rin chen grags/ rje btsun
brtse ba chen po/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rje sa paN/ bla ma gra thang pa/ bla ma kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma blo gros dpal/ dge bshes seng ge /mkhan po bsod nams shes rab/
mkhan po shes rab mgon/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ rje bsod nams seng ge/ rje btsun sgo rum pa chen po/
kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ zur thams cad mkhyen pa chos dbyings rang
grol/ bstan pa'i bdag po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ rdo rje 'chang phrin las rnam rgyal/ chos rje phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ byams pa kun dga' dbang rgyal/ mkhan
chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag ngag ming la'o/ khro mo rme brtsegs la brgyud pa mi 'dra ba yod 'dug kyang / mkhan chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims kyi gsan yig
shog hril la/ khro mo rme brtsegs zhes pa gong du yi ge bcug ste bstan 'dzin tshul khrims kyi gsan yig na/ brgyud pa thun mong ma gtogs mi 'dug pas/ de bzhin ltar 'dir bkod/des
bdag go /yang na ngor chen nas/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug /glo bo mkhan chen legs 'byung / bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug /'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/
yang na mkhas btsun dge stag par khro bo'i dbang po zhal dngos su gzigs pa'i zhal gzigs brgyud pa ni/ mkhas btsun dge stag pa/ dran bu rin chen grub/ mkhan chen shes rab
gzhon nu/ slob dpon dkon mchog mkhar/ ri lung sbug pa chos kyi mgon po/ lce blo ldan seng ge /lce btsun bsod nams dpal/ sprul sku dbang phyug rdo rje/ bka' bzhi pa seng
ge rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang

yon tan dpal/ bla ma blo bzang dpal/ mkhyen rab rin po che mchog grub/ rje btsun rdo rings pa chen po/ sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa man 'dra/ yang na mkhyen rab rje nas/ rje
dkon mchog tshul khrims/ 'gos ston rdo rje seng ge /mnga' ris ru thog rdo rje gzi brjid/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse man 'dra/ ! rje btsun sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i rme brtsegs
kyi sgrub thabs sogs kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa skya bka' 'bum skabs dang 'dra'o/ /yang / rjes gnang nyi gling rdo rje 'chang la yang zhus so/ / ! khro mo rme
brtsegs kyi rjes gnang dang de'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses mdzad pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na
rdo rje/ DA ki seng ge gdong can/ gru spang rtsa ba rdo rje seng ge /chos rje brag nag pa/ byang sems chen po/ bla ma dngos grub rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon bsod nams dar/ be
bug bde legs rgyal mtshan/ sngags 'chang chos rgyal bsod nams/ de sras chos skyong bsod nams bkra shis/ thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang
phyug rab brtan/ 'jam mgon bstan pa'i nyi ma bsod nams mchog ldan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /yang / rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan
chen zha lu pa des bdag go /lung brgyud ni/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /'phags mchog byams pa skal bzang / rdo rje 'chang dbang rab man 'dra/ yang na rje
dbang rab nas/ khyab bdag zha lu pa/ des bdag la'o/ / yang na rdo rje 'chang dbang rab/ rje bka' 'gyur ba/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis zhabs/ des bdag go ! /mkha'
'gro ma seng ge'i gdong can rjes gnang dang lo rgyus/ las tshogs/ gtor chog /mngon rtogs/ mkha' 'gro lnga'i bstod pa tshigs bcad

lnga'i brgyud pa ni/ mkha' 'gro seng gdong ma/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA/ sa chen/ rtse mo| rje btsun/ paN chen/ 'phags pa/ zhang dkon dpal/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa|
sa bzang ma ti/ theg chen pa/ gu shri ngag dbang bzang nam mkha' bzang po zer po/ bdag chen rgya gar shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen 'bum phrag gsum pa/ yon tan rgya mtsho/
sngags 'chang tshe bkras/ rje o rgyan rgyal po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /yang / seng gdong ma nag mo chos 'byung
gi steng na bzhugs pa'i rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ seng gdong ma/ dze tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA
ba rin chen grags nas/ theg chen chos rgyal bar gong 'dra/ de la ngang tshul bzang po/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ blo gros bzang po/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ lo tsA ba chos skyong
bzang po/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ bco brgyad pa mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ dbon rin po
che byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag go /seng gdong ma'i sgrub thabs las tshogs/ man ngag kha shas mkhyen rab chos rjes mdzad pa'i lung brgyud ni/ mkhyen rab rje/
'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ don yod rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams lhun grub/ mchog legs rdo rje man rjes gnang dang 'dra'o/ /yang / brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ bla ma
kun dga' grags pa/ rje ngang tshul bzang po/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma blo gros bzang po/ sku zhang mkhyen/ zha lu lo tsA/ sa lo/ dkon mchog lhun grub/
nam mkha' dpal bzang / sa chen kun dga' bsod nams kyi zhabs drung du seng gdong sngon mo mi mgo skam rlon rus rgyan yod pa gcig zhus/ ! seng gdong ma dmar mo rjes gnang
dus Da ma ru grol zhing byin

rlabs thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ seng gdong ma/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ ra sa chos grags/ bla ma don yod rdo rje/ paN chen nags kyi rin chen/ lo tsA ba manydzu shrI/
rje bsam grub rgyal mtshan/ mkhas btsun A nanda dhwa dza/ rje nor bu phun tshogs/ rje lha dbang blo gros/ ngor pa sangs rgyas seng ge /thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse
gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ sa chen kun dga' bsod nams/ des bdag go ! /nor can gyi rigs rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi rjes gnang dang chos skor la/ 'dul
ba lung las/ rgyal chen bzhi po sngon mkha' lding sgra snyan dang sgra chung / klu dbugs dang dbugs chen du gyur pa bzhi kas sangs rgyas 'od srung la bslab gzhi gzung
/ rgyal ba shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa la 'jig rten skyong bar smon lam btab/ rgyal po chen po rnam mang thos pa'i sras 'di nyid kyi gzi brjid ma bzod par lha min gyi dpung
phyir log pas lha rnams ngal bsos pas ngal bsos po dang / lha min gyi g.yul bshams pa'i tshe seng ge khros pa la bzhon nas bsrungs pas gnas srungs po dang / dug sbrul chen
por sprul nas lha min dbang po rab rgod kyi dmag rnams myos par byas pas lus ngan po zhes mtshan gyi rnam grangs mang po des mu stegs kyi sprang po nyi ma'i dngos grub
sogs bsgral bas mthu che/ 'dod rgu'i dpal 'byor stsol ba'i lha mchog sa brgyad pa'i dbang phyug mdo rgyud thams cad dang / khyad par gar mkhan mchog gi rgyud las gsungs
shing / rgya bod kyi mkhas grub rnams kyis chos skyong du mnga' gsol ba 'di la/ phyi 'gyur la rnam sras kyi bka' mi 'dra ba bco lnga tsam yod pa las/ 'di nyid kyi gong gnon
du phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi rjes gnang nod dgos pa ni gong du smos zin/ slob dpon chen po 'gro bzang snying pos rgyud dang man ngag la brten nas

rnam sras kun gyi rtsa bar gyur pa zhi ba bde byed ser po lha dgu rta bdag brgyad bskor du grags pa'i rjes gnang yig cha kun mkhyen bus mdzad pa nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
zangs dkar lo tsA 'phags pa shes rab kyis/ g.yor po jo ston la gnang bar smad lugs dang / stod kyi phyogs su gtum ston blo gros grags la gnang ba nas brgyud par stod lugs
gnyis kyi/ dang po smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro
bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che gon pa ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab/ g.yor po jo ston/ bcur bsod nams gra dol bar gyi rin chen/ 'jed
phu ba padma bkra shis/ rtag pa lha rje jo bzang / khro lo snubs byams pa'i dpal/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug /sems dpa' chen po bsod nams seng ge /yang rtse ba rin chen
seng ge /kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub/ bla ma thabs kyi blo gros/ bzad pa rin rgyal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ 'jam dbyangs
byang chub dbang rgyal/ yongs 'dzin shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog
grub/ de gnyis kas bdag la'o/ /yang na rdo rje 'chang / slob dpon ka ma ru pa/ slob dpon karNa pa/ slob dpon 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ kha che sadzdza
na/ kha che te dza de wa/ zangs dkar lo tsA/ zhu sa skya pa/ grags pa seng ge /rgya ston grub pa po/ rgya ston grub mchog /bla ma rdo rje dpal/ khro phu sems dpa' chen
po man 'dra/ gnyis pa stod lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba yan gong bzhin las/ gtum ston blo gros grags/ gtum ston mgon po yon

tan/ lung khu gon pa ba/ mkhon lung ston/ slob dpon legs pa'i shes rab/ bya sder ba byang chub rin chen/ bya sder ba byang chub gzhon nu/ mang mkhar blo bzang dkar mo/ mang

dbang phyug /rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /bzlas lung dus bla ma'i bgrang phreng mnyam du 'dren cing snying
po la rjes zlos brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas so/ /yang smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni| kun mkhyen bu'i rjes la/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/
rin chen dpal grub/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ rje bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ lha bo pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen khyab bdag rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /yang / byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang rab/ mkhan chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /drag po'i rjes
gnang byed na/ zhi ba bde byed ser chen dang nges par 'brel dgos so/ /! rnam sras drag byed gzhon pa med pa klu brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rjes gnang bu ston rin po che'i phyag

pa'i gang zag de/ rnam sras la mchod gtor mi

bcag /mjug tu rnam sras kyi tshe sgrub nyams su len dgos tshul snang ngo / /yang na sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje nas/ bco brgyad pa 'jam dbyangs chos rje/ gnas brtan bstan

tshugs ma dang bcas pa smin rgyas

su nos pa las/ lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang rnying ma'i skabs na'o/ ! /bde drod rang 'bar gyi sngon 'gro bde mchog lha lnga'i byin brlabs dang / khrid yig gnyis 'bri gung mkhan

'jam dbyangs chos dpal bzang po/ mus chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgyal sras byams mgon pa/ bo dong paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po/ thams
cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ paN chen bde ba'i rdo rje/ bla ma lha dbang phrin las/ mkhas grub tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go
/nye brgyud ni/ dus gsum rgyal yum rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ /ye shes sgyu ma'i rnam rol ni gu ma/ /bde drod rang 'bar dpal 'byor bzang po'i mtshan/ /dngos grub mchog brnyes
'jigs med dpa' bo'i zhabs/ /snyan brgyud rgya mtsho byang chub dbang gi rgyal/ /mkhas dbang paN chen bde ba'i rdo rje 'dzin/ /sku bzhi'i bdag nyid lha dbang phrin las rje/
/dkon mchog gsum dngos tshul khrims bkra shis dpal/ / gsol ba 'debs so phrin las rnam rgyal gyi/ /sgo gsum rdo rje gsum du byin gyis rlobs/ /yang na ras chen/ 'jam dbyangs
byang chub dbang rgyal man 'dra'o/ ! /bde mchog la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'bebs chog ling chu rtse khab nas thob pa'i

brgyud pa ni/ nam mkha' mdzod bla ma grub chen pa/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go ! /zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid ni/ rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga'
snying pos zla ba drug gi bar du 'jam dpal gyi sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ 'jam dbyangs gtso 'khor gsum zhal gzigs pa'i gtso bos dngos su gsungs pa'i blo sbyong zhen pa
bzhi bral/ de'i 'grel pa rje btsun grags pa dang / sa skya paN chen dang / 'phags pa rin po che dang / rdo rje gdan pa'i brag thog pa dran pa'i don la ci yang med pa sogs/
de rnams kyi steng nas dmigs khrid lan gnyis thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ rje btsun brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje
sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ bla ma na bza' brag phug pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang ma
ti paN chen/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal bzang / brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa nas rim par nyi
ma gling pa rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go ! /ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo lugs tshe dpag med lha gcig bum gcig tshe zan la brten pa'i dbang bzhi byin
rlabs kyi tshul du bskur ba dang / tshe khrid gnyis 'ba' ra ba dang / mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi yig cha nas thob pa'i dbang khrid gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ ston pa yang
dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ tshe dpag med/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo| ti pu gsang sngags sdong po/ ras chung rdo rje grags pa/ mi la bzhad pa rdo rje/ chos rgyal zla
'od gzhon nu/ bde legs khams pa rdor rgyal/ 'bri gung 'jig rten mgon po| spyan snga grags pa 'byung gnas/ rgyal ba yang dgon pa/ thugs sras spyan snga

rigs ldan/ zur phug pa/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / bla ma rin chen chos 'phel/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ sku zhang rin chen mkhyen rab mchog grub/ kun
bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug / mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ rtsa ba'i
bla ma rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /rje bla mas rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen par yang gsan 'dug ! /yang tshe dpag med grub rgyal ma lugs kyi tshe dbang bskur
chog tshe khrid rgyun khyer/ khrid dpe rnams kyi lung slar zhu rgyu brgyud ni/ sangs rgyas tshe dpag med/ ma cig grub pa'i rgyal mo nas/ 'ba' ra ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
bar dbang brgyud bzhin/ bya btang chu'i rnal 'byor/ 'dren mchog don yod rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab yon tan dpal 'byung / dpal ldan 'bum phrag gsum pa/ sngags 'chang yon
tan rgya mtsho/ rje u rgyan rgyal po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ rje ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen rgya mtsho/ des bdag go /'ba' ra ba'i tshe dbang
bskur chog gi lung rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis la yang thob/ ! 'phags pa thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid la jo bo rje nas rong pa phyag sor ba la brgyud pa skyer
sgang lugs/ dge slong ma dpal mo nas brgyud pa dpal mo lugs zhes rgya gar nas byon pa gnyis/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan la 'phags pa nyid kyis dngos su gnang ba zla
rgyal lugs/ bla ma gnyan dar ma 'od la rdo rje rnal 'byor mas dngos su gnang ba tshem bu lugs zhes bka' srol bzhi las/ tshar chen gyi gsung la mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
gis zin bris su mdzad pa nas tshem bu lugs kyi dmar khrid nos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ na mo lo ke shwa rA ya/ rgyal ba kun gyi yab gcig rdo rje 'chang / /rgyal ba'i yum gyur
rdo

rje rnal 'byor ma/ /rgyal ba'i bstan 'dzin grub dbang tshem bu pa/ /gsol ba 'debs so bdag rgyud byin gyis rlobs/ /tshig rkang bzhi pa 'di'i tshab tu/ zung ldan rgyan 'grig
pa'i slad du/ rgyal dbang tshe 'dir thob par byin gyis rlobs sogs bcos/ mkhas grub spyi bo lhas pa byang chub 'od/ /mkhas mchog byang chub tshul khrims brag dmar ba// mkhas
btsun bsod nams snying po dgon bsar ba/ /mkhas pa'i yang rtse thob par byin gyis rlobs/ /snying po'i don gzigs kun spangs kun tu bzang / /snying rje'i bdag nyid byang
sems rgyal ye'i zhabs/ /snying nas 'gro ba'i don mdzad gzhon seng ba/ /snying po'i bstan pa 'dzin par byin gyis rlobs/ /theg mchog lam ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal/ /theg
chen chos rgyal kun dga' bkra shis zhabs/ /theg chen chos rje'i thugs sras kun dga' legs/ /theg mchog lam gyis 'gro kun grol byed shog /rdo rje 'chang dbang blo gros
rgyal mtshan dpal/ /rdo rje bla ma rje btsun kun spangs zhabs/ / rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ded dpon kun dga'i mtshan/ /rdo rje bzhi yi go 'phang thob par shog / kun bzang bla ma'i
thugs sras tshar pa rje/ /kun mkhyen bla ma mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug zhabs/ /kun dga'i lam ston byams pa skal bzang rje/ /kun nas 'gro ba'i 'dren par 'gyur bar shog
/gsang sngags mdzod 'dzin dbang phyug rab brtan dpal/ / gsang chen slob bshad 'dzin pa mgon po'i mtshan/ /gsang sngags gsar rnying 'dzin gtso rgyal dbang zhabs/ /gsang bdag
bzhin du gsang mdzod 'dzin par shog / gsang lam zab ston ngag dbang bstan 'dzin gyis/ /gsang sngags thos pa'i rgya mtsho phrin las par/ /skyabs 'gro sems bskyed zung
'brel sngon 'gro'i lam/ /bskyed rdzogs zung 'brel zab mo dngos gzhi'i lam/ /bsngo ba smon lam zung 'brel rjes kyi

lam/ /stan thog gcig tu zung 'brel bsgom par shog /snang stong dbyer med chu zla 'ja' tshon ltar/ /rang lus cir snang 'phags pa'i skur bsgom zhing / /grag stong dbyer med brag
cha'i sgra brnyan ltar/ /sgra rnams yig drug bzlas par shes par shog /rig stong dbyer med ma bcos sems nyid 'di/ /rtsol med zhi lhag rang grol lhug pa'i ngang // sgom
med rnam par mi rtog dbyings nyid du/ /yengs med rtse gcig nyams su len par shog /zas gos gnas mal gnyid dang 'pho ba dang / /bar do tha mal snang bar ma shor bar/ /rjes
spyod spyod lam rnal 'byor drug po yis/ /gnas skabs kun tu lam gyis zin par shog /bla ma mchog dang dbyer med 'phags pa'i zhal/ /mngon sum ston ka'i zla dbang ltar mthong
zhing / /po ta la dang bde ba can sogs su/ /bdag dang 'gro rnams thogs med bgrod par shog /ces dmar khrid tshem bu lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ lam gyi rim pa'i
smon lam mdor bsdus dang bcas pa 'di yang rnal 'byor pa tshar pa blo gsal rgya mtshos gangs can gyi ri bo'i po la gnas tshe rang gi bsam gtan gyi khang bur sbyar ba 'gro
ba la phan par gyur cig 'di'i kun bzang bla ma nas mgon po'i mtshan gyi bar rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i gsung / gsang sngags gsar rnying sogs tshig rkang gsum
bdag rang gi'o/ ! /yang / thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid tshem bu lugs nA lendra rje bco brgyad pa la thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ bla

sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ gangs chen pa kun dga' dpal/ bka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ kun dga'
legs grub/ kun dga' chos grags/ mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ thugs rje'i bdag nyid byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag go ! /grub chen mi tra
dzo ki'i thugs kyi bcud 'phags pa thugs rje chen po'i bskyed rdzogs kyi rnal 'byor shin tu zab pa snying po don gsum du grags pa thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i
khrid yig dga' ldan du bgrod pa'i them skas la zhal shes snyan brgyud kyis brgyan pa'i nyams khrid thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen po/ byang sems blo gros
rin chen/ grub chen ti lo pa/ grub chen rol pa'i rdo rje/ grub chen mi tra dzo ki /khro phu lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug /khro phu bsod

ras gzigs kha sarpa Nis grub chen mi tra dzo ki la gnang ba sems nyid ngal gso'i khrid tshar chen gyi gsung la mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis zin bris mdzad pa nas khrid lung

grags pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ bar 'dir bla ma gcig gnyis shig ma rnyed/ 'jam dbyangs byang gling chos rje rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/
rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ khyab bdag zha lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ des bdag go /yang na gtsang nyeg pa rin chen rgyal mtshan nas/ snar thang byang
chen pa bsod nams blo gros/ chos rje don grub grags pa/ dka' bcu bsod nams grags pa man 'dra/ yang na bla ma dam pa nas/ gtsang nyeg pa rin chen rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ !
rin chen gling nas rin chen du ma yis/ /gru chen bkang nas rang gnas 'byor pa bzhin/ /rdo rje gdan 'dir sdom gsum legs blangs nas/ /dam chos mang thos mi lus don ldan nga'o/
/thob yig bum pa bzang po las man ngag khrid dang khrid tsam thob pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// //! grub pa'i dbang phyug bar dor mchog gi dngos grub brnyes pa nag po spyod
pa'i rnam 'phrul/ khyab bdag kun dga' grol mchog gis/ zab khrid brgya dang brgyad phyogs gcig tu sdom pa'i glegs bam ni/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa dge ba'i dbang
po'i zhal snga nas la khrid lung legs par nos pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs ni/ oM swasti siddhaM dang po nas/ bde mchog la gnas bkra shis shog gi bar ro/ /de yang sngon
'gro dang dngos gzhi rjes gsum gyi sngon 'gro kun la sbyar nas/ dngos gzhi dang

rjes so so ni/ ! khrid brgya'i thog ma zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid sa skya paNDi ta'i gsung la nub pa rig 'dzin grags kyi zin bris las btus pa'o/ ! /blo sbyong don bdun ma'i
khrid rgyal sras rin po che'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! rten 'brel snying po'i khrid mus chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang gi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! skyid sdug lam khyer gyi
khrid rgyal sras chos rdzong pa'i gsung la rje re mda' ba'i zin bris las btus pa/ ! sum pa'i blo sbyong gi khrid chos rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i khrid yig las btus pa/
! ma gcig gi khrid don khrid las btus pa/ ! snying po don gsum gyi khrid khro phu lo tsA ba'i yi ge las btus pa/ ! sems nyid ngal gso'i khrid yang rtse ba'i khrid yig
las btus pa/ ! skyes bu gsum gyi khrid mchims kyi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! bstan rim gyi khrid mchims kyi yig rnying las btus pa/ ! srid zhi mnyam nyid kyi khrid mchims kyi
khrid yig las btus pa/ ! dbu ma chen po'i khrid byang sems zla rgyal gyi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! bka' gdams lkog khrid mchims kyi yig rnying las btus pa/ ! bka' gdams
lha bzhi'i thub pa'i khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! bka' [-] gdams lha bzhi'i spyan ras gzigs kyi khrid mchims kyi khrid dpe za ma tog bkod pa dpang bzhag pa/ ! bka' gdams
lha bzhi'i mi g.yo ba'i khrid sngon gyi dpe rnying las btus pa/ ! bka' gdams lha bzhi'i sgrol ma'i khrid mchims kyi khrid las btus pa/ ! po to ba'i dpe chos kyi khrid
hor bka' pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! thig le bcu drug gi khrid bka' gdams glegs bam nas btus pa/ ! sher phyin bka' babs drug gi khrid rong ston gyi khrid yig las btus
pa/ ! zhi byed lam lnga'i khrid rong ston shes bya kun rig gi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! sgom rim thog mtha'

bar gsum gyi khrid rong ston shes bya kun rig gi khrid las btus pa/ ! byams chos lnga'i khrid bcom ldan rig ral gyi khrid dpe las cung zad btus pa/ ! rang stong gi lta khrid
pa tshab kyi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! gzhan stong gi lta khrid btsan kha bo che'i yig rnying las btus pa/ ! sbas don gyi khrid rang gi rgyas 'grel khrid tshul nyis brgya
dang sum cu'i rab tu dbye ba yod pa las btus pa/ ! tshe khrid rang gi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! sgrol dkar gyi khrid gsung rgyun las byung ba/ ! tshe dpag med dkar po'i
khrid chag lo'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! dmar khrid tshem bu lugs chos rje sher 'bum pa'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! dmar khrid dpal mo lugs yol ston chos dbang gi yig rnying
las btus pa/ ! dmar khrid zla rgyal lugs khrid dpe gnyis kyi snying po btus pa/ ! dmar khrid skyer sgang lugs chos sku shAkya rin chen gyi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! bde
mchog gi dmar khrid gsung rgyun las bris pa/ ! kye rdo rje'i dmar khrid gsung rgyun las bris pa/ ! phyag rdor 'khor chen gyi khrid dmar gyi yig rnying las btus pa/ ! gtum
po'i khrid gsang bdag sgrub chen gyi khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! phag mo kurma pA da'i khrid rin chen chos rgyal gyi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! ku ru kulle'i khrid gces btus
nas btus pa/ ! sbyor drug gi khrid tsandan dang de'i dri ltar rgyud 'grel las btus pa/ ! dus 'khor snyan brgyud kyi khrid rnying ma'i gal po rgyud lung pha ma med pa'i rgan
rgon sogs phyir bsal gang yid ches pa rnams chos rje mkhas pa'i dbang po'i zhal slob zhig gi ngag las rnyed pa'i cha shas tsam bkod pa/ ! u rgyan bsnyen sgrub kyi khrid
zla seng gi khrid las btus pa/ ! lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i khrid chos rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i khrid yig sbas don gsal ba las btus pa/ ! lam skor

phyi ma bsam mi khyab kyi khrid rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! lam skor phyi ma padma badzra gyi khrid rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid dpe las
btus pa/ ! lam skor phyi ma/ Dombhi pa'i lhan cig skyes grub kyi khrid rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! lam skor phyi ma gtum mo lam rdzogs kyi khrid
rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! lam skor phyi ma'i yon po srong ba'i khrid ni rje btsun grags pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! lam skor phyi ma phyag
rgya'i khrid rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! lam skor phyi ma phyag chen yi ge med pa'i khrid rje btsun grags pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! lam
skor phyi ma mchod rten drung thob gyi khrid rje btsun grags pas mdzad pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! mdo rgyud bsre ba'i khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! bar chad gsum
sel las phyi rol gdon gyi bar chad sel ba'i khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! 'byung ba lus 'khrugs kyi bar chad sel ba'i khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! ting 'dzin sems kyi
bar chad sel ba'i khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! phyag chen sdug bsngal gsum sel gyi khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! gnyug ma dran gsal gyi khrid yig rnying las btus pa/
! dag pa gsum gyi khrid chos rgyal 'phags pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! rang byin rlabs kyi dmigs pa nyi shu rtsa dgu'i khrid 'brog mi'i yig rnying las btus pa/ ! lam
sbas bshad kyi khrid chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! brda don gsal ba'i khrid sa skya paNDi ta'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! gsang 'dus rim lnga'i khrid
rdo rje 'chang gi gsung sgros las btus pa/ ! grol ba'i thig le'i khrid byang phug pa'i zin bris las btus pa/ ! spros med kyi khrid glo bo lo tsA

ba'i stong thun las btus pa/ ! rnal 'byor bzh-i rim gyi khrid glo bo lo tsA ba'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! 'jigs byed kyi rwa khrid skyo'i yi ge las btus pa/ ! yab la brten
pa'i rtsa dbu ma'i khrid rje btsun grags pa'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! yum la brten pa'i rtsa dbu ma'i khrid gsung rgyun bzhin snying po dril nas bris pa/ ! dril bu rim lnga'i
khrid tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal gyi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! nag po rim bzhi'i khrid rje sa chen gyi rim bzhi lam slong las btus pa/ ! bde mchog dkar po'i khrid dpyal
a mo gha'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! gdan bzhi'i khrid rngog zhe sdang rdo rje'i yig rnying las btus pa/ ! mahA mA ya'i khrid rngog pa'i yig rnying las btus pa/ ! bde mchog
bong zhal can gyi khrid zhal las 'ongs pa nyid nye bar bris pa/ ! phag mo sgom drug gi khrid dpyal pa'i yig rnying ji lta ba bzhin du btus pa/ ! nA ro chos drug gi khrid
gser zhun ma las bkol te bris pa/ ! ni gu chos drug gi khrid bsam sdings pa gzhon nu grub kyi khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! phyag rgya chen po ga'u ma'i khrid bsam sdings
pa gzhon nu grub kyi khrid las btus pa/ ! lam khyer gsum gyi khrid bsam sdings pa gzhon nu grub kyi khrid las btus pa/ ! sems 'chi med kyi khrid bsam sdings pa gzhon nu
grub kyi khrid las btus pa/ ! su kha chos drug gi khrid mkhyen rab rje'i khrid las btus pa/ ! bdag med ma'i nang khrid khyung po'i yig rnying las btus pa| ! lhan cig skyes
sbyor gyi khrid rgyal sras pa'i gsung las rgya ma ba'i zin bris mdzad pa las btus pa/ ! phyag rgya chen po lnga ldan gyi khrid spyan snga ba'i khrid yig las btus pa/ !
phyag rgya chen po yi ge bzhi pa'i khrid g.yag sde paN chen gyi khrid yig las btus pa/ ! sku gsum ngo sprod kyi khrid rje rang byung rdo rje'i khrid las btus pa/ ! rlung

sems gnyis med kyi khrid lha gzigs ras pa'i khrid dpe las btus pa/ ! sras mkhar ma'i khrid gter yig nang nas bkol te bris pa/ ! rngog pa'i bsre 'pho'i khrid rngog zhe sdang
rdo rje'i khrid las btus pa/ ! snyan gyi shog dril bzhi'i khrid mtshur dbang gi rdo rje'i yig rnying las btus pa/ ! snyan rgyud kyi khrid zhang lo'i khrid las btus pa/ !
lus med mkha' 'gro'i chos skor dgu'i khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! zhang gi zab rgya'i khrid ni zhang gi zab rgya nas btus pa/ ! dpal chen rga lo'i sbyor drug gi khrid
bla ma zhang mtshal pa'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! phag gru'i thel lugs skor gyi khrid phag gru'i gsung 'bum las btus pa/ ! dgongs gcig gi khrid rdo rje'i gsung zhe brgyad
pa las btus pa/ ! stag lung pa'i chos drug gi khrid dpal stag lung thang pa chen po'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! bla sgrub kyi khrid dpal ldan 'brug pa'i khrid dpe las btus
pa/ ! lo ras thub pa lnga ldan gyi khrid grwa dga' ldan pa'i khrid las btus pa| ! ri chos snying po drug gi khrid ri chos nyid las btus pa/ ! mgon po sku rags ma'i khrid
yig rnying na de ltar btus pa/ ! dpal gur gyi mgon po'i nang khrid yar lungs pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyi khrid yig nang ltar btus pa/ ! do ha skor gsum gyi khrid par phu
ba'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! grub thob chos drug gi khrid yig rnying las btus pa/ ! padma lam rim gyi khrid padma lam rim gyi gnad 'doms khol phyung ngo / / ! rgyal po
bka' 'bum gyi khrid lha rje dge ba 'bum gyi khrid las btus pa/ ! nor bu mthong grol gyi khrid bram pa'i khrid yig las btus pa/ ! sems khrid yid bzhin nor bu'i khrid kA
la dung mtsho nas spyan drangs pa'i dpe rnying las btus pa/ ! de ltar khrid tshul brgya dang brgyad thob pa'i brgyud pa rgyas pa/ mkhas grub dbang po kun dga' grol

mchog zhal snga nas kyis bla ma so so la gsan tshul slar bri/ re zhig la khyab bdag kun dga' grol mchog /spos khang mkhan chen shes rab rin chen nam bsam gtan rin chen/ lo
pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ dpal sa skya pa a mes kun dga' bsod nams/ de nyid kyi rigs chos gnyis ka'i sras mchog 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ mtshan gzhan bsod nams dbang phyug
zhabs/ mkhan chen byams pa dge ba'i dbang pos dgyes bzhin du phrin las par gnang ba'o/ /(ta)! bka' 'gyur lung gi skor ni/ chu 'brug lo sa ga'i tshes bco lnga rang lo nyer
brgyad lon tshe/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul
ba'i kha lo bsgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa shAkya thub pa thugs rje'i bdag nyid can gyis legs par gsungs pa'i dam pa'i chos ni thog mtha' bar
gsum du dge ba ste/ de'i nyan thos dag gi sa thog mar dge ba ni 'di lta ste/ lus kyi legs par spyod pa dang / ngag gi legs par spyod pa dang / yid kyi legs par spyod pa'o/
/ bar du dge ba ni lhag pa'i tshul khrims dang / sems dang shes rab la bslab pa'o/ /tha mar dge ba ni/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang
/ smon pa med pa'o/ /gzhan yang dang por dge ba ni/ dad pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bag yod pa'o/ /bar du dge ba ni/ dran pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / sems rtse gcig

pa'o/ /tha mar= shes rab dang lhag mthong dang ye shes so/ /gzhan yang dang por dge ba ni/ sangs rgyas la mi phyed par dang ba'o/ /bar= chos la= tha mar= dge 'dun la mi phyed
par dang bas 'bras bu thob pa'o/ /gang dang por dge ba ni gzhan la nyan pa'o// bar= tshul bzhin yid la byed pa'o/ /tha mar= 'phags pa'i yang dag par blta ba'o// gang thog
mar= sdug bsngal yongs su shes shing kun 'byung ba spong ba'o/ /bar= lam sgom pa'o/ /tha= 'gog pa mngon sum du byed pa ste/ 'di dag ni nyon mongs rnams kyi thog mar yang
dge /bar= tha mar yang dge ba'o/ /de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi thog mar dge ba ni byang chub kyi sems mi gtong ba'o/ /bar= theg pa chung ngu mi 'dod pa'o/ /tha=
thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du bsngo ba'o/ /gang thog= sems can thams cad la sems snyoms pas byams pa che ba'o/ /bar= sems can thams cad la ci bya snyam pas snying rje ba'o/
/tha= dga' ba dang btang snyoms mnyam pa'i sems kyi rtog pa'o/ /gang thog= 'jungs pa'i sems tshar gcod pa dang / ngang tshul ngan pa spong ba dang / gnod sems sel ba
dang / le lo spong ba dang / g.yeng ba mi spyod pa dang / shes rab 'chal pa spong ba'o/ /bar= sbyin pa dang tshul khrims dang bzod pa dang / brtson 'grus dang bsam gtan dang
shes rab kyi tshogs byed pa'o/ /tha= pha rol tu phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo ba'o// gang thog= bsdu ba'i dngos po
bzhis sems can rnams yongs su smin pa'o/ /bar= lus dang srog la mi blta bar dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin pa'o/ /tha= skyon med par ltung ba nyid srung ba'o/ /gnang thog=
sems sa dang mtshungs pa mi gtong bas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'o/ /bar= 'jug pa dang ldog pa'i shes pas phyir mi ldog pa'i

sa'o/ /tha= dbang thob pas skye ba gcig gis thogs pa ste 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi thog mar yang dge /bar= tha mar yang dge ba'o/ /zhes dkon mchog gi za ma
tog gi mdo las gsungs so/ /de lta bu'i gsung ganggA'i chu rgyun las rab ni lha klu mi dang dri za la sogs ris med pa'i 'gro ba rnams kyi khams dang bsam pa dang bag la nyal
ba la brten nas dbang por 'tsham pa'i drang nges kyi chos so so'i skad dang mthun par stsal ba'i tshad ni nam mkha'i pha mtha' bzhin rtogs par dka' bas nyan rang gi/ slob
mi slob kyi 'phags pa rnams dang srid pa rgyun gyi mtha' ma'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis kyang 'di tsam mo zhes gzung bar mi nus na so so skye bo rnams kyi yul lta
ga la zhig /'on te rgya mtsho las chu thigs tsam zhig yul dbus 'gyur 'chang sogs su 'phags pa dgra bcom pa rnams kyi bka' bsdu ba rim pa gsum dang 'dzam gling mdzes par
byed pa'i rgyan drug mchog gnyis/ mngon par rtogs pa'i sa lam mthon por gshegs pa'i grub chen brgyad cu rtsa bzhi sogs skyes chen du mas 'thor ba sdud pa dang 'chad nyan
gyis gtan la phab ste thos bsam sgom pa'i chu bo gcig tu 'khyil ba'i ma dros pa'i mtsho chen po las byang phyogs gangs ri'i ra bas bskor ba'i sman ljongs 'dir mdo rgyud
chu klung nye bar babs pa'i thog ma pho brang yum bu gla sgang gi yang thog tu dpal kun tu bzang po'i rnam par 'phrul pa lha tho tho ri bzhugs pa'i phyag tu nyi zer dang
lhan cig par gser shog la baiDUryas bris pa'i spang skong phyag brgya pa mdo sde za ma tog babs pas bstan pa'i dbu brnyes/ lag na padma mi'i gzugs can srong btsan sgam po'i
dus 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa thu mi sambho Tas rin po che tog gi gzungs/ sher phyin 'bum pa/ thugs rje chen po'i mdo rgyud nyi shu rtsa gcig bsgyur ba sogs

bstan pa'i srol btod/ 'jam dpal rdo rje'i sprul pa rje khri srong lde btsan gyi sku ring la mkhan slob gnyis dang bai ro tsa na sogs lo paN mang po dbu'i bla mchod du bkur
te theg pa che chung gi bka' dgongs 'grel mtha' klas pa bsgyur nas bstan pa dar rgyas su mdzad/ sad na legs 'jing yon gyi dus bande dpal brtsegs/ chos kyi snying po/ de wandhe
dpal gyi lhun po sogs kyis phang thang ka med kyi gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i gsung rab rnams la shlau ka grangs them byang bkod par dkar chag phang thang ma zhes
bka' 'gyur phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i thog ma yin zhing / de rjes ban de dpal brtsegs dang 'khon klu'i dbang po srungs sogs kyis stong thang ldan dkar na bzhugs pa'i gsung
rab rnams bsgrigs nas dkar chag ldan dkar ma mdzad/ sngon lha sras yab mes kyi ring la lo paN rnams kyis chos skad bod la ma grags pa las ming du btags pa mang dag cig
mchis pa'i nang nas 'ga' zhig chos kyi gzhung dang byA ka ra Na'i lugs dang mi mthun pa rnams btsan po khri lde srong btsan/ 'on ljang rdo na bzhugs pa'i dus nyi 'og gi
mkhan po A tsarya dzi na mi tra/ su rendra bo dhi/ shI lendra bo dhi/ dA na shI la| bo dhi mi tra dang / bod kyi mkhan po ratna rakShi ta/ dharma tA shI la/ lo tsA ba dznyA
na se na dza ya rakShi ta/ manydzu shrI warma/ na lenda ratnendra shaM la sogs lo paN rnams la rgyal pos dpyad pa gyis shig par bka' gnang ste 'gyur rnying mi bcos su
mi rung ba rnams kyang bcos skad kyi ming gces so 'tshal gyis kyang bsnan nas theg pa che chung gi gzhung las ji ltar 'byung ba dang gzhan pa'i mkhan po chen po nA gArdzu
na dang ba su bandhu sogs kyis ji ltar bshad pa dang byA ka ra Na'i lugs dang yang bstun te 'jal dka' ba rnams kyang tshig so sor phral nas gtan tshigs kyis bshad de gzhung
du bris/ skad rkyang pa bshad

mi 'tshal ba sgra ji bzhin du bsgyur bar rigs pa rnams kyang sgra btsan par bgyis te ming du btags/ skad kha cig don bzhin du gdags par rigs pa rnams kyang don btsan par bgyis
te ming du btags nas lo paN rnams kyis rje blon gdan 'dzom pa la zhus nas skad gsar bcad che 'bring chung gsum gyis gtan la legs par phab/ sngar ma 'gyur ba mang po gsar
du bsgyur/ bstan pa phyi dar la paNDi ta smr-i ti dznyA na kIrti/ jo bo chen po mar me mdzad/ kha che paN chen bsod snyoms pa shAkya shrI sogs 'phags yul gyi paNDi ta
du ma dang / lo chen rin bzang dang 'brog mi sogs 'jig rten gyi mig gcig pu mang du byon te mdo rgyud kyi bka' bstan bcos mtha' klas pa bsgyur zhing / bcom ldan ral gri'i
slob ma 'jam dgag pa shis rgya nag nas bka' 'gyur ro cog bzhengs pa'i cha rkyen du dngos po mang du bskur ba la brten nas 'dul ba lung gi ma dpe sngon mchims nam mkha'
grags kyis bzhengs pa dang / mdo sde'i skor chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i thugs dam lha mi'i rgyan mchog /gtsang chu mig ring mo'i mdo mangs 'dar phyar bas/ gru
spangs rtsa'i thugs dam 'dzam gling rgyan/ zha lu gser khang gi mdo mang mchims kyi thugs dam gser gzhung ma/ phyugs rgyal ma/ dgon gsar ma le tshan/ spun gsum gtsug lag
khang na bzhugs pa'i mdo mang sogs gung bsgrigs/ sher phyogs rgyud 'bum dang bcas pa dbus pa blo gsal/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba bsod nams 'od zer/ rgyang ro byang chub
'bum sogs mkhas pa mang pos sgo bstun te go rim 'khrul pa med par dpal snar thang gi gtsug lag khang du bzhengs/ mkhas pa chen po bcom ldan ral gris dkar chag nyi ma'i
'od zer mdzad/ ma phyi de nyid las tshal pa si tu dge ba'i blo gros kyis skyid shod tshal gung

thang gi gtsug lag khang du bzhengs pas tshal pa bka' 'gyur zhes grags che/ bka' 'gyur sngon ma rnams kyi rgyud 'bum du gsang 'dus gnyis med rnam rgyal rgya pho ba lung pas
brtsams pa sogs rgyud brdzus ma kha yar dang / mdo mang nas kyang dogs pa'i gnas su gyur pa rnams phyir dbyung / gsang sngags snga 'gyur gyi rgyud rnams slar zhus dag cig
mdzad bzhed kyis re zhig btang snyoms su bzhag ste shin tu kha gtsang ba snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po ches dkar chag tu btab nas zha lu gser khang
gi gtsug lag khang du bzhugs/ de nas rim gyis mched pa rnams la them spangs mar grags pa/ dam pa rnams kyi bstan pa la bya ba legs par mdzad pa'i phyag gi ri mo lus can bsod
nams kyi me long du shar ba'i bod dang bod chen po'i rgyal khams su bka' 'gyur ro cog gi glegs bam mang por 'phel la/ de'ang sher phyin dang mdo sde rin po che du ma
las/ dam pa'i chos kyi tshul chos 'di nyid gzung bar bya/ bcang bar bya/ lung dbog par bya/ lung nod par bya/ kha ton du bya/ kun chub par bya zhes lan grangs mang por rgya
cher bka' stsal pa ltar ri mor 'bri ba las kyang thos bsam sgom gsum du bya ba ni bsngags shing / de la dgongs nas sngon byon dam pa du mas 'bad pa chen pos nye bar btsal
ba'i lung gi rgyun rgyud skor tsam ma gtogs rim gyis je phrar gyur pa'i tshe mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang pos
rin po che bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan la gsan nas 'bum rab 'byams pa khu dbon sogs la gnang ba'i rgyun bzang po las mdo mang sher phyogs gzhan du cher ma 'phel ba'i
tshe lho brag sprul sku chos rgyal don grub/ zhwa dmar dkon mchog yan lag /rgyal tshab grags pa don grub gsum thugs sgam zhing

lung rnams kyang mthar chags su nges par mdzad pa'i nges shes kyi lo rgyus thos pas rgyal tshab grags don par sdom brtson tshogs gnyis dpal grub kyis zhus nges dang / de dang
dhI tsha sprul sku gnyis kyis sher phyogs dang mdo mang skor mkhas grub blo mchog rdo rje la tshig gcig tsam yang ma lus par gnang ba nas lung rgyun mtshan nyid pa yod
par nges pa rnyed pas yid drangs te 'dir snang gi rnam g.yeng ban bun rnams kyi rjes su ma 'brangs par 'bad pa chen pos zhus pa la/ ! bka' dang po bden bzhi'i chos 'khor
las byung ba 'dul ba lung / bar pa mtshan nyid med pa'i chos 'khor las byung ba sher phyogs/ mtha' ma legs par phye ba'i chos 'khor las byung ba dkon brtsegs dang phal chen/
'khor lo gsum po ci rigs par gtogs pa sde tshan phyogs gcig bsgrigs pa mdo mang / theg pa thams cad kyi yang rtser son pa rgyud 'bum dang lnga/ dang po ni/ chos mngon
pa la dgra lan gsum byung zer ba'i lo rgyus dang mtshungs pa lung zhu ba'i 'grel par bram ze'i rgyal po rgyal shes kyis mchod rten bshig /dge 'dun gyi kun dga' ra ba dag
me la bsregs/ dge slong mang du bsad/ glegs bam rnams kyang zhugs kyi phung por sbyangs pas bstan pa la 'phel 'grib byung bar brten/ dge slong rnams kyis yul gzhan dag
nas 'dul ba'i sde snod kyi glegs bam mang du bsdus kyang gzhung bla ma'i glegs bam ma rnyed pas nam zhig na kha che'i yul gyi dge slong zhig gi blo nas 'don pa thos te rtsad
bcad pas dge slong des cung zad gcig ni dran cung zad gcig ni mi dran no zhes smras pa na dran bzhin du 'don du bcug nas dge slong rnams kyis gzhung bla ma yi ger bkod/
slar rnam par dpyad par bya'o snyam pa'i ngang nas g.yeng bas lus pa yul mang por 'phel zhing / de la ma tshang ba dang ma dag pa byung bas bram

ze'i btsun pa yon tan 'od kyi 'dul ba'i rnam bshad kyi zhu ba las 'di skad byung ngo zhes dogs gnas su yang yang bkod cing / de'i phyir 'phags pa nye bar 'khor gyis zhus pa
kha che ba zhes bya ste zhes 'byung bas zhu ba rdzogs pa dang bcas pa'i gzhung dam pa ni yang dag par bsdus pa'i gzhi po nyams pas ma dag cing sngar gsung rab rnams mer
bsregs pa'i dus thal ba'i khrod nas rnyed par grags pa'i dang po'i gzhung ma nyams pa yul dbus kyi dge slong 'ga' zhig gi blo la snang ba 'phags pa'i gnas brtan chen po rnams
dang sde snod 'dzin pa'i mkhas pa mang pos dbus 'gyur 'chang du gtogs pa'i grong khyer chen po bcom brlag tu bsdus pa'i lung zhu ba ma rdzogs pa 'di dag pa yin la/ de'ang
gangs ri'i ljongs su 'gyur ro cog gi lung sde bzhi'i bzhugs tshul la snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che sogs mkhas pa mang dag gis pha'i so thar
mdo'i tshig gi 'grel pa pha'i rnam 'byed yin pas dang por pha'i so thar dang rnam 'byed/ de nas ma'i so thar dang rnam 'byed/ de nas so thar mdo'i don gyi 'grel pa lung gzhi/
de gnyis kyi kha skong ba phran tshegs/ de dag gi don zhus lan gyis gtan la 'bebs pa lung zhu ba'am gzhung bla mar mdzad nas rgyal rtse them spangs ma sogs go rim de
ltar yod/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig tu rtsa ba'i lung dge slong pha ma'i so thar gnyis/ de nas lung sde gzhi'i dang po lung gzhi/(tha)! bstan 'gyur
las cha shas tsam gyi lung thob pa la theg pa 'og ma dang

rgyu'i theg pa chen po dang 'bras bu'i theg pa rnams la rgya gzhung gtso bor byas pa'i skor gsum gyi dang po ni/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba'i tshig
le'ur byas pa/ me tog phreng rgyud/ dgra bcom pa sa ga lhas mdzad pa paN chen shAkya shrI dang / khro phu lo tsA byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thub
dbang / 'od srung chen po/ kun dga' bo/ sha na'i gos can/ nyer sbas/ dhi dhi ka /nag po pa/ legs mthong / dge 'dun 'bangs/ 'phags pa sa ga lha/ slob dpon ma ti ratna/
kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal/ seng ge zil gnon/ rin chen bsod nams seng ge /'um phug gnas rnying pa kun dga' dbang phyug /mkhan chen nyi
ma rgyal mtshan/ bka' bzhi pa shes rab seng ge /bka' bzhi pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon dge ba dpal/ mkhas btsun skal bzang pa/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ 'jam dbyangs
chos rje/ chos rje kun dga' dbang phyug /slob dpon sangs rgyas dpal grub/ ngor chen lha mchog seng ge /rje sangs rgyas seng ge /thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ khyab bdag bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ 'phags pa'i gnas brtan tshul khrims bkra shis/ des tshe dang ldan pa bdag
la'o/ ! /'dul ba mdo rtsa slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ nye bar 'khor/ 'od srung / kun
dga' bo/ sha na'i gos can/ nyer sbas/ dhi dhi ka /nag po pa/ legs mthong / phyir 'ong blos mi 'bebs/ slob dpon yon tan 'od/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ shAkya 'od/ seng ge'i gdong
can/ kha che dzi na mi tra/ dA na shI la/ g.yo dge 'byung / bla chen mu thur ba dgongs pa rab gsal/ klu mes tshul

khrims byang chub/ gzus rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ sog tshul khrims bla ma/ ko khyim pa ye shes bla ma/ nyang 'tsham pa rin chen bla ma/ de gsum ga la rgya 'dul ba dbang phyug tshul
khrims/ de nas rma tsho byang chub rdo rje/ byang 'dul brtson 'grus 'bar/ chos kyi dbang phyug /chos kyi byang chub/ chos kyi brtson 'grus/ chos grags/ rin chen dpal
bzang / rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub/ dmar ston rgya mtsho rin chen/ chos rje gzhon nu rgyal mchog /'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/
slob dpon don grub shes rab/ bla ma lha mchog seng ge /shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang man gong dang 'dra/! dge tshul gyi
'dul ba sum brgya pa slob dpon shAkya 'od kyis mdzad pa'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon yon tan 'od/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ shAkya 'od/ seng ge'i gdong can/ dharma pha la/
zhang zhung pa rgyal ba'i shes rab/ rab 'byor shes rab/ byang chub shes rab/ byang chub seng ge /rdo rje seng ge /smad g.yung drung / rtsi 'dul thugs rje byang chub/ bde
ba can pa shAkya byang chub/ zul phu ba yon tan grags/ slob dpon bsod blo/ slob dpon bka' bcu pa/ mkhan chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/ 'jam dbyangs
shes rab rgya mtsho/ slob dpon don grub shes rab/ bla ma lha mchog seng ge /shar khang pa shes rab rgyan/ paN chen thar rtse pa nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang
pa dpal ldan don grub/ 'phags pa 'dul ba 'dzin pa mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rje btsun rin chen rgya mtsho/ des bdag go ! |chos rgyal 'phags pas mdzad pa'i 'dul ba'i las
chog che chung gi lung brgyud sa skya bka' 'bum gyi skabs na'o/ /kun mkhyen bu ston gyis mdzad pa'i 'dul ba'i

las chog dang zhar byung khyim pa la phan gdags pa'i 'dul ba'i lag len cho ga dri ma med pa'i phreng ba dang 'dul ba'i zhe sa dgu phrugs gnyis kyi lung brgyud bu ston bka'
'bum skabs na'o/ /rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum gyi tshigs bcad mdzad pa po nyid la thos so/ ! /slob dpon dbyig
gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i shes bya'i gzhi lnga gtso bor brjod pa'i chos mngon pa mdzod kyi rtsa ba'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen/ blo gros brtan pa|
gang pa spel/ shAnti pa/ puNya shrI/ rngog lo blo ldan shes rab/ mchims lha rje go cha/ mchims brtson seng / mchims don grub rgyal ba/ mchims brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/
mchims blo gros brtan pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ mchims blo bzang grags pa| rong pa chos rgyal/ nyag ma ba rin chen/ dmar ston dpal ldan rin chen/ rong ston shes bya kun
rig /bzad pa blo gros rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel/ rje phrin las pa/ dpa' bo gtsug lag phreng ba/ zhwa dmar dkon mchog yan lag /karma pa dbang phyug rdo rje/
'jam dbyangs bla ma/ sman lung pa blo gros mchog gi rdo rje/ rab 'byams pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan rin po che sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ des bdag go /de'i 'grel pa chos mngon
rin chen 'dren pa'i shing rta rgyal dbang mchog gis mdzad pa'i lung brgyud ni/ mdzad pa po/ mkhan chen sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ des bdag go ! /gnyis pa ni slob dpon klu sgrub
kyi dgongs pa thal 'gyur ba'i lugs srol thun mong ma yin pa slob dpon zla grags kyi gzhung dbu ma 'jug pa dang 'grel pa dbu ma theg chen rgya mtshor 'jug pa'i gru rdzings
kyi lung brgyud ni/ rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ des bdag go ! /bka' gdams gzhung drug la skyes tshoms dad

pa'i gzhung gnyis/ sa rgyan spyod pa'i gzhung gnyis/ bslab spyod lta ba'i gzhung gnyis las/ slob dpon rgyal sras zhi ba lhas mdzad pa'i bslab pa kun las btus pa'i lung brgyud
ni/ rgyal sras zhi ba lha/ mi brjed gzungs thob nas/ rngog lo yan 'og spyod 'jug bzhin las/ slob dpon blo gros 'byung gnas/ phywa pa chos seng / slob dpon bsod nams rtse
mo/ gcung grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa skya paN chen/ phyar phu ba byang chub dpal/ mkhan po bde ba dpal/ bka' bzhi grags gzhon/ byang sems bsod nams grags/ kun mkhyen bu/
yang rgyal sras zhi ba lha/ e la dha ri/ dpa' bo'i sde/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje/ 'brom ston pa/ po to ba/ sha ra ba/ blo gros grags/ dpal ldan gro mo che/ zhang btsun
chen po/ zhang ston chen po/ sangs rgyas sgom pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ bcom ldan ral gri 'di ru bla ma 'ga' ma rnyaid/ rab 'byams dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam dbyangs dbang
phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ bka' rab 'byams smra ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ des bdag go ! /rgyal sras zhi ba lhas mdzad pa'i byang chub sems
dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i lung brgyud ni/ ston mchog shAkya'i rgyal po/ lha mchog 'jam dpal dbyangs/ zhi ba lha/ paNDi ta mi brjed gzungs thob/ dze tA ri/ zla grags chung
ba/ puNya shrI/ bal po ka na ka pa/ su ma ti kIrti/ rngog lo/ zhang mdzes/ gtsang nag pa/ yang na rngog /slob dpon blo gros 'byung gnas/ phywa pa chos kyi seng ge /gtsang

pa dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims zhabs/ des bdag go ! /dpal gsang 'dus kyi

chos skor slob dpon Arya de bas mdzad pa spyod bsdus sgron ma lo chen 'gyur nas lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang byang sems blo gros rin chen/ klu sgrub/ ma tang
gi pa| ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA/ tshur ston dbang gi rdo rje/ 'khon gad pa kIrti/ rje bsod nams rin chen/ tshul khrims skyabs/ 'phags pa skyabs/ gser sdings pa
gzhon nu 'od/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen bu ston/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
/ sems dpa' chen po/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge /dbang phyug grub pa/ rje yongs 'dzin/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen/ de gnyis ka la bdag chen ngag pa/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/
mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ dpal sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ dwags pau slob dpon bsod nams rgya mtsho/ nges par gnas lnga rig pa rnam sras gling
pa dkon mchog chos grags/ des phrin las pa la'o/ /slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa'i 'khrungs rabs so bzhi'i lung brgyud ni/ rgyal ba zas gtsang sras po/ mgon po 'jam dbyangs/
'phags pa klu sgrub/ mkhas mchog dpa' bo| 'jam dpal grags pa/ shAnti pa/ se'u ri pa/ 'jigs med grags pa/ dge 'byung sbas pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che 'bring chung gsum/ chos
kyi bshes gnyen/ pu Nya shrI/ steng pa lo tsA ba/ so 'dzam gling rgyan/ lho pa kun mkhyen/ bla ma rgya/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje| 'di nas bla ma bcu tsam ma rnyed/ bka'
'gyur ba mgon po pu Nya/ bshes gnyen chen po rin chen rgya mtsho/ des bdag go /yang na/ slob dpon dpa' bo nas legs ldan 'byed/ zla ba grags pa/ rig pa'i khu byug ku mA
ra lakSha/ ha su ma ti/ dza ya A nanda/ khu lo tsA ba/ legs ldan pa/ gtsang nag pa/ gshen chu skor ba/ gtsang pa jo nag pa/ 'od

zer mgon po/ 'jam dbyangs shAkya gzhon nu/ rje rang 'byung rdo rje man 'dra'o/ /! snyan ngag mkhan kun gyi gtsug nor chos rgyal dge ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa'i byang chub sems
dpa'i rtogs pa brjod pa dpag bsam 'khri shing yal 'dab brgya dang bdun/ le'u gcig sras zla ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa dang bcas yal 'dab brgya rtsa brgyad ni dang po rgyal
po rab gsal sems bskyed do/ /rtogs brjod 'di rnams kyi lung khungs 'dul lung sman gzhi na'o/ /dA na sbyin pa ste sbyin pa'i phar phyin la/ gnyis pa mi bdag (dA)dpal mdo
sde sna tshogs nas sdes sku smad byin/ /(dA)gsum pa gtsug 'di nyid kyi mdo sde na na nor bus gtsug nor sbyin/ /(dA)bzhi pa 'dul ba sman gzhi dang mdzangs blun na nga las
nu yis lha mi bsdus/ /(dA)lnga pa sa skyong zla 'od sna tshogs mdo dang mdzangs blun na dbu byin no/ /(bI) bIrya brtson 'grus/ drug pa ba da ra gling nor bu blangs/ /bdun
pa mu tig sna tshogs mdo sde dang 'dul lung sman gzhi nas 'khri shing bris skus grol/ /brgyad pa khyim bdag sna tshogs mdo dang rma bya'i 'khrungs rabs na dpal sbas bden
pa mthong / /dgu pa me lung gzhi dang skyes dgra bcom 'dul ba phran tshegs na yan lag 'byung / /bcu pa mngal dkon brtsegs le'u bcu gnyis/ phran tshegs 'byung rga nad 'chi
srid bstan/ /bcu gcig mdzes dga' lung phran tshegs gzhi na rab byung chags bral gyur/ /bcu gnyis 'phags skyes po phran tshegs kyi gzhi ni dmyal bar skyes/ /bcu gsum 'phrog
ma la phran tshegs bam po zhe gcig na ni bslab gzhi gnang / /bcu bzhi cho 'phrul mdzangs blun dang phran tshegs bstan nas mu stegs btul/ /bco lnga gsal sna tshogs mdo
sde dang 'dul ba gzhi na ldan grong du lha nas babs/ /bcu drug brag gong 'phangs sna tshogs mdo sde dang 'dul ba sman gzhir nas gyad rnams btul/ /bcu bdun rgyal tshab byams
'dul lung sman gzhi na pa lung bstan no/ /(pra) pradznyA shes rab ste/ bco brgyad me long gdong gi 'dul ba sman gzhi na

khrims lugs bstan/ /bcu dgu shA ri'i bu yi 'dul lung rab byung gzhi dang mngon par 'byung ba'i mdor rnam thar gsungs/ /nyi shu gro zhun bye ba rna yi 'dul lung ko pags kyi
gzhir rabs/ /nyer gcig a ma skyong 'dul lung gso gzhi nas dang mdo mngon 'byung ma'i lo rgyus so/ /nyer gnyis rgyal byed tshal chen yongs 'dul ba gnas mal las su bzung /
/nyer gsum dkon brtsegs mngon 'byung yab 'dul lung sras mjal ba'i rtogs pa brjod/ /(dA)nyer bzhi thams 'dul ba sman gzhi dang cad sgrol dge 'dun dbyen gzhi na gyis legs spyad
rabs/ /nyer 'dul lung dbyen gzhi lnga ser skya'i gnas sna tshogs mdo nas mngon 'byung mngon rgya rol par byung / /nyer drug bdud tshogs lung dbyen 'dum mngon 'byung
mdor bcom nas mngon sangs rgyas/ /nyer bdun shAkya lung dbyen 'dum byung mngon 'byung mdor ba'i rgyal rabs skor/ /nyer brgyad gro zhun 'dul ba dbyen 'dum na bye ba nyi shu
pa/ /nyer dgu glang chen 'dul lung dbyen gzhi na nor skyong rjes su bzung / /(kSha) kShanti bzod pa ste/ sum cu ka shi mdzes 'dul lung dbyen 'dum dang ko'u di nya rtogs
brjod na pas bzod tshul bstan/ /(pra)so gcig ri dwags gser 'dul ba dbyen gzhi na logs chos 'khor bskor/ /(kSha)so gnyis mdzangs blun/ drin lan bsab pa'i mdo na dge byed
rgya mtsho'i nor bu len/ /(shI) shI la tshul khrims te/ so gsum khyad par lo mas g.yon 'dul ba dbyen 'dum na can bskyabs/ /so bzhi klu rgyal dga' bo lung rnam 'byed na nyer
dga' btul// so lnga khyim bdag legs byin bden pa mthong / /so drug khyim bdag gdangs sna tshogs mdo sde dang lung rnam 'byed na can mig rdul spangs/ /so bdun gang lung
sman gzhi na po'i bsod nams dus su smin/ /(shI)so brgyad lkugs pa 'phye lung sman gzhi dang rnam 'byed bo'i sngon rabs gsungs/ /(kSha)so dgu drang srong bzod pa lung gzhi
na la dga'i rabs/ /bzhi bcu ser skya nya lus lung gzhi dang rnam 'byed sogs na mgo bco brgyad/ /zhe gcig rgyal po u tra lung

rnam 'byed na ya na'i skabs/ /zhe gnyis mkhas pa zhes dri ma med pa'i mdo na bya dgra bcom mo// (dA)zhe gsum rgyal po gser mdog dri ma med pa'i mdo dang sna tshogs mdo sder
skyes pa'i rabs/ / (dA)zhe bzhi gser gyi lag pas dngul byin pa/ /zhe lnga ma skyes dgra dri ma med pa'i mdo dang lung dbyen gzhi na yis mtshams med byas/ /(kSha)zhe drug
lhas lung gzhi na byin byas shes lo rgyus so| |zhe bdun sa la'i sdong bu'i rgyu mtshan gsungs/ /(bI)zhe brgyad don grub nor lung gzhi na bus dbul 'phongs bsal/ /zhe dgu
glang can bu mo chos gos can/ /lnga bcu thub pas las bcu spyad tshul lo/ /(dA)nga gcig gser ldan mo yis nu sha byin/ /(dA)nga gnyis bsod nams mi dman g.yul 'khrug spangs/
/(pra)nga gsum legs bshad tshol gyis legs bshad nyos/ /(dhya)dhya na bsam gtan te/ nga bzhi rgyal bu sman gyis nad kun bsad/ /(dA)nga lnga thams cad ster gyis thams cad
byin/ /nga drug klu chen ba lang skyong zhes btul/ /nga bdun 'dren pas mchod rten bsngags pa gsungs/ /(dA)nga brgyad rgyal po bsod nams stobs kyi rtogs brjod na bsod nams
stobs kyi rabs/ /nga dgu ku lA la yis tshul khrims ku lA la yi rtogs pa brjod pa na bsrungs/ /drug cu klu gzhon rgyal bar lung bstan thob/ /re gcig zhing pa bkra shis sna
tshogs mdo sde dang sman gzhi na khyo shug grol/ /re gnyis grags byin nye ba'i dge slong ma'i rnam 'byed dang po na lnga sde'i 'khor/ /re gsum lung gzhi na 'od srung chen
po'i rnam thar ro/ /(dA)re bzhi rgyal po nor nor bzang rtogs brjod dang sman gzhi na bzang 'khor lo bsgyur/ /(dhya)re lnga thub pa rwa gcig lung dbyen 'dum na sngon byung
bstan/ / (pra)re drug gzhon nu snyan ngag lung dbyen 'dum na mkhan gyur tshul/ /re bdun dge 'dun lung gzhi'i bam po dgu na srung gis dmyal ba gzigs/ /re brgyad padma
ldan dang tshangs byin rabs/ /re dgu chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyi rnam thar na rab gnas so/ /bdun cu nyi ma gung

pas phran tshegs bam po sar na kha cher bzhugs/ /don gcig sha na'i gos can lung phran tshegs na bstan pa'i bdag /don gnyis mdzangs blun dang phran tshegs na nyer sbas bstan
pa'i bdag por gyur/ /don gsum klu la spring yig lung phran tshegs na tshong zong phul/ /don bzhi mya ngan med pas de nyid kyi rnam thar na sa gzhi phul/ /don lnga rten 'brel
bcu gnyis sgoms shig gsungs/ /don drug rgyal ngan be du ra yi skabs/ /don bdun ke ne lung gzhi na ya kas yang srid spangs/ /don brgyad brgya byin ltung ba'i 'jigs sna
tshogs mdo sde na las bskyabs/ /(dA)don dgu dbang chen sde sna tshogs mdo sde na dang 'tsho ba bde/ /brgyad cu rab bzang rab phran tshegs na dga' gdul bya'i mtha'/ /gya
gcig lung gzhi na rgyu yi mchog ces gsungs pa'o/ /gya gnyis dmyal ba mngon ldan 'dul ba dgra bcom gyi gzhi bam po gya gsum na srid pa'i go /gya gsum sgra gcan 'dzin 'dul
ba gzhi bam po dgu bcu na gyi rtogs pa brjod/ / gya bzhi sbrang rtsi'i dbyangs kyis durga lung gnas mal gzhi bam po don bzhi na btul/ /(dA)gya lnga phan pa tshol bas lung
dbyen 'dum bam po don bdun na rang rgyal gsos/ /(shI)gya drug ba men lung gzhi bam po don bzhi na ya rabs spyod tshul bstan/ /gya bdun padmo can gyis sna tshogs mdo sde
na gtum mo btul/ /gya brgyad nag mdo sde las brgya na pa glang brten sred pa zad/ /gya dgu chos lung sred chu srin chags bral bstan/ /dgu bcu nor 'dul ba can bu bcas bden
pa mthong / /(pra)go gcig shi bis sna tshogs mdo sde dang lung phran tshegs na legs bshad khrag gis nyos/ /(kSha)go gnyis mdza' bo'i bu mos 'jug 'dul lung gzhung dam pa'i
bam po so lnga dang / rtogs brjod brgya pa sems bskyed/ /go gsum ma gha dha bzang las brgya pa na mo yi rabs/ /go bzhi grags pa'i bshes gnyen rtogs brjod brgya pa na dgra
bcom mo/ /(dA)go lnga stag mo lus mdzangs blun na sbyin lo rgyus bcas/ /(dA)go drug glang po'i lung gzhi las srog gis blun

po bskyabs/ /(dA)go bdun ru sbal dka' thub lnga brgya grol/ /(dhya)go brgyad dka' las brgya na thub lnga brgyas dgra bcom thob/ /(dA)go dgu rgyal po padma can gyi skabs/ /brgya
phrag bsod nams rab las brgya dang rtogs brjod brgya pa na gsal smon sems bskyed/ / (dhya)brgya gcig sngo bsangs can lung sman gzhi na gyis pha ma bskyangs/ /(pra)brgya
gnyis seng ges lung sman gzhi na don mthun nyis 'bum bskyabs/ /(dA)brgya gsum dga' ba'i gong bur 'khrungs pa'i rgyud/ /(dA)brgya bzhi ri bong chos lung gzhi na kyi 'khor
lo bskor/ /brgya lnga re ba ti yis rgyu 'bras bstan/ /(bI)brgya drug gser gyi go cha 'khor lo bsgyur/ / (pra)brgya bdun khyim bdag zas gtsang legs bshad 'byin/ /(dA)brgya
brgyad sprin gzhon 'khor lo bsgyur rgyal thob/ /phar phyin drug gi ngos 'dzin rgyal dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i dgongs bzhed de/ de dag gi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ chos rgyal dge ba'i dbang po/ sras zla ba'i dbang po/ paNDi ta lakShmI kA ra/ shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ gcung blo gros brtan pa| dbon po chos skyong dpal/ spang
lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ lo chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bo dong paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ stag lung zhabs drung ngag dbang grags pa/
kun spangs rnam rgyal grags pa/ 'bum rab 'byams pa rin chen chos dbang / rab 'byams chos rje tshul khrims dbang phyug / dpal khang lo tsA ba/ mang thos chos kyi rgya mtsho/
mdo khams pa yon tan rgya mtsho/ 'bras spungs pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen pa'i rtse mo/ kun bzang rtse pa dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ g.yu lo bkod pa
rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ khu ston ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ dam pa'i chos kyi gan mdzod rin chen rgya mtsho'i sde/ des bdag go /yang na dpal khang lo tsA/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub
dbang rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen pa'i rtse

mo man gong ltar ro/ /lung spar ma'i steng nas zhus shing spar byang sogs rje rin chen rgya mtshos ma gsan pa/ slar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa
chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ zha lu mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ des phrin no/ /sa skya paNDi tas mdzad pa'i dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed chen
po dang thub pa'i dgongs pa gsal ba'i lung rgyud ni/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /sa skya bka' 'bum dang
'dra'o/ ! /dpal mnyam med dI paM kA ra shrI dznyA na'i thugs dam du mdzad pa'i chos chung brgya rtsara grags pa/ byang chub lam gyi sgron ma rgya gar gyi paNDi ta dI paM
kA ra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur 1/ spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma jo bos ne pA la'i yul du grogs po'i don du mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang nag tsho
lo tsA ba'i 'gyur 2/ bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa gser gling rgyal pos dge slong de wa ma ti btang ba'i ngor jo bos mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng
gi 'gyur 3/ dbu ma'i man ngag jo bo dang nag tsho lo tsA ba'i 'gyur 4/ snying po bsdu ba jo bo dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims 'byung gnas de ba rtsa'i 'gyur 5/ snying po nges
par bsdu ba jo bos snye thang du mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang nag tsho lo tsA ba'i 'gyur 6/ byang chub sems dpa' nor bu'i phreng ba jo bo nyid kyis sgra rang bsgyur
du mdzad pa 7/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams ngag du byas pa 'gyur byang mi gsal ba 8/ 'khor ba las yid nges par 'byung bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i glu jo
bo dang lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng ges bsgyur ba la slar yang nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas 'gyur bcos mdzad pa 9/ tshul khrims kyi spyod pa'i glu paNDi ta badzra pA Ni
dang chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 10/ chos kyi dbyings su

blta ba'i glu jo bo dang tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur 11/ dran pa gcig pa'i man ngag jo bos lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i ngor mdzad pa lo paN de gnyis kyi 'gyur 12/ byang
chub sems dpa' las dang po pa'i lam la 'jug par bstan pa jo bos lha bla ma byang chub 'od kyi don du mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i
'gyur 13/ skyabs su 'gro ba bstan pa 'gyur byang mi gsal ba 14/ theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs yi ge bsdus pa jo bo dang lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur 15/
theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs shin tu bsdus pa 'gyur byang gong 'dra 16/ rang gi bya ba'i rim pa bskul ba dang bcas pa yi ger bris pa 'gyur byang gong dang 'dra
ba 17/ mdo sde'i don kun las btus pa'i man ngag jo bo dang nag tsho lo tsA ba'i 'gyur 18/ mi dge ba bcu'i las lam bstan pa 'gyur gong 'dra 19/ las rnam par 'byed pa 'gyur
gong dang 'dra 20/ ting nge 'dzin tshogs kyi le'u jo bo dang dge slong shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur 21/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga 22/ kha ton dang glegs
bam bklag pa'i sngon du bya ba'i cho ga rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na kha ton dang glegs bam gnyis chos tshan so sor phral 'dug cing thar rtse sgrub khang shar pa gsum
gyi gsan yig na gcig tu mdzad 23/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa'i sAtstsha gdab pa'i cho ga 24/ bla ma'i bya ba'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa gong gsal bzhi po de la 'gyur byang
mi gsal 25/ sems bskyed pa dang sdom pa'i cho ga'i rim pa jo bo dang dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur slar yang paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal
bas bcos shing gtan la phab pa 26/ chos tshan nyer drug po 'di rnams dpal dI paM kA ra nyid kyis mdzad pa yin/ slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa'i byang chub sems
dpa'i sdom pa'i cho ga paNDi ta pu Nya shrI mi tra dang

lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyi 'gyur 27/ dpal mgon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i cho ga paNDi ta su rendra bo dhi dang bande ye shes sde'i
'gyur 28/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang yi dam blang ba'i cho ga mkhan po chen po su ma ti kIrti dang
lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na sems bskyed dang yi dam blang ba kha phral te angki yang so sor snang ngo 29/ slob
dpon mkhas pa chen po byang chub sems dpa' dgra las rnam rgyal gsang ba'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa'i las dang po pa'i sa sbyang ba slob dpon kr-iShNa pa dang lo tsA
ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 30/ des mdzad pa'i sems rin po che rnam par sbyang ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i springs yig A tsarya du lo pa dang lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab
kyi 'gyur dpe rnying pa 'dra na dgra las rgyal zhes pa las rnam mi 'dug pa rgya skad sor bzhag bsgyur ba 'dra ste slob dpon dze tA ri yin par mjug tu/ 'jam dpal rdo rjes
byin brlabs pa'i/ /dze tA ris mdzad gzhung 'di la/ /brten nas rang sems sbyang ba la/ /mkhas pa rnams kyis brtson par rigs/ /zhes snang bas bod skad la rnam bsnan pa legs
par mngon no 31/ slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i bshes pa'i spring yig slob dpon sarba dznyA de wa dang lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur 32/ mkhas
pa tsandra go mis mdzad pa'i slob ma la springs pa'i yi ge lo paN bshad ma thag pa'i 'gyur 33/ slob dpon ma ti tsi ma khol tras mdzad pa'i rgyal po ka ni ka la springs
pa'i yi ge paNDi ta bi dya kA ra pra bha dang lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gis bsgyur ba slar yang A tsarYYa dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa 34/ slob dpon don yod 'char gyis rgyal
po snyan ngag mkhan la gdams pa'i dri ma med pa'i dris lan rin

chen phreng ba zhes bya ba paNDi ta ka ma la gupta dang lo chen rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 35/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis dge slong rab gsal gzhon nu la springs
pa sarba dznyA de ba dang lo tsA ba bande dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur 36/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i shes rab brgya pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa lo paN
bshad ma thag pa'i 'gyur 37/ slob dpon btsun pa chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i dam pa'i chos dran pa nye bar bzhag pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon dharma
kA ra dang lo tsA ba gtsang de bendra rakShi ta'i 'gyur 38/ slob dpon mkhas mchog rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa slob dpon a dzi ta shrI
bha dra dang lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur 39/ btsun pa chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa paN chen buddha kA ra warma dang
lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 40/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i mya ngan gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon a dzi ta shrI bha dra dang lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi
'gyur 41/ slob dpon gsang ba byin gyis mdzad pa'i gzhon nu ma bdun gyi rtogs pa brjod pa 'gyur byang med pa 42/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i yon tan bdun yongs
su brjod pa'i gtam paNDi ta ganggA dha ra dang lo chen rin bzang gi 'gyur 43/ des mdzad pa'i tshul khrims kyi gtam slob dpon dza lan dha ra dang lo tsA ba rin bzang gi 'gyur
44/ des mdzad pa'i tshogs kyi gtam paNDi ta ganggA dha ra dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 45/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i mi khom pa brgyad kyi gtam
slob dpon a dzi ta shrI bha dra dang lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur 46/ slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa'i legs par bshad pa rin po che za ma tog lta bu'i gtam le'u brgyad
pa

slob dpon ru tra dang lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur 47/ slob dpon ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa'i phyin ci log bzhi spong ba'i gtam paNDi ta buddha bha dra dang lo tsA ba rin bzang
gi 'gyur 48/ des mdzad pa'i rtsod pa'i dus kyi gtam slob dpon a dzi ta shrI bha dra dang lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur 49/ slob dpon sa 'tsho byin gyis mdzad pa'i dben
pa'i gtam paNDi ta dI paM kA ra dang lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur thar rtse sgrub khang shar pa gsum gyi gsan yig na chos byin zer ba 'dug kyang dpe rnying pa
'ga' dang / rdo rje gdan pa'i gsan yig na 'di ltar snang 50/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i rin chen phreng ba las byung ba'i yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga tshigs
su bcad pa nyi shu pa 51/ des ba tshwa can gyi chu klung gi mdo las byung ba'i sems can mgu bar bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa bcu gcig pa slob dpon buddha kA ra warma dang
lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 52/ slob dpon btsun pa gzhan la phan pa'i dbyangs dgon pa bas mdzad pa'i smon lam bdun cu pa zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa paNDi
ta dharma shrI bha dra dang lo tsA ba dpal gyi lhun po'i sde'i 'gyur 53/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i don dam byang chub sems sgom pa'i rim pa rin po che'i sgron
ma zhes bya ba padma ka ra warma dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 54/ des mdzad pa'i kun rdzob byang chub sems sgom pa'i man ngag padma spungs pa zhes lo paN bshad
ma thag pa'i 'gyur 55/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdo las phyung ba'i 'phags pa sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa 56/ chos rjes su dran pa 57/ dge 'dun rjes su dran pa 58/
'dod pa'i yon tan rnam pa lnga'i nyes dmigs bshad pa dang bcas pa'i gzhi slob dpon dharma shrI bha dra dang lo tsA rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 59/ 'phags pa rtog pa chen po
yongs su rgyas pa'i mdo sde las byung ba'i sdig pa bshags

pa'i cho ga 60/ bslab pa kun las btus las byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i yi ge brgya pa'i bsrung ba dang sdig pa bshags pa'i cho ga slob dpon zhi ba lhas mdzad pa 61/ slob
dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa'i mdo sngags gnyis thun mong ba'i maNDal gyi cho ga 'gyur byang mi gsal ba 62/ slob dpon dgra las rnam rgyal gsang bas mdzad pa'i maNDal
'bul ba'i cho ga a du lo pa dang chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 63/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa'i pha rol tu
phyin pa'i theg pa'i maNDal gyi cho ga lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyi 'gyur 64/ slob dpon rnyog pa med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i maNDal gyi cho ga slob dpon a du lo pa dang lo
tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur 65/ slob dpon kaM ma las mdzad pa'i sngags kyi maNDal gyi cho ga 'gyur rnying 66/ slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa'i ting nge
'dzin gyi tshogs kyi le'u zhes bya ba slob dpon bi na ya tsandra dang lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 67/ slob dpon nag po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi
tshogs kyi le'u zhes bya ba paNDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 68/ slob dpon a ba dhU tI pas mdzad pa'i bsam gtan gyi chos drug rnam par bzhag
pa slob dpon dharma shrI bha dra dang lo tsA ba rin bzang gi 'gyur 69/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon dA na shI las mdzad pa 'gyur byang gong dang 'dra ba 70/ sa'i snying po 'khor
lo bcu pa'i mdo las byung ba'i gnas dang spyad par mi bya ba ste ting nge 'dzin gyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs rnam par bzhag pa rgya nag gi mkhan po hwa shang zab mo dang lo
tsA ba rnam par mi rtog pa'i 'gyur 71/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor rtog pa'i gegs sel zhes bya ba 'gyur rnying yin zhing
'di gsang

sngags yo ga'i rgyud la brten nas bshad pa 'dra zer ba snang ngo 72/ mkhas pa chen po byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor gyi mtshan nyid bden pa 'gyur byang mi gsal
ba 73/ slob dpon kA ma la shI las mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor sgom pa la 'jug pa slob dpon pradznya warma dang lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur 74/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi zhabs
kyi padma'i ze'u 'bru spyi bos len pa'i sde snod gsum pa slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor sgom pa'i lam 'gyur byang mi gsal ba 75/ slob dpon phyogs kyi
glang pos mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor la 'jug pa slob dpon dharma shrI dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 76/ slob dpon dge ba'i go chas mdzad pa'i mi sdug pa sgom pa'i rim
pa 'gyur rnying 77/ slob dpon nag po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i lus yongs su dpyad pa'i sgom pa'i rim pa slob dpon de nyid dang lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur 78/
slob dpon chen po dpal ye shes grags pas mdzad pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa sgom pa'i rim pa'i man ngag slob dpon padma kA ra warma dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i
'gyur 79/ dkyil 'khor chen po'i slob dpon mahA ma tis mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bla na med par sgom pa'i mdo'i rjes su 'gro ba zhes pa A tsarYYa bi na ya
tsandra dang lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di'i mjug tu mi mchog gang zhig gis ni zhes sogs tshig 'bru bcu gcig snang ba sus mdzad ma nges 80/ slob dpon chos kyi
dbang pos mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag slob dpon dza lan dha ra dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 81/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas
zhi bas mdzad pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sgom pa'i man ngag slob dpon shanti bha dra dang lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur 82/ slob dpon ye

shes zla bas mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor dpyod pa'i sgom don mdor bsdus te bstan pa slob dpon pradznyA warma dang lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur 83/ mkhas pa chen po dze tA ris mdzad
pa'i bde bar gshegs pa'i gzhung rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon shanti bha dra dang dge slong shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur 84/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad
pa'i yon tan bdun bstan pa'i gtam paNDi ta ka ma la gupta dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 85/ mkhan po zhi ba lhas mdzad pa'i bslab pa kun las btus pa'i tshig
le'ur byas pa 86/ de'i mngon par rtogs pa dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa paNDi ta de nyid dang nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur 87/ 'phags pa klu
sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i theg pa chen po nyi shu pa kha che A nanda dang lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur 88/ des mdzad pa'i 'phags pa sA lu ljang pa'i tshig le'ur
byas pa paNDi ta dharma shrI bha dra dang lo tsA ba legs pa'i blo gros dang dznyA na ku mA ra'i 'gyur slad kyi dpal brtsegs rakShi tas bcos pa 89/ des mdzad pa'i rten cing
'brel bar 'byung ba'i snying po'i tshig le'ur byas pa 90/ des mdzad pa'i rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i snying po'i rnam par bshad pa 91/ de gnyis la 'gyur byang mi
gsal/ des mdzad pa'i rmi lam yid bzhin nor bu'i gtam zhes pa kha che shrI rA tha dang lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur 92/ des mdzad pa'i byang chub sems kyi rnam
par bshad pa chos 'di'i mdzad pa po'i che ba dang brjod bya bzang ba dang rjod byed dbyings su gyur pa'i stobs kyis rtsal phyung zhing bsgyur ba mang du snang ba las lo
tsA ba rab zhi chos kyi bshes gnyen gyis bsgyur ba la gzhi byas gu rub chos kyi shes rab/ seng dkar shAkya 'od/ shes rab grags pa/ mar pa chos dbang / pa tshab nyi ma grags/
mang nang grags

'byor shes rab bdun gyi 'gyur la don gang bzang phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa 93/ des mdzad pa'i bla na med par bstod pa paNDi ta lo tra dang lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur 94/ des
mdzad pa'i srid pa las 'das par bstod pa kha che shrI rA tha dang lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur 95/ slob dpon dkon mchog 'bangs kyis mdzad pa'i yon tan mtha'
yas par bstod pa paNDi ta sarba dznyA de ba dang lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la bande dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa 96/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad
pa lo paN bshad ma thag pa'i 'gyur 97/ yang / des mdzad pa'i yon tan mtha' yas par bstod pa'i don gyi tshig le'ur byas pa lo paN bshad ma thag pa'i 'gyur 98/ slob dpon
thu btsun grub rjes mdzad pa'i khyad par du 'phags par bstod pa sgyur byed gong dang 'dra ba 99/ slob dpon bde byed bdag pos mdzad pa'i lha las phul du byung bar bstod
pa sgyur byed gong dang 'dra ba 100/ slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa'i skyabs su 'gro ba bdun cu pa jo bo rje dang lo tsA ba rin bzang gi 'gyur 101/ slob dpon bi mA

gsum gyis 'ching ba'i lugs bskur chog mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa'i steng nas rjes gnang thob/ lung dbu tshugs tsam/ sa chen ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams kyi zhabs
drung du thob/ rjes gnang dgu bcu go gnyis su mdzad pa'i lugs kyi bskur chog kun mkhyen rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa'i steng nas bum dbang yod pa'i rjes gnang dang lung thob

pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba yig sna nyis brgya dang bzhi bcu

tshig gsum bkod pa'i rgyal po'i sgrub thabs paNDi ta ku mu ta 'byung ba'i blo gros zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ de'i sgrub thabs rin chen 'byung gnas sbas pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad
pa'o/ /'di gnyis la lha mi gsal ba 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud nas lha kha bskang stai rjes gnang yod pa'i lugs so/ /rje btsun rdo rje gdan gtso 'khor gsum pa'i sgrub thabs man
ngag gi cho ga /de gsum la rjes gnang gcig /yang de'i sgrub thabs mi 'dra ba gnyis/ 'phags pa yi ge drug pa rig pa chen po dkar po phyag bzhi pa gtso 'khor gsum pa'i sgrub

gros zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon dge byed bde byed zer ba'ang 'dug kyis mdzad pa'i kha sarpA Ni lha lnga'i sgrub thabs/ dpal ldan mkha' spyod 'jig rten dbang phyug lha

sgrub thabs/ seng ge sgra'i sgrub
