bcad gcig 3/ snyan ngag rgyun chags 3/ sngags par 'os pa'i rab byed 2/ gang gi srid gsum ma 2/ rin chen dpa' shi la springs pa 2/ chang la bsngags pa'i rab byed bdud
rtsi bum pa/ chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta bde ba can du gshegs pa'i tshe dbus gtsang gi grwa pa rnams la gnang ba'i bka' shog 3/ gza' lnga/ lnga bsdus sgra gcan gyi rtsis
rin po che'i 'od zer 4/ dus gsal sgron me rgyas bsdus gnyis 7/ gdong gdod ma'i dus gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i rtsis 2/ rtsis kyi gtsug lag mthun par nges pa 2/ dhru
ba gnyis pa zhes bya ba'i rtsis 2/ lo bdag gi rtsis nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa 2/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i gtsug lag gi de kho na nyid rin po che'i sgron me zhes bya
ba dang / sangs rgyas bltams pa la sogs pa'i dus rtsis 9/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab 'gyur ro 'tshal bzhengs pa'i gsal byed sdeb sbyor gyi rgyan rnam par bkra ba 5/ chos
bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed/ tshogs gnyis rdzogs pa'i chu gter las 'khrungs zhes pa 3/ dam chos rin po che shin tu rgyas pa'i sde snod bzhengs tshul ston pa'i rab byed 3/
chos rin po che nye bar bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed thugs rje'i chu 'dzin legs 'ongs zhes pa 3/ gsung rab bzhengs pa'i mtshon byed

thugs rje'i thugs ni zhes pa 3/ gsung rab rin po che rnam par bkod pa'i mtshon byed ces bya ba 3/ yang / chos bzhengs tshul chos kyi dbyings las zhes pa 2/ chos bzhengs pa'i
mtshon byed nye bar bkod pa zhes bya ba 2/ bkra shis kyi skor rnams tshang bar bzhugs 17/ khyon 302chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po ches rin chen sgang bla brang du yab
sras gong ma bzhi dang 'phags pa rang gi bka' 'bum gyi phyed yan rdzogs mtshams su dus 'khrug langs pa'i de lhag rnams snar thang chu mig tu gsungs pa'i dus snga phyi
gnyis la lung nyan par yod pa dkon gnyer dpon dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gnyan phu ba kun rdor/ 'jam skya pa/ tshogs sgom pa/ zhang ston pa sogs kha yar la brgyud pa'i lung tshang
bar yod pa'i yab sras gsum gyi lung rnams tshang mar yod ces gsung ngo / /de ltar na rje btsun sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ chos rje sa paN/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa/ dga' ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang
ma ti paN chen/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ bla ma lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhar chen seng ge dpal bzang / brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan
pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ 'bri khung mkhan chen rnam mgon dri med sde/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ rab 'byams smra ba dpal ldan
don grub/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ chos rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ bla ma byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ rdo rje 'chang blo gros
dbang phyug /mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/ dge slong bskal bzang phrin las/ byams pa kun dga' bstan dar/ bslab

gsum rnam par dag pa khyab bdag byams pa phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag wA gindra la'o/ /skabs su bab pa'i yid ches ngo mtshar ba'i 'phros don/ rang gzhan gyi bzang rtog
spel ba cung zad bri'o/ /de yang / rdzong pa dang / ngor pa spyi mthun zhing / skabs 'dir rje btsun mu srad pa'i gsung las 'di skad du chos kyi rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan gyis/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge'i thugs dgongs rdzogs phyir du mkhan po shes rab rdo rje dang / dbus pa rin rgyal gnyis mnga' ris dbus rtsang khams gsum gyi
dgon gnas kun tu mngags nas/ rje btsun yab sras gsum gyi bka' 'bum/ lung yod pa kun las lung blangs te/ glegs bam dang dpe lung phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs so/ /zhes grags pas/
rje btsun bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan 'di nyid/ lugs srol 'di la bka' bsdu ba po yin no/ /de dag du ma 'dus pa phyis su/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos kyang slar
rnyed pa rnams kha skong bar mdzad pas shin tu bka' drin che ba yin no/ /zhes kho bo'i bla ma rnams gsung ngo / /chos rje khu dbon gyi bka' 'bum ni/ zhang dkon dpal nas
yongs su rdzogs par brgyud de 'ongs pas/ glegs bam dang dpe lung snga mo nyid nas phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs te gnas so/ /de la 'di skad ces bya ste/ ye daM gzhon tshul gsum
gsum las sa/ A daM mgon tshul dang sras rtse/ bar ma'i dang po rnam pa lnga/ bsod seng dpal rgyal gzhon bzang rje zhes gsungs so/ /de dag gi don ni/ mkhan chen sher rdor
bas rje sa chen gyi bka' 'bum bla ma gsum las lung blangs te/ de'ang bla ma ye shes dpal/ bla ma dam pa| byang chen pa gzhon tshul te gsum mo/ /rje rtse mo'i bka' 'bum
bla ma drug las lung blangs te/ bla ma a mo gha/ bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen gzhon nu mgon/ bla ma

gzhon tshul/ dang ma ba brtson 'grus byang chub/ sras kun rin te drug go /rje btsun gyi bka' 'bum bla ma bcu gcig las lung blangs te/ bar ma'i A mo gha/ bla ma dam pa/ gzhon
nu mgon/ gzhon tshul/ brtson 'grus byang chub ste lnga dang / rin po che bsod nams dbang phyug /bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /rgyal sras thogs
med/ bka' bcu gzhon nu seng ge /bla ma sangs rgyas rin chen te bcu gcig go |de la dkar chag gi rim pa shes par 'dod na mu srad pa rang gi yi ger gzigs/ 'dir ni gang las blangs
pa'i brgyud pa'i rim pa bri bar bya ste/ thog mar rje sa skya pa chen po'i bka' 'bum la/ (a)yi rtags can/ rgyud sde spyi rnam/ brtag gnyis bka' 'grel/ brtag gnyis bsdus
don/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi TI ka mu tig phreng ba/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi zin bris le 'grel/ bsdus don/ rtog bdun TI ka rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ bla ma sa skya pa
chen po/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ bla ma ye shes dpal/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ mkhan chen rgyal bzang pa/ mkhan chen byang seng pa/ theg
chen chos kyi rgyal po nas 'og nas gsal lo/ /yang / chos rje bla ma dam pa las theg chen pa nyid la brgyud pa/ (khi)yig gi rtags can/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug zhal gzigs dus
su bstod pa a la la ste ma/ rgyud sde'i dum bu brgya bcu gsum pa/ gur gyi tho yig /gur gyi bshad pa'i chings/ mngon byung gi rnam 'phrul/ gdan gyi rnam dag /gur gyi uShNI
Sha'i man ngag /kye rdor mtsho skyes kyi lo rgyus/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi zin bris/ mtsho skyes bskyed chog gi zin bris/ glu'i bshad pa/ rtsa'i mngon rtogs/ mtsho
skyes sgrub thabs sa bcad/ mtsho skyes mngon rtogs tshigs bcad ma/ rdo rje snying 'grel gyi yig sna/ nag po dkyil chog gi tho yig /nag po dkyil

chog sbyin sreg gi tho yig /sbyin sreg gi rnam bshad/ ro sreg gi tho yig /gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi tho yig /gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi gsal byed/ gsang ba'i de kho
na nyid kyi cha bla ma'i gsung gnang ba gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi bsdus don/ o la pa ti'i man ngag /o la pa ti'i bsdus don/ o la pa ti dang dpyid kyi thig le'i sngags
rims bsgom pa'i man ngag /rdo rje phur pa'i mngon rtogs/ las byang / phur pa'i mchod gtor bsdus pa/ bzlas pa'i man ngag /bsnyen phur bca' ba'i man ngag /gdon 'dul ba'i man
ngag /sangs rgyas lag bcangs kyi man ngag /sgron ma'i dbang chog gi bsdus don/ seng ge sgra'i bsnyen sgrub/ gtor ma'i rnal 'byor/ maNDal la brten te gzungs sgrub pa/ lha
'grub mi 'grub rmi lam brtag pa/ nad sos pa mi ldog par bya ba/ gdon 'grol ba'i cho ga bha ya na'i srung 'khor/ nam mkha' lding gi mngon rtogs bstod pa dang bcas pa rnams

dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ rje

gi brgyud pa ni/ sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ mchims chos seng / mchims blo brtan/ 'jam gsar/ rje btsun rgwa lo/ rong pa sher

seng / rin po che bsod nams grags pa/ bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen sher rdor nas gong bzhin/ yang / (khA)yig gi rtags can/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs/ de'i cha lag mkha'

bstod pa/ rim gsum 'thad ldan/ 'jigs byed kyi bstod pa/ bdag med ma'i bstod pa dri ma med pa/ gur gyi thig gi gsal byed/ rtsa ltung 'khrul spong / bla ma lnga bcu pa'i

byung tshul/ kun tu spyod pa'i bsdus don/ lU hi pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs

bsgom rim/ nag po dkyil chog /sgrub thabs sbyin sreg /de kho na nyid gsal ba/ o la pa ti ste lnga la sa bcad re re/ nag po pa'i lo rgyus dang spyi chings/ dgra nag gi mngon
rtogs/ phur pa'i sgrub thabs/ phur pa'i tho yig /gzhan phan 'od zer/ sbyong rgyud spyi don/ bsdus don/ dpung bzang gi mdo 'grel/ lag na rdo rje'i gzungs kyi lag tu blang
ba'i rim pa/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i TI ka /rgyud 'bum gyi dkar chag / las dang po pas lag tu blang bya'i rin chen phreng ba phyag yig dgu phrugs/ spyod 'jug bsdus don/
zhen pa bzhi bral gyi man ngag /shAkya'i rgyal rabs/ bod kyi rgyal po'i rgyal rabs/ sde pa'i gyes mdo/ 'khon gyi gdung rabs/ dus tshod nges par bzung ba'i yi ge /gza' skar

gi rtags can/ sgrol ma nyin zhi mtshan khro'i brgyud pa ni| rje btsun rin po che/ sa paNDi ta/ sher 'byung / ye rgyal/ dkon mchog 'byung gnas/ ye shes mgon po/ seng
ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen sher rdor nas gong bzhin no| |(nya)yig gi rtags can/ he ru ka'i chas drug /rab gnas don gsal/ gtor ma brgya rtsa'i rim pa rnams kyi brgyud pa
ni/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paNDi ta/ mdo sde dpal/ 'jam skya'o/ /bla ma dpal ldan pa/ mkhan chen sher rdor nas gong bzhin no/ / (ta)yig gi rtags can/ rdo rje 'byung ba'i
TI ka'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun rin po che/ sa paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ spru lung pa/ zhang dkon dpal/ slob dpon rin chen dpal/ bla ma rgyal po dpal/ rgyal sras
thogs med/ mkhan chen sher rdor nas gong bzhin no/ /(tha)yig gi rtags can gong du song la/ da ni bcu gcig pa/ (da)yig gi rtags can kye rdor bstod pa daNDa ka /dus mtha'i
cho ga gzhan phan bdud rtsi/ bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa bdun rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun grags pa/ sa skya paN chen/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ cog ro ston gzhon/
chos brtson/ bla ma sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen sher rdor nas gong bzhin te/ de ltar rje btsun dkar po rnam gsum gyi bka' 'bum/ bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen sher rdor/
theg chen chos kyi rgyal po rnams kyis bla ma mang po las lung blangs shing thams cad theg chen chos rje la 'dus/ de la

lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ rje btsun brag thog pa chen po/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po sogs so/ /chos rje khu dbon las/ 'jam dbyangs
sa paNDi ta'i bka' 'bum rnams ni| 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa la bka' babs te/ 'phags pa rang gi bka' 'bum dang bcas nas/ bla ma zhang dkon mchog dpal la byung
/ de nas/ rgyal ba brag phug pa chen po 'jam dbyangs don yod rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge / theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng
ge dpal/ chos rje brag thog pa chen po/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa chen po sogs so/ / 'on kyang rdo rje gdan pas rigs gter rang 'grel chos rje g.yag
pa nas brgyud pa bshad pa dang bcas pa gsan pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs sa paNDi ta chen po/ 'u yug pa rigs pa'i seng ge /'u yug pa mdo sde dpal/ gu ru 'jam dpal rgyal
mtshan/ spang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ brtson 'grus dpal/ dkon mchog grags/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas dpal/ bla ma kun dga' bzang
po/ bla ma shes rab dpal ldan/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa chen po/ yang / brtson 'grus dpal/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ bla ma kun dga' bzang po/ yang / sa paNDi ta/ 'phags
pa rin po che/ zhang dkon dpal/ brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ bla ma kun bzang / yang / bla ma dpal ldan tshul
khrims/ grub chen buddha shrI/ bla ma kun bzang / bla ma shes rab dpal ldan/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa chen po'o/ /de ltar 'phros don 'di rnams la'ang yig cha yod
med/ mtshungs mi mtshungs sogs khyad par cung zad tsam 'dug par/

slar zhib dpyod rigs shing / mdor na/ sa lugs thams cad bka' 'bum brgyud lugs khog gcig las gyes tshul/ rang lugs ni gong du bshad pa ltar yin zhing / sgyi chu ba'i lugs ni/
theg chen chos rje/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ bdag po dpal ldan chos skyong / rje btsun mu srad pa sogs dang / ngor lugs kyang mkhan chen byang chub seng ge /shar
pa ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rje ngor chen sogs so/ /'o na brag thog gsan yig sogs las/ gnyan phu ba kun rdor dang / sa bzang paN chen sogs 'dug pa rnams la don med do zhe na
ma yin te/ de'ang mu srad pas brgyud rim nges pa rnams la rtags mdzad kyi/ ma nges pa gzhan yang / lung rgyun yod la rtags med pa mang du 'dug pas/ de dag las sa bzang
sogs brgyud pa'ang yod thang bas/ thams cad dgongs pa mthun zhing ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su shes par bya'o/ /chos kyi rje rin chen rgya mtsho'i gsan yig na/ bla ma paN chen
bsod nams mchog ldan la/ sa paN gyi bka' 'bum nas po ti dza dzha nya gsum dang / 'phags pa'i po ti Ta Tha Da Dha ste bzhi rnams dang / slar brgyud pa bsre ba'i phyir du
bla ma paN chen nyid la ldab nas zhus pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan yan gong bzhin las/ de la 'jam dbyangs dpal ldan rdo rje/ rab 'byams dpal ldan
don grub/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ bla ma paN chen la bdag rin chen rgya mtshos zhus/ yang / lugs gcig la| 'jam dbyangs byang dbang / sngags 'chang tshe
bkras/ rab 'byams dpal grub bo| |brgyud pa 'di dag pa 'dra zhes/ chos rje nyi ma gling pa gsung zhes snang ngo / / brgyud lugs phyi ma dag pa ganggA'i chu rgyun na 'dug
pas cung zad spros/ zhabs drung bla chen dang bla chen ye shes dbang po nas brgyud pa gzhan dang gzhan dag na rgyas par

bris pa dang 'dir yang mthun no/ /rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims zhabs la zhus pa/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ mtshan brjod 'don thabs/ rnam 'joms rnam bshad bdud rtsi spel ba/ gang zhig
shing dbang / thub pa'i dgongs gsal/ sems bskyed chen mo/ zhen pa bzhi bral 'grel pa/ phyi nang gsang ba'i maNDal/ mtsho skyes kyi aShta'i tshigs bcad/ 'jam dbyangs dmar
ser sgrub thabs/ nyin zhag phrugs gcig gi gtor ma'i rim pa/ tshogs bdag bstod pa rnams kyi brgyud pa/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang shI la mangga
la pA da/ des bdag go /bla ma paN chen la chos rje rin chen rgya mtshos sa skya bka' 'bum gsan dus/ bdag ni nyi gling rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi dngul gdung bzhengs pa'i
thig rtsa dang gzungs 'bul ba dang thug pas skal ba mi bzang bar gyur to/ /dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi bka' 'bum pusta ka bcu gnyis nas lung phran
bu'i lam 'bras glegs bam pod nag ma gong du bris/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i srung 'khor bdud thams cad 'joms pa/ mngon rtogs dngos grub 'dod 'jo/ dkyil chog rgyud don gsal
ba chos phreng brgyud pa 'di'i tshab rdo rje chos legs rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bla chen kun rgyal/ theg chen chos rgyal/ rin chen seng ge dpal/
brag thog pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa nas rim par/ bla ma rdo rje grags pa/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ rdo rje 'dzin pa paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ chos
rje phrin las rnam rgyal/ byams pa bstan pa rgya mtsho/ bla ma rnam rgyal yar 'phel/ mkhan chen chos dbang rgya mtsho/ bla ma kun dga' chos 'phel/ chos rje phun tshogs

bdag go /mchod phreng mchod sprin rgya mtsho yang zhus/ brgyud pa 'og na'o/ /kye rdor mngon rtogs yan lag drug pa lam 'bras skabs na'o/ /rdo rje phur pa'i mngon rtogs rgyas
'bring bsdus gsum dang / dkyil chog rtogs par sla ba rnams kyi brgyud pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ brag thog pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ 'jam dbyangs

'phel/ phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ dge 'dun yar 'phel/ byams pa bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag wA gindra sh-I la dhwa dza la'o/ /bla ma u rgyan rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs dbang

ldan/ byams pa kun dga' dbang rgyal/ bka' drin bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag ngag ming la'o/ /mkhan chen zha lu pa la thob bo/ ! /spru lung pa kun dga' smon lam gyis

gsan/ des bdag la'o/ /rnam bshad nyin mor byed pa bzhin no/ /kun bzang rol pa'i dpung gnyen/ (pa)kun

rig gzhan phan snang ba mtha' dpyad dang bcas pa/ rje btsun rnams la zhu ba'i 'phrin yig brgyud pa 'og dang 'dra tshod las bdag gi bla ma phun tshogs chos 'phel gy-is kun bzang

rje la phyag 'tshal/ /bar ro/ /'bri gung mkhan chen rnam rgyal mgon po'i bka' 'bum las/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa'i rnam thar rin chen slar zhu phreng ba'i brgyud
pa ni/ snag dbon mdzad pa po/ mkhyen rtse tshe dbang kun mkhyen/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rin po che rnam rgyal dpal bzang / mkhas mchog rin chen rgya mtsho/
des bdag go /mkha' spyod gsol 'debs/ 'khor 'das bde skyid ma/ lo chen shes rab rin chen gyis rdo rje gdan pa la bstod pa slar zhu dpal ldan legs tshogs/ 'jam dbyangs

sel gyi brgyud pa ni/ mdzad pa po/ thugs sras shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rin po che rnam rgyal dpal bzang / rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/
des bdag go /yang / rnam thar ngo mtshar rin chen gter mdzod brgyud pa 'jam dbyangs byang dbang la mkhyen rtse tshe dbang kun mkhyen dang / slob dpon mkhyen rab rnam
rgyal gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis kar 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go /brtse ba can/ (pa)a la la ste ma/ tshangs gtsug
ma/ tshangs spyod ma/ srid bsgral ma/ chos rgyal ma/ gang gi blo gros/ legs rgyu dge tshogs/ (pa)srid gsum 'gro bla/ (pa)phun tshogs bslab gsum/ (pa)rgyal bdag g-i bla
mas dkon mchog sbyin pa'i drung du gsan/ de'i drung bdag gis thob ba kun 'dus/ dpal gang drin/ (pa)shes bya kun rig /lam 'bras phyag mchod/ gang gi mchod rdzas sogs/ thos
rgya ma/ phyogs bcu ma/ bdag ni ma/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gzungs/ mtshan bdag gi bla mas dkon mchog sbyin pa'i drung du gsan/ de'i drung du bdag gis thob brjod phan yon
dang bcas/ sgrol ma rtsa gcig lha mo la gus gsol gdab bcas/ lam lo rgyus bzhin yin 'dra bas phun tshogs chos 'phel drung bdag gis thob 'bras gsol 'debs kha skong dal 'byor
rnyed dka' sogs/ rgyal po mdo lnga/ nor rgyun ma/ khyim bdag zla ba bzang pos zhus pa/ 'chi med rnga sgra'i gzungs/ tshe mdo nas mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa oM gsum yod
pa/ (pa)brgyad stong pa spar ma nas so/ /byams bdag gi bla mas dkon mchog sbyin pa'i drung du gsan/ de'i drung bdag gis thob smon/ bdag bstod mang du thos pa rnams kyi
brgyud pa/ rje btsun gong ma'i bstod pa bka' 'bum dang 'dra'o/ /de lhag rnams bla ma u rgyan rgyal po/ 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims
bkra shis dang / rje

rin chen rgya mtsho/ bstan pa rgya mtsho/ bsod nams blo gros/ bsod nams rnam rgyal/ dkon mchog sbyin/ kun dga' bstan dar/ byams pa phun tshogs chos 'phel/ des bdag ngag ming
la'o/ /bka' drin mnyam med paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims gnyis/ de gnyis kas bka' drin du stsal lo/ /de gnyis las rtags med pa nyi gling rje dang / pa'i rtags can kun
bzang rtse paN chen no/ /'di dag gi lung rgyun nye bar mkho bas ha cang dar so che bshis bris pas ma lang ba lta bus skyon du song nas brgyud pa ma rnyed pa 'dra'o/ /! thams
cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa dang dbyer med pa nyi ma gling pa rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis dpal bzang po'i bka' 'bum mthong thos don ldan pusta ka gnyis kyi
chos kyi rnam grangs la phan pa gtso bor mdzad pa'i skor dang / bshad pa gtso bor mdzad pa'i skor gnyis/ dang po la mchog gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i rim pa dang / thun mong
gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i rim pa gnyis kyi dang po la/ dngos grub kyi rtsa ba bla ma la gsol ba gdab pa/ byin brlabs kyi rtsa ba yi dam la gsol ba gdab pa/ smin grol gyi
lam/ khrid kyi rim pa ste bzhi'i dang po la/ bla ma spyi la gsol ba gdab pa dang / bye brag rtsa ba'i bla ma la gsol ba gdab pa gnyis kyi dang po ni/ lam 'bras bla brgyud
mang 'dus gzungs/ lam 'bras bla brgyud la gsol 'debs/ de dag gi thugs rje la bskul ba/ kun rig brgyud 'debs/ gur lha gsum ma'i bla gzungs/ gnyan mgon bla gzungs/ shAkya'i
rgyal po la bstod pa/ bsnyen rdzogs bla gzungs/ rgyud sde man ngag bcas pa'i bla gzungs/ bsnyen rdzogs brgyud 'debs/ khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum gyi sdom bshags
dang bcas pa/ zhang dkon dpal gyi sku bstod do| |gnyis pa ni/ bla ma dam chos gling pa'i sku bstod/ bla ma gling stod pa'i sku bstod/

bla ma rnam rgyal chos gling pa'i sku bstod/ bla ma kun bzang rtse pa'i sku bstod/ bla chen rin po che'i sku bstod/ yang / sku skye rin po che'i sku bstod/ bla ma snang gsal
ba'i sku bstod/ bla ma mkhan gyi sku bstod/ slob dpon rdo rje blo gros kyi sku bstod/ bka' 'gyur ba chen po'i sku bstod/ zha lu mkhan chen gyi sku bstod/ bla ma paN chen
gyi sku bstod/ de dag gi thugs rje la bskul ba/ lam 'bras gsol 'debs 'don lugs rnams so/ /gnyis pa ni/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal la bstod pa'o/ / gsum pa la rnal 'byor bla med
dang / yo ga dang / spyod pa dang / bya ba'i rgyud de bzhi'i dang po la/ kye rdo rje'i mngon rtogs tshul bcu'i ngos 'dzin gsal ba'i sgron me/ kye rdor bum pa bcu'i sgrub
tshul/ slob dpon nag po lugs kyi kye rdo rje'i bdag 'jug /dus kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga'i zin bris/ yang / zin bris gcig /dus 'khor dbang bdun zin bris/ dka' gnad zin bris/
dus 'khor sku gsung thugs kyi thig rtsa rab gsal/ dus 'khor phyag rgya 'ching chog /gsang 'dus gnyis kyi zin bris/ gsang 'dus mchod phreng / sa lugs phur pa'i dka' gnad/
gshed dmar gyi mchod phreng zin bris/ 'jigs byed zhe dgu dang ro langs brgyad bskor gyi thig rtsa zin bris/ rnam 'joms 'bir lugs kyi tho/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i thig rtsa/
'khor lo bsgyur drug gi thig rtsa'o/ /gnyis pa ni/ rdor dbyings zin bris/ rdor dbyings slob ma rjes 'dzin/ kun rig zin bris/ kun rig sgrub mchod kyi sa gzungs/ kun rig
mdun bskyed rgyas pa| dpal mchog bum sgrub rgyas pa/ dbang sogs kyi zin bris/ gsum pa ni/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi rjes gnang lo rgyus dang bcas pa/ rnam snang mngon byang
thig rtsa 'khrul sel lo/ /bzhi pa ni/ mchod rten thig rtsa legs pa'i cha bsags so/ /

bzhi pa ni/ lam 'bras byin rlabs kyi tho/ khrid tshul thun grangs kyi sdom tshig /sgrol dkar tshe khrid dang bcas pa'o/ /gnyis pa thun mong gi dngos grub bsgrub pa ni/ ngag
lam brgyud ltar yin 'dra bas phun tshogs chos 'phel drung du lam 'bras skabs thob dang phreng ba byin brlabs/ kye rdor bsnyen pa rab gsal dam pa'i zhal gyi bdud rtsi/ kye
rdor dang gur zhal gyi bsnyen pa kha skong sbyin sreg /kye rdor thun mtshams kyi gtor ma'i rnal 'byor/ rab gnas sta gon zin bris/ kye rdor la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin re
ma'i chog khrigs/ rdo rje phur pa'i sbyin sreg zin bris/ las bzhi mgon po'i mngon rtogs bstod pa dang bcas pa/ rnam bdag gi bla mas kun bzang dbang 'dus drung du gsan/
de'i drung du bdag gis thob sras gtor chog /tshogs bdag gtor chog /phyi nang gsang ba'i maNDal gsal byed/ gtor ma brgya rtsa'i chog khrigs/ klu gtor/ phyag len sdom tshig
nyer mkho la/ ngag dang phreng ba byin rlabs rgyas pa/ rang bzhin brgyad cu'i rnam rtog dbye ba/ kye rdor lha mo brgyad kyi gdan gyi dag pa/ zhu 'bul gyi phyag gsum drug

can las rim par brgyud pa'o/ / mtha' can/ rjes gnang / mgor/ oM swasti/ srid gsum dbang bsgyur/ nas/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis sbyar ba'o/ /mtha' can/ gtor

mgor/ bla ma dang

nag po chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal gdong bzhi lcam dral la zla ba re re zhing dus bzang pa'o/ /nas/ gtor ma ma chag pa gal che'o/ /mtha' can/ rtsa sngags/ las sngags/
them yig ni/ mgor/ oM mahA kA la kA la/ bi ka Ta/ nas/ siddhi/ thog mar shri dang te'i bar na yi ge /nas/ sngags kyi them yig bstan pa'o/ /athi-i/ yang / oM swasti/ shrI
mahA' kA la pudzante/ nas/ ra tri ta hUM phaT swAhA/ mtha' can/ rten gzugs shing / mchod pa nas/ las kyi mjug bsdu bar yig sna bco brgyad dang / mdos chog /de dag gi mgor
mchod brjod/ mthar sbyar byang gi ris yod pa ni/ lha mchog mahA kA la mthu bo che dang / khyed la mthun pa'i dam rdzas 'bul ba ni/ /dang / dur khrod chen po'i gnas brgyad
dang / /rgya gar skad du/ mahA kA la tsa turmu kha ru ni/ dang / padma nyi ma ro steng du/ /dang / mi rtog dbyings nas thugs rje'i sku bzhengs shig /dang / rdo rje 'chang
dbang thugs kyi phrin las las/ /dang / 'jigs byed dpa' bo srid gsum g.yo/ /dang / dpal ldan dbang ldan srid gsum dbang bsgyur zhing / /dang / sangs rgyas thams cad gcig
bsdus pa/ /dang / srid gsum dbang bsgyur dpal ldan nag po che/ /dang / stong nyid snying rje'i bdag nyid sku/ /dang / mthu chen sdang ba'i dgra yi dgra/ /dang / sku gsum
mngon gyur rdo rje 'chang dbang gi / dang / rgyal ba kun gyi thugs las sprul pa'i sku/ /dang / nag po chen po mche ba can/ / dang / legs ldan nag po'i las byed pho nya'i
tshogs/ /dang / dpal ldan mgon po phyag bzhi pa/ /dang / thugs dam mdos kyis bskang ba ni/ /nas/ dgra phyogs su byas na the tshom med do/ /sa ma pa tha/ athi-i/ mtha'
can rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang chen po/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ gnyan lo tsA ba/ gnam kha'u pa rdo rje bdud 'joms/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob

tshul khrims bkra shis/ de'i bka' drin las phrin las pa'o/ /gur lcam dral ltar sbags te sgrub pa'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum ni/ mgor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la gus pas phyag

byang seng pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ mkhan chen lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' rnam
rgyal/ 'bri khung mkhan chen rnam rgyal mgon po/ 'jam dbyangs byang chub dbang rgyal/ sngags 'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma rnam rgyal bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs dbang

bzang pa'ang 'dug /gzhan yang brgyud srol gnyis tsam yod/ yang gur mgon lha gsum sbags bsgrub ni/ mgor/ oM swasti siddhaM/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/
/dpal nag po chen po lcam dral gyi mchod gtor/ nas/ 'phags pas bris nas jim gyin la phul ba'o/ /mtha' can dang / 'di'i lung thos

btags ma/ gur gyi mdos chog gnam lcags 'bar ba/ mgon po rnam rol la mkho ba'i thig rtsa smras so'i mtha' can/ gri gug lha lnga thun mong min pa'i zur 'debs zhal bzhi
pa'i gtor chen dang pu tra ming sring ru 'dren dang bcas pa'i 'chams yig lag len la 'dris par bya'o/ /mtha' can/ de dag gi lung thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mdzad pa po thams

can/ mgor/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// nag po chen po gdong bzhi pa'i phrin las bsgrub pa'i/ nas/ sngags 'chang kun dga'

bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos pho brang ta'i tu'i hA'i sde chen por sbyar ba'o'i/ mtha' can/ mgor/ 'khor 'das bde skyid ma lus 'byung ba'i gnas/ /nas/ dge bar gyur
cig /mtha' can/ brgyud pa gur pod bzhin/ (na)! chos tshigs kyis phye ba'i yul dbus bod gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir/ sems can gyi don du phebs pa'i mkhas grub dam pa rnams kyi
bka' 'bum las/ lung phran tshegs thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ chos skyong ba'i rgyal po srong btsan sgang po'i ma Ni bka' 'bum stod cha smad cha la pusta ka re mnga'
ris rdzong dkar gyi spar ma'i steng nas yongs rdzogs la/ brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bka' 'bum bskor gsum gyi sa bcad kha byang dang bcas pa/ mdo skor zhes pa zhal gdams
lo rgyus chen mo| sgrub thabs phran tshegs las tshogs sum cu rtsa drug /sum skor rtsa ba cig skor/ bshad thabs kyi yan yag lag dang bshad 'grol chen mo/ rgyal po'i skyes
rabs nyi shu rtsa gcig pa/ chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po'i zhal gdams/ chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po rgyal bu 'jig rten dbang phyug tu skye ba bzhes pa/ rgyal po yab yum
thugs kar thim tshul/ thugs rje chen po'i las tshogs te mdor na stod cha smad cha zhes pa'i po ti gnyis la dbu shog lnga yod pa mya ngan dang bral bar gyur to'i bar kyi

btsan sgam po/ thu mi saM bho Ta/ grub

thob myang dngos grub man 'dra'o/ /sprul sku myang ston/ ras pa mi bskyod rdo rje/ bla ma shAkya bzang po/ lha rje dge ba 'bum/ lcam ye shes mchog /chu sgom zhig po/ mtha'
bzhi bya bral/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams seng ge /bla ma bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ bla ma blo gros rgyal mtshan/ 'phags mchog nor bu bzang po/ mkhas grub rgyal mtshan bzang po
'di la ma Ni bka' 'bum na nye brgyud ring brgyud gnyis kar bzang po rgyal mtshan yod pas brtag / 'khrul zhig mdo sngags paN chen/ mkhas grub rnam rgyal rin chen/ 'jigs med
nam mkha' don grub/ bla ma u rgyan rgyal po/ mtshungs med lha dbang phrin las/ rigs kun khyab bdag paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ des bdag go ! /nyang gi gter ma nas shog
bu bcu gcig thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mtshungs med lha dbang phrin las/ rdo rje 'chang tshul khrims bkra shis/ des bdag go ! /jo bo rje'i sku bstod phun tshogs bhangga
la 'brom ston gyis mdzad pa'i lung zha lu mkhan chen pu Nya zhabs drung du zhus/ ! rgyal sras chen po thogs med bzang po dpal gyi bka' 'bum nas thor bu gcig tu bsdus pa spar
ma pusta ka gcig gi lung sha lung nas gnas lnga rig pa byams pa bsod nams phun tshogs la zhus/ ! mthu stobs kyi mnga' bdag grub pa'i dbang phyug rwa lo rdo rje grags
pa'i lugs kyi rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rwa pod du grags pa'i chos sde'i rnam grangs la| rtog bdun/ nag 'grel/ dkar 'grel/ bcud thigs/ bsnyen sgrub dgra srog dbang bsdud/ mngon

sreg /dbang chu/ dmar po mda' gzhu 'gengs pa/ rwa pa'i chos brgyad/ rtog bdun man ngag bdun pa/ shog dril gsum gyi gdams pa/

rdor grags/

rdum/ rwa rdo rje grags/ ye shes seng ge /'bum seng / de nas rtsad gcod gsung / rwa lo'i nyams mgur chos brgyad/ rgya ston gyi bsrung bzlog bsad gsum gyi man ngag /rtsa

bkra shis

rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' bkra shis/ dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen puNya zhabs/ des bdag go /yang na/ kun mkhyen bu/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra shrI man gong ltar ro/
/yang na/ bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan chos bzang / dbu mdzad rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen puNya ba ra siddhi/ des bdag go /gsang 'dus rgyud 'grel gsol 'debs bla

chos skor spros med kyi gzhung rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i gzhung 'grel 'od gsal 'char ba'i rim pa'i byin rlabs kyi 'grel pa 'jug bde gsal ba'i brgyud pa/ kun mkhyen
bu/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man gsol 'debs bla ma'i yon tan rjes
dran ltar ro/ /! rnal 'byor rgyud kyi skor ma lus pa thob pa las/ thog mar/ rnal 'byor rgyud kyi bshad thabs kyi yan lag rnam par bzhag pa rnal 'byor rgyud kyi rgya mtshor
'jug pa'i gru rdzings kyi lung brgyud ni/ kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub/ gu ru dpal mchog don grub/ mkhas mchog tsandra shrI ratna/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal
mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man gsol 'debs bla ma'i yon tan rjes dran ltar ro/ /rdor dbyings dkyil chog rdo rje thams cad 'byung ba'i rgya cher bshad pa yid bzhin nor bu'i
brgyud pa/ kun mkhyen bu/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra shrI/ slob dpon shar chen ye shes rgya mtsho/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ dbon rgyal ba/ don grub rgyal mtshan/ bkra shis
rgyal mtshan/ dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen puNya ba ra siddhi/ des bdag go/

de nyid bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus don de nyid snang ba'i rgyan dmar nag dang bcas pa'i lung brgyud ni/ kun mkhyen bu/ rgyal ba mchog grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal
mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ bla ma'i yon tan rjes dran ltar ro/ /yang na kun mkhyen bu/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra man 'dra'o/ /rdor dbyings dkyil chog rin chen bsam
'phel gyi brgyud pa/ bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /dkyil chog gi lhan thabs sgrub mchod sbrel ma byed thabs shog gcig ma'i lung brgyud/ gong ma tshol/ bkra shis rgyal mtshan
man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /'di ma thob/ rdor dbyings 'grel lugs kyi dbang chog rgyas pa'i kha skong gsal bar ston pa mgron thabs kyi lha sangs rgyas stong
du bzhis ma tshang ba'i bstod pa/ gsang ba yum bzhi'i mchod gar/ rdor dbyings mchod phreng bla med mchod sprin/ rdor dbyings zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg bsod
nams dpal 'bar/ dbang gi sbyin sreg /drag po'i sbyin sreg /gzhal yas khang gi gnas lugs gsal byed/ rdul tshon spyan drang ba'i cho ga /rab gnas bkra shis rgyas byed/ de'i
sdom tshig gsan tshe brgyud pa 'di ka /de'i sdom tshig /rdor dbyings 'grel lugs kyi dbang chog rgyas pa'i kha skong rnams kyi lung brgyud/ bde mchog chos 'byung ltar
ro/ / mgron thabs kyi lha sangs rgyas stong du bzhis ma tshang ba'i bstod pa'i lung brgyud lugs gcig ni/ bkra shis rgyal mtshan yan 'dra ba las/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen puNya/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen chos legs/ des bdag go /yang / rab gnas bkra shis rgyas byed lugs gcig ni/ bkra shis rgyal mtshan
yan gong ltar las/ kun dga' bkra shis/ lha bo rin chen rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen puNya man 'dra'o/ khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dkyil chog 'jig rten

gsum rgyal 'byung ba dang / bshad rgyud rdo rje rtse mo rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil chog mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog /rtse mo'i sa chog rgyas pa mchan dmar nag gsum dang bcas pa'i lung
brgyud/ kun mkhyen bu ston/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /zhang zhung mang nang pa
nas brgyud pa'i rig ma bcu drug gi mchod gar lung brgyud bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /rtse mo la mkho ba'i phyag rgya'i rgyud tshig logs su phye ba/ mkhan chen gsan
yig na med pas phyag rgya zhe brgyad pa'i sdom tshig la lung yod med dpyad/ dpal mchog rigs bsdus kyi dkyil chog don yod pa'i dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor 'byung ba/ dpal mchog
rigs bsdus bstod tshan pa gsum yod chen/ dpal mchog rigs bsdus pa'i rdo rjes sgrub pa rnams kyi lung brgyud/ bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /yang na thugs sras rin rnam/
dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra man gong ltar ro/ /yang / dpal mchog rigs bsdus dkyil chog brgyud lugs gcig /kun mkhyen bu/ rgyal ba mchog grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims
rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man gong ltar ro/ /yang na/ kun mkhyen bu nas/ shar chen slob dpon ye shes rgya mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam
rgyal/ bar 'dir bla ma gsum tsam dpn: ma rnyed/ gra thang mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ paN chen dpal ldan tshul khrims/ mkhan chen puNya zhabs/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen
chos legs/ des bdag go /dpal mchog gi thig rtsa'i lung brgyud ni/ kun mkhyen bu/ rgyal ba mchog grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man
bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /lha mo bcu gnyis kyi mchod gar/ gsang ba yum bzhi'i mchod gar gnyis kyi lung brgyud/ bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /yang

na thugs sras rin rnam/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra man 'dra/ dpal mchog rdor sems dkyil chog dam tshig chen po'i de kho na nyid 'byung ba/ dpal mchog rdor sems zhi ba'i sbyin
sreg dge zhing zhi byed/ rdo rje sems dpa' myur du sgrub mchan la lung med pa'i bde ba chen po'i rnam par 'phrul pa rmad du byung ba/ dus tha ma'i cho ga thar pa'i grong
'jug rnams kyi bkra shis gcig 'dug par lung byung yang / mkhan chen gsan yig na mi 'dug pas brtag lung brgyud kun mkhyen bu/ rgyal ba mchog grub/ mkhas pa tsandra/ tshul
khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man gsol 'debs bla ma'i yon tan rjes dran ltar ro| |yang / zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /dus mtha'i cho ga gnyis kyi lung brgyud ni/
kun mkhyen bu| thugs sras rin rnam/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan/ tsandra shrI man 'dra/ dpal mchog lha'i bkra shis tshigs bcad bkra shis 'phel byed lung brgyud/ bde mchog
chos 'byung ltar ro/ /kun rig dkyil chog las sgrib rgyun gcod/ kun rig kha skong mchod phreng / 'khor los bsgyur ba'i skabs nas gsungs pa'i shaM pa ta'i gar dpe/ sbyong
rgyud me ltar 'bar ba'i skabs nas gsungs pa'i kun rig zhi ba'i sbyin sreg sdug bsngal zhi sdig pa zer byed/ rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg /dbang gi sbyin sreg /tshe dpag med kyi
skabs nas gsungs pa'i drag po'i sbyin sreg /kun rig skabs nas gsungs pa'i ro sreg cho ga sdig pa zhi byed rnams kyi lung brgyud/ bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /yang / ro
sreg gi cho ga sdig pa zhi byed kyi brgyud lugs gcig ni/ kun mkhyen bu/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra shrI man 'dra'o/ /gtsug dgu'i dkyil chog ngan song rgyun gcod lung brgyud/
kun mkhyen bu/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan nas rin chen chos legs yan dpal mchog ltar/ 'di'i bar kha shas ma tshang / kun dga' brtson
'grus/

bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ des bdag la'o/ /mkhyen rab chos rje man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro| |phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dkyil chog 'chi med grub pa/ de'i lha
tshogs la bstod pa/ rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa'i dkyil chog las sgrib rgyun gcod/ de la brten pa'i ro sreg cho ga rnams kyi lung brgyud/ bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /mi 'khrugs
pa'i dkyil 'khor la bstod pa lung byung yang mkhan chen gyi gsan yig na mi 'dug pas dpyad/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad
pa'i bsdus don nyung ngu rnam gsal mchan bcas lung brgyud/ kun mkhyen bu/ rgyal ba mchog grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man bde mchog
chos 'byung ltar ro/ /chos dbyings gsung dbang dkyil chog mkhas pa'i dga' ston/ kun mkhyen bu/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab
chos rje/ byang gling dbon rgyal ba/ 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' bkra shis/ dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen
puNya/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen chos legs/ des bdag go /de'i dkyil 'khor la bstod pa bde ba las 'khrungs kyi lung brgyud/ kun mkhyen bu/ thugs sras rin rnam/ sku zhang nam
mkha'i mtshan/ mkhas pa tsandra man bshad ma thag pa ltar ro/ /rnam snang mngon byang dkyil chog sngags 'grol mchan bcas lung brgyud/ kun mkhyen bu/ mkhan chen grags gzhon
pa/ mkhan po grags rgyan pa/ yon tan dpal/ blo bzang pa/ mkhyen rab chos rje man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /mchod rten sgrub pa'i cho ga byin rlabs dpal 'bar gyi
lung brgyud/ kun mkhyen bu/ thugs sras rin rnam/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan/ bla ma don grub legs pa/ tshul khrims

rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /dpa' bo gcig sgrub rgyud la brten pa'i gnod sbyin pho mo'i 'khor lo bri thabs brgyud pa/ gong ma tshol/
bkra shis rgyal mtshan man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /gar mkhan mchog gi rgyud la brten pa'i rnam sras kyi sgrub thabs dgos 'dod 'byung ba/ gsang bdag gos sngon can
la spro ba lnga'i sgo nas bstod pa/ rnam sras zhi drag gnyis kyi rjes gnang rnams kyi brgyud pa kun mkhyen bu/ mkhas grub bsod nams 'phel ba/ stag tshang lo tsA shes rab
rin chen/ yab rin chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mai tri don grub rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos kyi rgya mtsho/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ mkhan
chen puNya zhabs/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen chos legs/ de gnyis kas bdag go /yang na dbang phyug rab brtan yan gong bzhin la/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ sa skya
khri chen kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam mgon sa skya pa bsod nams dbang phyug / mkhan chen puNya/ des bdag go /yang na kun mkhyen bu/ thugs sras rin rnam/ sku zhang nam mkha'/
tsandra shrI/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje nas/ rdo rings pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen man 'dra'o/ /yang / gos sngon can gyi bstod pa dang
zhi drag rjes gnang gi lung brgyud lugs gcig ni/ mkhyen rab chos rje yan gong bzhin/ gzhon rgyal ba/ don grub rgyal mtshan/ bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' bkra shis/ dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen puNya/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen chos legs/ des bdag go /'khor lo'i bri yig brgyud pa/ gong ma tshol/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan
man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /rnam sras bstod chen rgyal po'i thugs rab tu mnyes par byed pa'i le'u bcu gcig brgyud pa/ rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug

rab brtan yan dgos 'dod 'byung ba bzhin/ rdo rje 'chang bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen puNya zhabs/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen chos legs/ des bdag go /'dul
ba'i las chog dang / zhar byung khyim pa la phan 'dogs pa'i lag len gyi cho ga dri ma med pa'i phreng ba'i brgyud pa/ kun mkhyen bu/ slob dpon bsod nams dpal grub/ nor
bzang rin chen/ rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ lo tsA ba chos skyong bzang po/ sa lo 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ chos rje dkon mchog lhun
grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhan chen dpal ldan don grub/ bka' 'gyur ba mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mkhan chen rin chen
bsod nams mchog grub/ des phrin las pa la'o/ ! /bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa'i gsal byed chos kyi 'byung gnas gsung rab rin po che'i gter mdzod kyi lung brgyud/ kun mkhyen
bu/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ nor bzang rin chen/ bka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje man bde mchog chos 'byung ltar ro/ /bu ston snying gi
thur ma'i lung brgyud dang / rgyud 'bum dkar chag dang / bka' 'bum dkar chag rnams kyi lung brgyud ni/ gong ma ma rnyed/ byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ kun dga'
bkra shis/ rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen puNya zhabs/ rdo rje 'chang rin chen chos legs bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ des bdag phrin las rnam rgyal la dgyes pa chen
pos stsal lo/ /'dul ba'i zhe sa dgu phrugs kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa slar 'tshol/ ! thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i rnam sras gtor chog dgos 'dod 'byung
ba'i zhal shes kyi lung mkhan chen zha lu par thos/ ! sku zhang mkhyen rab rin

chen mchog grub kyi bka' 'bum gyi khrod nas lung thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ sems nyid ngal gso'i brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bde mchog lU hi pa'i rdzogs rim brgyud 'debs/
nag po rim bzhi'i brgyud 'debs/ dril bu lus dkyil dbang bka'i brgyud 'debs/ dril bu rim lnga'i brgyud 'debs/ bde mchog dkar po'i brgyud 'debs/ ni gu chos drug brgyud 'debs/
su kha chos drug brgyud 'debs/ dmar khrid brgyud 'debs/ phyag drug pa'i brgyud 'debs/ rje nyid kyi rnam thar mthong ba don ldan/ sbyor drug khrid yig /lam 'bras khrid
yig /rtsa dbu ma'i khrid yig / lo yi lU hipa'i khrid yig /dril bu rim lnga'i khrid yig /de'i byin rlabs/ nag po rim bzhi dang dpyid thig gnyis kyi khrid yig /spros med
rgyun gyi rnal 'byor/ su kha chos drug khrig yig /de'i byin rlabs/ tshe khrid rin chen gter mdzod kyi nyams len/ dmar khrid thugs rje chen po'i 'pho ba/ gcod khrid nam mkha'
sgom byed/ nyams 'gyur/ dge slong gi nyams len mdor bsdus/ sgom bde rab 'byams par zhal gdams/ rdzong chen tshe sgrub/ mgon rkyang rjes gnang / dus 'khor sgrub dkyil/
thugs dkyil/ sgrub thabs bsdus pa rnams kyi lhan thabs re re/ kye rdor mngon byang lnga'i gnad bsdus/ lo yi lU hi pa'i sgrub dkyil lhan thabs/ lus dkyil lhan thabs/ nag
po pa'i lhan thabs/ sdom 'byung gi lhan thabs/ padma dra ba'i lhan thabs/ rdo rje phreng ba'i lhan thabs rin po che'i phreng ba/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i lhan thabs/ mchod
phreng / gshed dmar lha lnga'i lhan thabs/ phyag rdor 'khor chen lha bco brgyad kyi lhan thabs/ gshen po rjes 'dzin/ kun rig lhan thabs/ 'chi med rnga sgra'i lhan thabs/
ras chung lugs kyi tshe dbang bskur tshul/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang byed tshul/ rta mgrin

nag po'i rjais gnang gi tho/ rta mgrin sgyer skyer sgang lugs kyi tho/ 'jam dbyangs dkar po'i sgrub thabs/ spyan rab ras gzigs kyi sgrub thabs/ seng mdong gdong ma'i sgrub
thabs las tshogs/ man ngag kha shas dang bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub don yod rgyal mtshan/
mkhas btsun bsod nams lhun grub/ mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag go !
/mkhyen rab chos rje'i rnam thar rgyas pa/ 'gos lo tsA ba chos skyong bzang pos bsgrigs pa mkhyen rab chos rje nyid kyis lung gnang ba'i brgyud pa dang / myang 'das rnam
thar 'jam dbyangs chos rjes mdzad pa dang / rnam thar gsol 'debs stong ra ba kun dga' legs grub kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ shAkya
don grub/ stong ra ba kun dga' legs grub/ kun dga' chos grags/ mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ des bdag la'o/ ! /'jam
dbyangs chos rjes mdzad pa'i yig bca'/ rdo rje rab brtan ma'i gtor chog 'dod rgu'i dpal ster dang / bstod pa bdud dpung zil gnon 'dod rgu'i dpal ster/ phyag na rdo rje
'gro bzang lugs dang / rnam sras zhi drag 'brel ma rnams kyi phyag len yang dag pa zhes bya ba le tshan gnyis/ rnam sras kyi dkar chag rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs
chos rje/ don yod rgyal mtshan sogs rdo rje rab brtan ma'i gtor chog dang 'dra/ rnam sras ser chen gyi yig cha kun mkhyen bus mdzad pa'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ bu ston
thams cad mkhyen pa rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan can/ rin chen

dpal grub/ mkhyen rab rje/ 'jam dbyangs chos rje/ rje don yod rgyal mtshan man gong 'dra/ rnam sras zhi drag gi bstod pa thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i yi ge
ma mo las spel ba gnyis kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thugs sras rin po che man gong 'dra'o/ /! mnyam med ri bo dga' ldan pa'i bka' 'bum skor nas rje btsun tsong kha
pa chen po blo bzang grags pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa'i lam gyi gtso bo rnam gsum bsdus pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slar bri/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i
bka' 'bum nas drang nges rnam 'byed kyi dka' 'grel/ mtshan brjod TI ka / sgrol ma rtsa gcig TI ka rnams kyi lung brgyud ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ se
ra rje btsun chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan khri pa/ dge 'dun rgyal mtshan/ paN chen rin po che blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang
rgya mtsho/ rje ngag dbang blo bzang / mkhan chen sbyin pa rgya mtsho/ des bdag la dgyes pa chen pos stsal lo/ ! /hrIH dus gsum gyi rgyal ba ma lus pa'i thugs rje'i ngo
bo thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho 'jigs med go cha thub bstan lang tsho'i sde'i bka' 'bum mthong grol chen mo nas pusta ka bcu gsum tsam gyi lung thos
pa'i chos tshan la sngon chad go rim nges pa'i dkar chag mi 'dug pas/ 'dir chos tshan gyi go rim rang gi sgra 'dzin gyi bdud rtsir ji ltar babs pa rnams brgyud pa dang
bcas pa la/ gsung ba po'i rtogs pa brjod pa/ gang du gsungs pa'i gnas/ gang gi phyir gsungs pa/ gang gsungs pa'i chos te bzhi'i dang po la gang du sku bltams pa la sogs
pa thun mong du grags pa'i rnam thar dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i rnam thar/

gsan sbyong mdzad pa gsum gyi dang po ni/ rnam thar du ku la'i gos bzang glegs bam me 'brug zla 2tshes 1bsod nams chos 'dzom yan gnyis kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bstan
pa'i bdag po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho'i zhabs/ rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ rje ngag dbang nam mkha'/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ des bdag phrin las rnam rgyal
la dgyes pa chen pos bstsal to/ /gnyis pa ni ches shin tu gsang ba'i rnam thar pusta ka gcig /gsum pa la gnyis kyi dang po mi'i bla ma la gsan pa dang / lhag pa'i lha
la gsan pa gnyis kyi dang po ni/ (ga)gsan yig ganggA'i chu rgyun pusta ka bzhi'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal dbang zhabs/ rje 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ des bdag go / gnyis pa ni
ches gsang ba'i rnam thar na gsal/ gnyis pa ni lugs gnyis kyis mngon par mtho ba dga' ldan pho brang dang / rang byon 'phags pa'i gtsug lag khang dang / sog yul/ rgya nag
la sogs pa'o/ /gsum pa gang gi phyir gsungs pa la/ bka' drin dran pa'i phyir gsungs pa dang / gdul bya so so'i ngor gsungs pa gnyis kyi dang po ni/ bla ma lnga bcu pa
las/ dbang bskur mchog thob rdo rje yi/ /slob dpon la ni de bzhin gshegs/ /phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten khams bzhugs pa/ /dus gsum du ni mngon phyag 'tshal/ /zhes dang / he badzra
las/ dngos grub thob pa'i slob ma gang / / yang dag ye shes snang ba po/ /mnar med spang ba'i rgyu yin phyir/ /grub pas bla ma mngon phyag 'tshal/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar
ya rabs kyi spyod tshul bla na med pa ston pa'i phyir/ rtsa ba'i bla ma'i rnam thar/ brgyud pa'i bla ma'i rnam thar gnyis kyi dang po ni/ paN chen rin po che blo bzang
chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi gsang ba'i rnam thar gyi lung brgyud ni/ rgyal dbang zhabs/ pha bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ sprul sku dkon mchog nyi

kha'i rtags can brgyud pa/ rgyal dbang zhabs/ 'jam dbyangs dpal bzang / rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ sprul sku ngag dbang dkon mchog nyi ma/ des bdag go /ga'i rta'i rtags
can brgyud pa/ rgyal dbang zhabs/ rje 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ des bdag go /nga'i rtags can brgyud pa/ rgyal dbang

zhabs/ ngag dbang mkhyen brtse/ rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ sprul sku ngag dbang dkon mchog nyi ma/ des bdag go /cha'i rtags can brgyud pa/ rgyal dbang zhabs/ ngag dbang phrin
las/ rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa man 'dra'o/ ! /yang / gong gi 'phros/ sde pa'i brtan bzhugs dpal ldan sa gsum ma nas bzung / skyam pa ngag dbang chos 'dzin gyi ngor stsal
ba'i tshe chang gi snod dngul gyi par pu'i kha byang bdud rtsi 'khyil snod ma rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rgyal dbang zhabs/ rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa man 'dra'o/ ! /gtor
ma sna tshogs skor la/ brgya rtsa gsum/ klu gtor che chung gnyis/ dkar chab bzhi/ dbu mdzad kyis zhus pa'i bsur bsngo/ bsangs mchod bkra shis 'khyil pa rnams kyi brgyud pa/
rgyal dbang zhabs/ rje 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ des bdag go /gsol mchod skor la/ ja mchod pad raka mdangs 'phrog /ro brgya gda' ba gnyis kyi brgyud pa/ rgyal dbang zhabs/
rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ sprul sku ngag dbang dkon mchog nyi ma/ /des bdag go /dpal ldan dung skyong dbang mo/ (ka)grib btsan bcas pa'i gsol mchod don gnyis lhun grub/
(ka)zhang blon mchod gtor nor bu'i phreng ba/ (ka)zhang blon gtor 'bul bdud rtsi'i bum bzang / (kha)chos skyong spyi'i gtor bsngo/ (ka)chos skyong nyid kyis zhus pa'i
rgyal gsol/ (kha)thang lha'i gsol mchod yid 'phrog rab dkar/ (kha)gnas chung gsol mchod dri med thub bstan/ (kha)dam can skyes bu chen po'i mchod gtor mthu stobs nus pa/
(kha)rdo rje drag rgyal ma'i gtor 'bul/ (kha)gnas chung ba'i gtor 'bul/ (kha)gnod sbyin beg tse lcam dral gyi spyan 'dren/ (kha)rma chen spom ra'i gsol mchod/ (kha)gtsug
na nor bu 'chang ba'i klu'i gsol mchod klu rang gis zhus pa/ (kha)gnas chung par phrin bcol

dam sgrags/ (kha)rta rgod shel lcags kyi mchod sprin/ (kha)khyab 'jug gi las byang tshangs pa'i sgra dbyangs/ (kha)'phyong rgyas lha bka' sdod bcas pa'i gsol mchod grib btsan
pas zhus pa/ (kha)tshangs pa dung thod can gyi gsol mchod/ (ga)rdo rje brag sprul skus zhus pa'i gter srung lhang lha'i gsol mchod/ (kha)(ga)mtsho khri shog rgyal mo'i
yul lha nye 'khor gsol mchod/ (ga)ar ge chos skyong gis zhus pa'i rgyal gsol/ (kha)ri bo chos gling gi bstan ma klu bdud gsol mchod/ (ga)tshong 'dus chos skyong gis zhus
pa'i gsol mchod/ (ga)gdong nas kyis zhus pa'i gur zhal gtor bsngo/ (ga)zhang blon las byang yongs 'du'i 'khri shing / (ga)gsang phu bse khrab pa'i gsol mchod/ (ga)gur zhal
las mgon bcas pa'i bskang ba phun tshogs 'dod rgu'i dpal ster/ (ga)rta thub dkar po bsten pa'i dgra lha'i gsol mchod/ (ga)rgyal gsol gar dbang bde chen ma/ (kha)g.ya'
ma rdo rje spun gsum gnyer pa seng gdong bcas pa'i gsol mchod/ (ga)zha lu mkhan gyis zhus pa'i rgyal gsol/ (ga)lha mo tsaNDi ka dang sham po'i gsol mchod/ (ga)bstan skyong
rdo rje g.yu sgron ma'i gsol mchod/ (ga)chu bo ri'i gsol mchod gtor 'bul rje khra tshang pa'i ngor/ (nga)dga' gdong chos skyong gsol mchod chos skyong nyid kyis zhus pa/
(ga)gter bdag gling pa'i ngor gur zhal gtor chog /(ka)dam can skyes bu thig le rtsal dang / chu rgyud rgyal po'i gsol mchod/ (dznyA)sa skyong blo bzang ngor chos skyong
spyi'i gtor bsngo/ (ga)dmag dpon gangs la nyi shar gyi gsol mchod dmag dpon rang gis zhus pa/ (ga)srung ma bzhi'i gsol mchod/ (ga)ri bo brag btsan gsol mchod/ (ka)thang
sag bran kha dpal yon gsol mchod/ (ka)rdo rje brag sprul sku'i ngor 'dod khams dbang phyug ma'i gsol mchod/ (ka)re ma

ti'i bskang ba bsdus pa/ (ka)las gshin sogs kyi gtor 'bul bkras rnam pas zhus pa/ (ka)btsan rgod kha che dmar po'i gsol mchod/ (ka)dpang gzu legs ldan phyag drug ma/ (ka)dbu
mdzad kyis zhus pa'i gsol mchod ka ca'i rjes 'brang ma/ (dznyA)byang gling rgyal pos zhus pa btsan rgod gangs la nyi shar gsol mchod/ (ka)pho lha dpal 'byor rgyal pos gsol
mchod/ (ka)khra 'brug chos skyong gis zhus pa'i sde brgyad spyi'i gsol mchod rnams la/ ka'i rtags can brgyud pa rgyal dbang zhabs/ rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ sprul sku
dkon mchog nyi zla/ des bdag go /kha'i rtags can/ rgyal dbang zhabs/ 'jam dbyangs dpal bzang / rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa man 'dra'o/ /ga'i rtags can/ rgyal dbang mchog
/rje 'jam dbyangs bstan 'dzin/ des bdag go /(dznyA)khal kha rgyal po la gnang ba zhal gdams mu thi la'i 'khri shing ste/ dznyA'i rtags can rgyal dbang mchog /rtsa ba'i bla
ma mchog gi sprul sku ngag dbang dkon mchog nyi ma/ des phrin las par dgyes pa chen pos bstsal to/ /bkra shis lhun po'i sprul sku rin po che blo bzang ye shes la gnang
ba'i brtan bzhugs/ rgyal dbang thugs rje chen po/ des bka' drin bla na ma mchis pa bskyangs pa'i dus der bdag phrin las rnam rgyal la gnang ba'o// //(pa)! rig gnas skor la/
bzo rig pa la lus bzo thun mong ba 'chams dkyus ma rnga 'gros sogs dang / thun mong ma yin pa rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i gur

rigs bsdus kyi sa'i cho ga'i gar dang bgegs gzhom dang / me tog 'bul ba dang / mchod pa ste de dag gi gar dang / dus 'khor gyi sa gar dang / dkyil 'khor so so'i stangs stabs
dang / lam 'bras sogs kyi lus sbyong 'phrul 'khor sogs dang / phur pa'i rtsa 'chams sogs/ gzor ging bcas pa dang / cha lang / sil snyan gling bu rgyud mang dril dkrol sogs
so/ /ngag bzo gar rnams kyi glu dang / yog dbyangs/ chos skyong gur zhal pu tra sogs kyi bskang mdos kyi dbyangs chen drug cu rtsa gnyis/ phur pa tshes bcu bcas pa'i
dbyangs/ gong bstod kyi gdangs sogs/ mkhas par grags pa rnams kyi drung du nges 'drongs mang du sbyangs shing / de dag gi brgyud pa 'dren srol mi 'dug kyang / rang dgar mi
shes pas brgyud pa bar ma chad pa don gyis thob/ rang lo drug par yi ge gzab bshur/ de nas rim par lanydza wartu/ 'bru ma/ gong dkar yig gsar sogs/ bkra shis chos sder
rig 'dzin sman lung pa'i dngos slob blo gros nor bu la lo chen chos skyong bzang po'i sum rtags 'grel pa nas ri mo zhus/ nyi gling du rtsis phran bu zhus/ de nas mkhas pa'i
spyod yul phyi nang thun mong ba'i rig gnas chen po rnams la tshwa ran bltas pa 'di 'dra yi ger dgod pa'i 'os min rung / gtso bor skye ba phyi ma rnams su slob pa'i rten
'brel dang / sa bcad 'di ma stongs tsam du/ dbu mdzad tshe dbang bsam grub la thub pa'i dbu phyag zhabs gsum gyi thig bcas/ pha ma'i ngag ma bcag tsam du gso ba rig pa'i
rtsa rgyud nas cung zad zin/ nyi gling rin po che'i zhabs drung du sgra mtshams sbyor lnga pa'i ri mo rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i steng nas zhus/ de skabs su sa gzhong la
dung dkar dang sha sha dha ra bris pa'i sa gnyis spral dpral bar byug cing sngags de nyid brjod pa sgra dbang zhes pa thob/ rje bla mas grwa thang gnas chung

pa la gsan no/ /sdeb sbyor rin chen 'byung gnas dang / me tog chun po nas lci yang ngos 'dzin sogs/ me long ma nas snyan ngag gi ltogs lha sod tsam/ dpal ldan 'bras spungs
su kha dog dkar dmar la tshad ma'i snying 'dod bsad do/ /de nas mkhas par grags pa sna tshogs drung du/ rgyud sde so so'i dkyil 'khor bri thig /shraddha ka ra warma'i gzhung
dang / slob dpon rtse mo'i dbang chu chen mo/ dkyil chog so so/ bu ston rin po che'i rdor dbyings thig rtsa rgyas pa sogs nas bshad pa dang lag len mthun pa'i ming thogs
tsam sbyangs/ yid bzo ni spyir de dag thams cad la khyab byed du yod mod/ khyad par thos sbyangs las byung ba'i bsam sgom 'chad rtsod rtsom pa dang / bskyed rdzogs la
nyams len cung zad byas pa ste/ thob yig bum pa bzang po las rig gnas kyi le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// //! bde bar gshegs pa sras dang bcas pa rnams kyis gsungs pa'i chos nyan
pa la phan yon dpag tu med pa yod de/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang ba bstan pa'i mdo las/ dam chos 'dzin pa'i bsod nams ni/ /sangs rgyas kun gyis nan tan du| |bskal pa
bye bar brjod mdzad kyang / /mtha' mar phyin par 'gyur ma lags/ / zhes dang / rnam bshad rig pa las/ dad pas nyan pa gang gis na/ /mtho ris dga' ba'i bsod nams dang / /gang
gis mya ngan 'das thob pa'i/ /shes rab sa bon brtas par 'gyur/ /zhes dang / slob dpon dpa' bos/ thos pa gti mug mun sel sgron ma yin/ /rkun po la sogs mi 'khyer nor gyi
mchog /kun tu rmongs pa'i dgra 'joms mtshon cha yin/ /thabs tshul man ngag ston pa grogs kyi mchog /sogs dang / gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdo las/ 'jig rten sangs
rgyas 'byung ba brgya lam ste/ /

mi yi lus ni tshogs kyis rnyed par dka'/ /kye ma dad pa dang ni chos nyan pa/ /'di 'dra bskal pa brgyar yang rnyed par dka'/ /zhes dang / rgya rol las/ mi dang sangs rgyas
'byung rnyed dka'/ /dad pa'ang shin tu rnyed par dka'/ /mi khom brgyad spangs rnyed par dka'/ /chos nyan pa ni gtso bo yin/ /zhes dang / dkon brtsegs las/ thos par 'dod pas
thos pa 'phel/ /thos pas shes rab 'phel bar 'gyur/ /shes rab kyis ni don rnams sbyong / /don thob nas ni de thob 'gyur/ /zhes so/ /dam pa'i chos kyi don phun sum tshogs
pa ma go yang dam pa'i chos thos pa la phan yon tshad med de/ dge slong chos sred chu srin du gyur pa'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi sgra tsam thos pas mir skyes pa dang / khye'u
chu 'bebs kyis sangs rgyas kyi mtshan bsgrags chos bshad pas nya khri tham pa lhar skyes/ dge 'dun srung gis mdo bton pa/ drang srong lnga brgyas phag nyan byas pas phyir
mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu thob/ gzungs rnams nas gzungs gang dag dud 'gro'i skye gnas pa rnams kyi rna lam du bsgrags pas ngan 'gro las thar ba sogs gsungs so/ / rnam pa
thams cad mkhyen pa rgyal ba nyid kyis kyang / kun dga' bo dang / 'od srung chen po la byang chub kyi yan lag bdun nas brtsams te chos gsan gsungs so/ /des na bdag ni/ gsang
sngags rgyud sde dang mthun/ spyod pa 'dul ba dang mthun/ bshad pa mngon pa dang mthun/ sgom pa mdo sde dang mthun pa/ paN grub rnams kyis bshad/ lo tsA bas bsgyur/ mkhas
pa rnams la yongs su grags pa'i chos rnams/ dper na/ shi bi'i rgyal pos rang gi sha khrag gis mchod nas srin po la chos nyan pa dang / rgyal po legs bshad tshol gyis
chos kyi yon du rang lus ri bo'i rtse nas 'phangs pa dang / shi bi'i rgyal pos lus la mar me stong spar ba dang / rje btsun 'jam dbyangs da dung 'dren

pa rnams las thos pa rgya mtsho bsag sogs/ de bzhin du rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi gsung rab ma lus pa khong du chud par gyur cig gu snyam du sems so/ /'dir le'u dang
rdzogs so bris pa la skyon med de/ so so'i go rim dang bstun te slar chos zhus pa rnams de dang de dag gi skabs su bri rgyu'o/ /! bsngo smon shis brjod ni/ 'dir 'bad ngal
bas thob yig bkod gyur pa| |mkhas mchog rnams kyi dgongs pa rdzogs sam snyam/ /blun rmongs rnams la tshul 'dis ci zhig bya/ /skyes bu 'bring po rnams la phan nam snyam/
/de ltar thos sbyangs las byung dge tshogs rgyu/ /tshad med zhing na grangs med sangs rgyas rnams/ /rgyal ba'i myu gu gsung skyes dang bcas pa/ /chos kyi 'khor lo gang du
bskor ba der/ /sring mo the tshom sel ba'i ting 'dzin ltar/ /de dag re re'i drung na lus dbang re/ /sprul nas dam chos bdud rtsi ji snyed pa/ /thos nas ji bzhin 'dzin pa'i
phyir du bsngo/ ! /lha dbang gtsug rgyan nor bu rin chen 'dra/ /rtsa brgyud bla ma rnams kyi bkra shis shog /dngos grub kun 'byung bum pa bzang po bzhin/ /yi dam lha
tshogs rnams kyi bkra shis shog / kun la phan mdzad nam mkha'i nor bu ltar/ /rgyal sras nyan rang rnams kyi bkra shis shog /'jigs dang bskal pa'i mtsho chen dang mtshungs
pa'i/ /mkha' 'gro chos skyong srung ma'i bkra shis shog /sprin med mkha' la nyi shar ji bzhin du/ /sangs rgyas mkha' dbyings gang ba'i bkra shis shog /chu stod zla ba'i
nam mkha'i snang tshul ltar/ / dam chos char chen 'bebs pa'i bkra shis shog /nor 'dzin rtsi bcud rkang 'thung rgyas pa bzhin/ /dge 'dun sa gzhi gang ba'i bkra shis shog /rab
dga' rgyal po'i pi wang rgyud stong ltar/ /'chad nyan rgyun mi chad pa'i bkra shis shog /'khor lo bsgyur rgyal

byon ltar 'gro ba kun/ /bde skyid phun sum tshogs pa'i bkra shis shog /rgyal ba sras bcas rgyal ba rgya mtsho la/ /myur du 'gran par nus pa'i bkra shis shog /thob yig bum pa
bzang po las bsngo ba smon lam las bkra shis rgyas par brjod pa'i le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o/ /thob yig bum pa bzang po zhes bya ba re zhig rdzogs so// //
